---
layout: post
title: 罗怙世系
tags: raghuvamsa
---

#### <span class="box">1.1</span>

vāg-arthāv-iva saṃpṛktau vāg-artha-pratipattaye, jagataḥ pitarau vande pārvatī-parameśvarau.

> 为了获得言与义，我礼敬结合一如言与义般的世界之父母，Pārvatī 及最胜的自在天。

#### <span class="box">1.2</span>

kva sūryaprabhavo vaṃśaḥ kva cālpaviṣayā matiḥ, titīrṣur-dustaraṃ mohād-uḍupenāsmi sāgaram.

> 何处是太阳族裔的世系？何处又是境域微渺的思想？出于愚痴，我企图凭小舟渡过难渡的大海。

#### <span class="box">1.3</span>

mandaḥ kavi-yaśaḥ-prārthī gamiṣyāmy-upahāsyatām, prāṃśu-labhye phale lobhād-udbāhur-iva vāmanaḥ.

> 愚钝的、渴望诗人荣誉的我将被嘲笑，如同出于贪婪而举起手臂的侏儒之于巨人方及的果实。

#### <span class="box">1.4</span>

athavā kṛta-vāg-dvāre vaṃśe 'smin-pūrva-sūribhiḥ, maṇau vajra-samutkīrṇe sūtrasyevāsti me gatiḥ.

> 或者，我得以步入这由前辈学人们打开的语言之门的世系，如同丝线得以穿过被金刚刺穿的摩尼。

#### <span class="box">1.5</span>

so 'ham-ājanama-śuddhānām-āphalodaya-karmaṇām, āsamudra-kṣitīśānām-ānāka-ratha-vartmanām.

> 他们出生后始终纯洁，劳作直到成果现起，统治的大地直达大海，行车的道路直抵天国，

#### <span class="box">1.6</span>

yathā-vidhi-hutāgnīnāṃ yathā-kāmārcitārthinām, yathāparādha-daṇḍānāṃ yathā-kāla-prabhodhinām.

> 他们按照仪轨祭祀火，如愿礼遇祈求者，按罪施罚，按时醒觉，

#### <span class="box">1.7</span>

tyāgāya saṃbhṛtārthānāṃ satyāya mitabhāṣiṇām, yaśase vijigīṣūṇāṃ prajāyai gṛhamendhinām.

> 他们为了舍弃而积聚财富，为守诺言而慎于言语，为求荣誉而渴望胜利，为了子孙而成立家室，

#### <span class="box">1.8</span>

śaiśave 'bhyasta-vidyānāṃ yauvane viṣayaiṣiṇām, vārddhake muni-vṛttīnāṃ yogenānte tanu-tyajām.

> 他们童年时勤学知识，青年时追逐外境，老年时寂默生活，最后则凭瑜伽舍弃身体，

#### <span class="box">1.9</span>

raghūṇām-anvayaṃ vakṣye tanu-vāg-vibhavo 'pi san, tad-guṇaiḥ karṇam-āgatya cāpalāya pracoditaḥ.

> 听闻了他们的种种品德，受到激励的我不揣冒昧，即便言辞浅薄，也要叙述罗怙家族。

#### <span class="box">1.10</span>

taṃ santaḥ śrotum-arhanti sad-asad-vyakti-hetavaḥ, hemnaḥ saṃlakṣyate hy-agnau viśuddhiḥ śyāmikāpi vā.

> 就让明辨真伪的善人们听听它，因为金子的纯或不纯将在火中显现。

#### <span class="box">1.11</span>

vaivasvato manur-nāma mānanīyo manīṣiṇām, āsīn-mahīkṣitām-ādyaḥ praṇavaś-chandasām-iva.

> 太阳之子名曰摩奴，智者之中备受尊敬，他是最初的大地之主，如同颂诗中的唵。

#### <span class="box">1.12</span>

tad-anvaye śuddhimati prasūtaḥ śuddhimattaraḥ, dilīpa iti rājendur-induḥ kṣīra-nidhāv-iva.

> 在这纯洁的家族中，生出一位更加纯洁的人，王中之月 Dilīpa，仿佛乳海之中生出明月。

#### <span class="box">1.13</span>

vyūḍhorasko vṛṣa-skandhaḥ śāla-prāṃśur-mahābhujaḥ, ātma-karma-kṣamaṃ dehaṃ kṣātro dharma ivāśritaḥ.

> 胸脯宽厚，肩如公牛，高似娑罗，手臂粗壮，犹如刹帝利之法所依止的胜任自身职责的肉身。

#### <span class="box">1.14</span>

sarvātirikta-sāreṇa sarva-tejo'bhibhāvinā, sthitaḥ sarvonnatenorvīṃ krāntvā merur-ivātmanā.

> 威力超过一切，盖过一切光辉，他挺身站立，高于一切，如同须弥山跨越大地。

#### <span class="box">1.15</span>

ākāra-sadṛśa-prajñaḥ prajñayā sadṛśāgamaḥ, āgamaiḥ sadṛśārambha ārambha-sadṛśodayaḥ.

> 他的智慧等同于形体，学问等同于智慧，努力等同于学问，成就等同于努力。

#### <span class="box">1.16</span>

bhīma-kāntair-nṛpa-guṇaiḥ sa babhūvopajīvinām, adhṛṣyaś-cābhigamyaś-ca yādoratnair-ivārṇavaḥ.

> 对于臣民，他拥有既可怕又可爱的王者之德，既不可冒犯，又可以接近，如同大海拥有海妖和珍宝。

#### <span class="box">1.17</span>

rekhā-mātram-api kṣuṇṇād-ā manor-vartmanaḥ param, na vyatīyuḥ prajās-tasya niyantur-nemi-vṛttayaḥ.

> 在他的驾驭下，臣民们运转如车轮，丝毫也不偏离自摩奴开辟的道路。

#### <span class="box">1.18</span>

prajānām-eva bhūty-arthaṃ sa tābyho balim-agrahīt, sahasra-guṇam utsraṣṭum-ādatte hi rasaṃ raviḥ.

> 只是为了臣民的福利，他才问他们收取赋税，因为太阳吸取水分是为了千倍地洒下。

#### <span class="box">1.19</span>

senā paricchadas-tasya dvayam-evārtha-sādhanam, śāstreṣv-akuṇṭhitā buddhir-maurvī dhanuṣi cātatā.

> 他的军队只是装饰，为达目的只用二种：通晓经典的智慧，及弓上张开的弓弦。

#### <span class="box">1.20</span>

tasya saṃvṛta-mantrasya gūḍhākāreṅgitasya ca, phalānumeyāḥ prārambhāḥ saṃskārāḥ prāktanā iva.

> 他保守机密，深藏表情和行动，工作的开始要从结果推断，如同前世的业行。

#### <span class="box">1.21</span>

jugopātmānam atrasto bheje dharmam anāturaḥ, agṛdhnur ādade so 'rtham asaktaḥ sukham anvabhūt.

> 

#### <span class="box">1.22</span>

jñāne maunaṃ kṣamā śaktau tyāge ślāghāviparyayaḥ, guṇā guṇānubandhitvāt tasya saprasavā iva.

> 

#### <span class="box">1.23</span>

anākṛṣṭasya viṣayair vidyānāṃ pāradṛśvanaḥ, tasya dharmarater āsīd vṛddhatvaṃ jarasā vinā.

#### <span class="box">1.24</span>

prajānāṃ vinayādhānād rakṣaṇād bharaṇād api, sa pitā pitaras tāsāṃ kevalaṃ janmahetavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.25</span>

sthityai daṇḍayato daṇḍyān pariṇetuḥ prasūtaye, apy arthakāmau tasyāstāṃ dharma eva manīṣiṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.26</span>

dudhoha gāṃ sa yajñāya sasyāya maghavā divam, saṃpadvinimayenobhau dadhatur bhuvanadvayam.

#### <span class="box">1.27</span>

na kilānuyayus tasya rājāno rakṣitur yaśaḥ, vyāvṛtta yat parasvebhyaḥ śrutau taskaratā sthitā.

#### <span class="box">1.28</span>

dveṣyo 'pi saṃmataḥ śiṣṭas tasyārtasya yathauṣadham, tvājyo duṣṭaḥ priyo 'py āsīd aṅgulīvoragakṣatā.

#### <span class="box">1.29</span>

taṃ vedhā vidadhe nūnaṃ mahābhūtasamādhinā, tathā hi sarve tasyāsan parārthaikaphalā guṇāḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.30</span>

sa velāvapravalayāṃ parikhīkṛtasāgarām, ananyāśāsanām urvīṃ śaśāsaikapurīm iva.

#### <span class="box">1.31</span>

tasya dākṣiṇyaruḍhena nāmnā magadhavaṃśajā, patnī sudakṣiṇety āsīd adhvarasyeva dakṣiṇā.

#### <span class="box">1.32</span>

kalatravantam ātmānam avarodhe mahaty api, tayā mene manasvinyā lakṣmyā ca vasudhādhipaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.33</span>

tasyām ātmānurūpāyām ātmajanmasamutsukaḥ, vilambitaphalaiḥ kālaṃ sa nināya manorathaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.34</span>

saṃtānārthāya vidhaye svabhujād avatāritā, tena dhūr jagato gurvī saciveṣu nicikṣipe.

#### <span class="box">1.34*</span>

gaṅgāṃ bhagīratheneva pūrveṣāṃ pāvanakṣamām, icchatā saṃtatiṃ nyastā tena mantriṣu kosalā.

#### <span class="box">1.35</span>

athābhyarcya vidhātāraṃ prayatau putrakāmyayā, tau daṃpatī vasiṣṭhasya guror jagmatur āśramam.

#### <span class="box">1.36</span>

snigdhagambhīranirghoṣam ekaṃ syandanam āsthitau, prāvṛṣeṇyaṃ payovāhaṃ vidyudairāvatāv iva.

#### <span class="box">1.37</span>

mā bhūd āśramapīḍeti parimeyapuraḥsarau, anubhāvaviśeṣāt tu senāparivṛtāv iva.

#### <span class="box">1.38</span>

sevyamānau sukhasparśaiḥ śālaniryāsagandhibhiḥ, puṣpareṇūtkirair vātair ādhūtavanarājibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.39</span>

mano'bhirāmāḥ śṛṇvantau rathanemisvanonmukhaiḥ, ṣaḍjasaṃvādinīḥ kekā dvidhā bhinnāḥ śikhaṇḍibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.40</span>

paraparākṣisādṛśyam adūrojjhitavartmasu, mṛgadvandveṣu paśyantau syandanābaddhadṛṣṭiṣu.

#### <span class="box">1.41</span>

śreṇībandhād vitanvadbhir astambhāṃ toraṇasrajam, sārasaiḥ kalanirhrādhaiḥ kvacid unnamitānanau.

#### <span class="box">1.42</span>

pavanasyānukūlatvāt prārthanāsiddhiśaṃsinaḥ, rajobhis turagotkīrṇair aspṛṣṭālaveṣṭanau.

#### <span class="box">1.43</span>

sarasīṣv aravindānāṃ vīcivikṣobhaśītalam, āmodam upajighrantau svaniḥśvāsānukāriṇam.

#### <span class="box">1.44</span>

grāmeṣv ātmaviṣṛṭeṣu yūpacihneṣu yajvanām, amoghāḥ pratigṛhṇantāv arghyānupadam āśiṣaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.45</span>

haiyaṃgavīnam ādāya ghoṣavṛddhān upasthitān, nāmadheyāni pṛcchantau vanyānāṃ mārgaśākhinām.

#### <span class="box">1.46</span>

kāpy abhikhyā tayor āsīd vrajatoḥ śuddhaveṣayoḥ, himanirmuktayor yoge citrācandramsor iva.

#### <span class="box">1.47</span>

tat tad bhūmipatiḥ patnyai darśayan priyadarśanaḥ, sāyaṃ saṃyaminas tasya maharṣer mahiṣīsakhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.48</span>

sa duṣprāpayaśāḥ prāpad āśramaṃ śrāntavāhanaḥ, sāyaṃ saṃyaminas tasya maharṣer mahiṣīsakhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.49</span>

vanāntarād upāvṛttaiḥ samitkuśaphalaharaiḥ, pūryamāṇam adṛśyāgnipratyudyātais tapasvibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.50</span>

ākīrṇam ṛṣipatnīnām uṭajadvārarodhibhiḥ, apatyair iva nīvārabhāgadheyocitair mṛgaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.51</span>

sekānte munikanyābhis tatkṣaṇojjhitavṛkṣakam, viśvāsāya vihaṃgānām ālavālāmbupāyinām.

#### <span class="box">1.52</span>

ātapātayasaṃkśiptanīvārāsu niṣādibhiḥ, mṛgair vartitaromantham uṭajāṅganabhūmiṣu.

#### <span class="box">1.53</span>

abhyutthitāgnipiśunair atithīn āśramonmukhān, punānaṃ pavanoddhūtair dhūmair āhutigandhibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.54</span>

atha yantāram ādiṣya dhuryān viśramayeti saḥ, tām avāropayat patnīṃ rathād avatatāra ca.

#### <span class="box">1.55</span>

tasmai sabhyāḥ sabhāryāya goptre guptatamendriyāḥ, arhaṇām arhate cakrur munayo nayacakṣuṣe.

#### <span class="box">1.56</span>

vidheḥ sāyantanasyānte sa dadarśa tapondhim, anvāsitam arundhatyā svāhayeva havirbhujam.

#### <span class="box">1.57</span>

tayor jagṛhatuḥ pādān rājā rājñī ca māgadhī, tau gurur gurupatnī ca prītyā pratinanandatuḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.58</span>

tam ātithyakriyāśāntarathakṣobhapariśramam, papraccha kuśalaṃ rājye rājyāśramamuniṃ muniḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.59</span>

ath' ātharvanidhes tasya vijitāripuraḥ puraḥ, arthyām arthapatir vācam ādade vadatāṃ varaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.60</span>

upapannaṃ nanu śivaṃ saptasv aṅgeṣu yasya me, daivīnāṃ mānuṣīṇāṃ ca pratihartā tvam āpadām.

#### <span class="box">1.61</span>

tava mantrakṛto mantrair dūrāt prāsamitāribhiḥ, pratyādiśyanta iva me dṛṣtalakṣabhidaḥ śarāḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.62</span>

havir āvarjitaṃ hotas tvayā vidhivad agniṣu, vṛṣṭir bhavati sasyānām avagrahaviśoṣiṇām.

#### <span class="box">1.63</span>

puruṣāyuṣajīvinyo nirātaṅkā nirītayaḥ, yan madīyāḥ prajās tasya hetus tvadbrahmavarcasam.

#### <span class="box">1.64</span>

tvayaivaṃ cintyamānasya guruṇā brahmayoninā, sānubandhāḥ kathaṃ na syuḥ saṃpado me nirāpadaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.65</span>

kiṃ tu vadhvāṃ tavaitasyām adṛṣṭasadṛśaprajam, na mām avati sadvīpā ratnasūr api medinī.

#### <span class="box">1.66</span>

nūnaṃ mattaḥ paraṃ vaṃśyāḥ piṇḍavicchedadarśinaḥ, na prakāmabhujaḥ śrāddhe svadhāsaṃgrahatatparāḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.67</span>

matparaṃ durlabham matvā nūnam āvarjitaṃ mayā, payaḥ pūrvaiḥ svaniḥśvāsaiḥ kavoṣṇam upabhujyate.

#### <span class="box">1.68</span>

so 'ham ijyāviśuddhātmā prajālopanimīlitaḥ, prakāśaś cāprakāśas ca lokāloka ivācalaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.69</span>

lokāntarasukhaṃ puṇyaṃ tapodānasamudbhavam, saṃtatiḥ śuddhavaṃśyā hi paratreha ca śarmaṇe.

#### <span class="box">1.70</span>

tayā hīnaṃ vidhātar māṃ kathaṃ paśyan na dūyase, siktaṃ svayam iva snehād vandhyam āśramavṛkṣakam.

#### <span class="box">1.71</span>

asahyapīḍaṃ bhagavann ṛṇam antyam avehi me, aruṃtudam ivālānam anirvāṇasya dantinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.72</span>

tasmān mucye yathā tāta saṃvidhātuṃ tathārhasi, ikṣvākūṇāṃ durāpe 'rthe tvadadhīnā hi siddhayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.73</span>

iti vijñāpito rājñā dhyānastimitalocanaḥ, kṣaṇamātram ṛṣis tasthau suptamīna iva hradaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.74</span>

so 'paśyat praṇidhānena saṃtateḥ stambhakāraṇam, bhāvitātmā bhuvo bhartur athainaṃ pratyabodhayat.

#### <span class="box">1.75</span>

purā śakram upasthāya tavorvīṃ prati yāsyataḥ, āsīt kalpatarucchāyām āśritā surabhiḥ pathi.

#### <span class="box">1.76</span>

dharmalopabhayād rājñīm ṛtusnātām imāṃ smaran, pradakṣiṇakriyārhāyāṃ tasyāṃ tvaṃ sādhu nācaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.77</span>

avajānāsi māṃ yasmād atas te na bhaviṣyati, matprasūtim anārādhya prajeti tvāṃ śaśāpa sā.

#### <span class="box">1.78</span>

sa śāpo na tvayā rājan na ca sārathinā śrutaḥ, nadaty ākāśaṅgāyāḥ srotasy uddāmadiggaje.

#### <span class="box">1.79</span>

īpsitaṃ tadavajñānād viddhi sārgalam ātmanaḥ, pratibadhnāti hi śreyaḥ pūjyapūjāvyatikramaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.80</span>

haviṣe dīrghasattrasya sā cedānīṃ pracetasaḥ, bhujaṃgapihitadvāraṃ pātālam adhitiṣṭhati.

#### <span class="box">1.81</span>

sutāṃ tadīyāṃ surabheḥ kṛtvā pratinidhiṃ śuciḥ, ārādhaya saptnīkaḥ prītā kāmadughā hi sā.

#### <span class="box">1.82</span>

iti vādina evāsya hotur āhutisādhanam, anindyā nandinī nāma dhenur āvavṛte vanāt.

#### <span class="box">1.83</span>

lalāṭodayam ābhugnaṃ pallavasnigdhapāṭalā, bibhratī śvetaromāṅkaṃ saṃdhyeva śaśinaṃ navam.

#### <span class="box">1.84</span>

bhuvaṃ koṣṇena kuṇśodhnī medhyenāvabhṛthād api, pasraveṇābhivarṣantī vatsālokapravartinā.

#### <span class="box">1.85</span>

rajaḥkaṇaiḥ khuroddhūtaiḥ spṛśadbhir gātram antikāt, tīrthābhiṣekajāṃ śuddhim ādadhānā mahīkṣitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.86</span>

tāṃ puṇyadarśanāṃ dṛṣtvā nimittajñas taponidhiḥ, yājyam āśaṃsitāvandhya prārthanaṃ punar abravīt.

#### <span class="box">1.87</span>

adūravartinīṃ siddhiṃ rājan vigaṇayātmanaḥ, upasthiteyaṃ kalyāṇī nāmni kīrtita eva yat.

#### <span class="box">1.88</span>

vanyavṛttir imāṃ śaśvad (?) ātmānugamanena gām, vidyām abhyasaneneva prasādayitum arhasi.

#### <span class="box">1.89</span>

prasthitāyāṃ pratiṣṭhethāḥ sthitāyāṃ sthitim ācareḥ, niṣaṇṇāyāṃ niṣīdāsyāṃ pītāmbhasi piber apaḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.91</span>

vadhūr bhaktimatī cainām arcitām ā tapovanāt, prayatā prātar anvetu piteva dhuri putriṇām.

#### <span class="box">1.90</span>

ity ā prasādād asyās tvaṃ paricaryāparo bhava, avighnam astu te stheyāḥ sāyaṃ pratudvrajed api.

#### <span class="box">1.92</span>

tatheti pratijagrāha prītimān saparigrahaḥ, ādeśaṃ deśakālajñaḥ śiṣyaḥ śāsitur ānataḥ.

#### <span class="box">1.93</span>

atha pradoṣe doṣajñaḥ saṃveśāya viśaṃpatim, sūnuḥ sūnṛtavāk sraṣṭur visasarjodita sriyam.

#### <span class="box">1.94</span>

satyām api tapaḥsiddhau niyamāpekṣayā muniḥ, kalpavit kalpayām āsa vanyām evāsya saṃvidhām.

#### <span class="box">1.95</span>

nirdiṣṭāṃ kulapatinā sa parṇaśālām adhyāsya prayataparigrahadvitīyaḥ, tacchiṣyādhyayananiveditāvasānāṃ saṃviṣṭaḥ kuśaśayane niśāṃ nināya.

#### <span class="box">2.1</span>

atha prajānmām adhipaḥ prabhāte jāyāpratigrāhitagandhamālyām, vanāya pītapratibaddhavatsāṃ yaśodhano dhenum ṛṣer mumoca.

#### <span class="box">2.2</span>

tasyāḥ khuranyāsapavitrapāṃsum apāṃsulānāṃ dhuri kīrtanīyā, mārgaṃ manuṣyeśvaradharmapatnī śruter ivārthaṃ smṛtir anvagacchat.

#### <span class="box">2.3</span>

nivartya rājā dayitāṃ dayālus tāṃ saurabheyīṃ surabhir yaśobhiḥ, payodharībhūtacatuḥsamudrāṃ jugopa gorūpadharām ivorvīm.

#### <span class="box">2.4</span>

vratāya tenānucareṇa dhenor nyaṣedhi śeṣo 'py anuyāyivargaḥ, na cānyatas tasya śarīrarakṣā svavīryaguptā hi manoḥ prasūtiḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.5</span>

āsvādavadbhiḥ kavalais tṛṇānaṃ kaṇḍūyanair daṃśanivārṇaiś ca, avyāhataiḥ svairagataiḥ sa tasyāḥ samrāṭ samārādhantatparo 'bhūt.

#### <span class="box">2.6</span>

sthitaḥ sthitām uccalitaḥ prayātāṃ niṣeduṣīm āsanabandha dhīraḥ, jalābhilāṣī jalam ādadhānāṃ chāveya tāṃ bhūpati anvagacchat.

#### <span class="box">2.7</span>

sa nyastacihnām api rājalakṣmīṃ tejoviśeṣānumitāṃ dadhānaḥ, āsīd anāviṣkṛtadānarājir antarmadāvastha iva dvipendraḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.8</span>

latāpratānodgrathitaiḥ sa kiśair adhijaydhanvā vicacāra dāvam, rakṣāpadeśān munihomadhenor vanyān vineṣyann iva duṣṭasattvān.

#### <span class="box">2.9</span>

viṣṛṣṭapārśvānucarasya tasya pārśvadrumāḥ pāśabhṛtā samasya, udīrayām āsur ivonmadānām ālokaśabdaṃ vayasāṃ virāvaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.10</span>

marutprayuktāś ca marutsakhābhaṃ tam arcyam ārād abhivartamānam, avākiran bālalatāḥ prasūnair ālokaśabdaṃ vayasāṃ virāvaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.11</span>

dhanurbhṛto 'py asya dayārdrabhāvam ākhyātam antaḥkaraṇair viśaṅkaiḥ, vilokayantyo vapur āpur akṣṇāṃ prakāmavistāraphalaṃ hariṇyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.12</span>

sa kīcakair mārutapūrṇarandhraiḥ kūjadbhir āpāditavaṃśkṛtyam, śuśrāva kuñjeṣu yaśaḥ svam uccair udgīyamānaṃ vanadevatābhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.13</span>

ṛktas tuśārair girinirjharāṇām anokahākamptapuṣpagandhī, tam ātapaklāntam anātapatram ācārapūtaṃ pavanaḥ siṣeve.

#### <span class="box">2.14</span>

śaśāma vṛṣṭyāpi vinā davāgnir āsīd viśeṣā phalapuṣpavṛddhiḥ, ūnaṃ na sattveṣv adhiko babādhe tasmin vanaṃ gopatri gāhamāne.

#### <span class="box">2.15</span>

saṃcārapūtāni digantarāṇi kṛtvā dinānte nilayāya gantum, pracakrame pallavarāgatāmrā tasmin vanaṃ gopatri gāhamāne.

#### <span class="box">2.16</span>

tāṃ devatāpitratithikriyārthām anvag yayau madhyamalokapālaḥ, babhau ca sā tena satāṃ matena śraddheva sākṣād vidhinopapannā.

#### <span class="box">2.17</span>

sa palvalottīrṇavarāhayūthāny āvāsavṛkṣonmukhabarhiṇāni, yayau mṛgādhyāsitaśādvalāni śyāmāyamānāni vanāni paśyan.

#### <span class="box">2.18</span>

āpīnabhārodvahanaprayatnād gṛṣṭir gurutvād vapuṣo narendraḥ, ubhāv alaṃcakratur añcitābhyāṃ tapovanāvṛttipathaṃ gatābhyām.

#### <span class="box">2.19</span>

vasiṣṭhadhenor anuyāninaṃ tam āvartamānaṃ vanitā vanāntāt, papau nimeṣālasapakṣmapaṅktir upoṣitābhyām iva locanābhyām.

#### <span class="box">2.20</span>

puraskṛtā vartmani pārthivena pratyudgatā pārthivadharmpatnyā, tadantare sā virarāja dhenur dinakṣapāmadhyagateva saṃdhyā.

#### <span class="box">2.21</span>

pradakṣiṇīkṛtya payasvinīṃ tāṃ sudakṣiṇā sākṣatapātrahastā, praṇamya cānarca viśālam asyāḥ śṛṅgāntaraṃ dvāram ivārthasiddheḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.22</span>

vatsotsukāpi stimitā saparyāṃ pratyagrahīt seti nanandatus tau, bhaktyopapanneṣu hi tavidhānāṃ prasādacihnāni puraḥphalāni.

#### <span class="box">2.23</span>

guroḥ sadārasya nipīḍya pādau samāpya sāṃdhyaṃ ca vidhiṃ dilīpaḥ, dohāvasāne punar eva dogdhrīṃ bheje bhujocchinnaripur niṣaṇṇām.

#### <span class="box">2.24</span>

tām antikanyastabalipradīpām anvāsya goptā gṛhiṇīsahāyaḥ, krameṇa suptām anu saṃviveśa suptotthitāṃ prātar an'(?)ūdatiṣṭhat.

#### <span class="box">2.25</span>

itthaṃ vrataṃ dhārayataḥ prajārthaṃ samaṃ mahiṣyā mahanīyakīrteḥ, sapta vyatīyus triguṇāni tasya dināni dīnoddharaṇocitasya.

#### <span class="box">2.26</span>

anyedyur ātmānucarasya bhāvaṃ jijñāsamānā munihomadhenuḥ, gaṅgāprapātāntavirūḍhaśaṣpaṃ gaurīguror gahvaram āviveṣa.

#### <span class="box">2.27</span>

ity adriṣobhāprahitekṣaṇena ity adriṣobhāprahitekṣaṇena, alakṣitābhyutpatano nṛpeṇa prasahya siṃhaḥ kila tāṃ cakarṣa.

#### <span class="box">2.28</span>

tadīyam ākranditam ārtasādhor guhānibaddhapratiśabdadīrgham, raśmiṣv ivādāya nagendrasaktāṃ nivartayām āsa nṛpasya dṛṣṭim.

#### <span class="box">2.29</span>

sa pāṭalāyāṃ gavi tasthivāṃsaṃ dhanurdharaḥ kesariṇaṃ dadarśa, adhityakāyām iva dhātumayyāṃ lodhradrumaṃ sānumataḥ praphullam.

#### <span class="box">2.30</span>

tato mṛgendrasya mṛgendragāmī vadhāya vadhyasya śaraṃ śaraṇyaḥ, jātābhiṣaṅgo nṛpatir niṣaṅgād uddhartum aicchat prasabhoddhṛtāriḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.31</span>

vāmetaras tasya karaḥ prahartur nakhaprabhābhūṣitakaṅkapattre, saktāṅguliḥ sāyakapuṅkha eva citrārpitārambha invāvatasthe.

#### <span class="box">2.32</span>

bāhupratiṣṭambhavivṛddhamanyur abhyarṇam āgaskṛtam aspṛśadbhiḥ, rājā svatejobhir adahyatāntar bhogīva mantrauṣadhiruddhavīryaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.33</span>

tam āryagṛhyaṃ nigṛhītadhenur manuṣyavācā manuvaṃśaketum, vismāyayan vismitam ātmavṛttau siṃhorusattvaṃ nijagāda siṃhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.34</span>

alaṃ mahīpāla tava śrameṇa prayuktam apy astram ito vṛthā syāt, na pādaponmūlanaśakti raṃhaḥ śiloccaye mūrchati mārutasya.

#### <span class="box">2.35</span>

kailāsagauraṃ vṛam ārurukṣoḥ pādārpaṇānugrahapūtapṛṣṭam, avehi māṃ kiṃkaram aṣṭamūrteḥ kumbhodaraṃ nāma nikumbhamitram.

#### <span class="box">2.36</span>

amuṃ puraḥ paśyasi devadāruṃ putrīkṛto 'sau vṛṣabhadhvajena, yo hemakumbhastananiḥsṛtānāṃ skandasya mātuḥ payasāṃ rasajñaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.37</span>

kaṇḍūyamānena kaṭaṃ kadācid vanyadvipenonmathitā tvag asya, athainam adres tanayā śuśoca senānyam ālīḍham ivāsurāstraiḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.38</span>

tadā prabhṛty eva vanadvipānāṃ trāsārtham asminn aham adikukṣau, vyāpāritaḥ śūlabhṛtā vidhāya siṃhatvam aṅkāgatasattvavṛtti.

#### <span class="box">2.39</span>

tasyālam eṣā kṣudhitasya tṛptyai pradiṣṭakālā parameśvareṇa, upasthitā śoṇitapāraṇā me suradviṣaś cāndramasī sudheva.

#### <span class="box">2.40</span>

sa tvaṃ nivartasva vihāya lajjāṃ guror bhavān darśitaśiṣyabhaktiḥ, śastreṇa rakṣyaṃ yad aśakyarakṣaṃ na tad yaśaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ kṣiṇoti.

#### <span class="box">2.41</span>

iti pragalbhaṃ purusādhirājo mṛgādhirājasya vaco niśamya, pratyāhatāstro giriśaprabhāvād ātmany avajñāṃ śithilīcakāra.

#### <span class="box">2.42</span>

pratyabravīc cainam iṣuprayoge tatpūrvasaṅge vitathaprayatnaḥ, jaḍīkṛtas tryambakavikṣaṇena vajraṃ mumukṣann iva vajrapāṇiḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.42*</span>

pratyāha vainaṃ śaramokṣavandhyo mā pattraparvāt svarabhedam āptaḥ, prahīṇapūrvadhvaninādhirūḍhas tulām asārena śaradghanena.

#### <span class="box">2.43</span>

saṃruddhaceṣṭasya hetuḥ hāsyaṃ vacas tad yad ahaṃ vivakṣuḥ, antargataṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ hi veda sarvaṃ bhavān bhāvam ato 'bhidhāsye.

#### <span class="box">2.44</span>

mānyaḥ sa me sthāvarajaṅgamānāṃ sargasthitipratyavahārahetuḥ, guror apīdaṃ dhanam āhitāgner naśyat purastād anupekṣaṇīyam.

#### <span class="box">2.45</span>

sa tvaṃ madīyena śarīravṛttiṃ dehena nirvartayituṃ prasīda, dināvasānotsukabālavatsā visṛjyatāṃ dhenur iyaṃ maharṣeḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.46</span>

athāndhakāraṃ girigahvarāṇāṃ daṃṣṭrāmayūkhaiḥ śakalāni kurvan, bhūyaḥ sa bhūteśvarapārśvavartī kiṃcid vihasyārthapatiṃ babhāṣe.

#### <span class="box">2.47</span>

ekātapatraṃ jagataḥ prabhutvaṃ navaṃ yayaḥ kāntam idaṃ vapuś ca, alpasya hetor bahu hātum icchan vicāramūdhaḥ pratibhāsi me tvam.

#### <span class="box">2.48</span>

bhūtānukampā tava ced iyaṃ gaur ekā bhavet svastimatī tvadante, jīvan punaḥ śaśvad upaplavebhyaḥ prajāḥ prajānātha piteva pāsi.

#### <span class="box">2.49</span>

athaikadhenor aparādhacaṇḍād guroḥ kṛṣānupratimād bibheṣi, śakyo 'sya manyur bhavatā vinetuṃ gāḥ koṭiśaḥ sparśayatā ghaṭodhnīḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.50</span>

tad rakṣa kalyāṇaparaṃparāṇāṃ bhoktāram ūrjasvalam ātmadeham, mahītalasparśanamātrabhinnam ṛddhaṃ hi rājyaṃ padam aindram āhuḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.51</span>

etāvad uktvā virate mṛgendre pratisvanenāsya guhāgatena, śiloccayo 'pi kṣitipālam uccaiḥ prītyā tam evārtham abhāṣateva.

#### <span class="box">2.52</span>

niśamya devānucarasya vācaṃ manuṣyadevaḥ punar apy uvāca, dhenvā tadadhyāsitakātarākṣyā nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ sutarāṃ dayāluḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.53</span>

kṣatāt kila trāyata ity udagraḥ kṣatrasya śabdo bhuvaneṣu rūḍhaḥ, rājyena kiṃ tadviparītavṛtteḥ prāṇair upakrośamalīmasair vā.

#### <span class="box">2.54</span>

kathaṃ nu śakyo 'nunayo maharṣer viśrāṇanāc cānyapayasvinīnām, imām anūnāṃ surabher avehi rudraujasā tu pahṛtaṃ tvayāsyām.

#### <span class="box">2.55</span>

seyaṃ svadehārpaṇaniṣkrayeṇa nyāyyā mayā mocayituṃ bhavattaḥ, na pāraṇā syād vihatā tavaivaṃ bhaved aluptaś ca muneḥ kriyārthaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.56</span>

bhavān apīdaṃ paravān avaiti mahān hi yatnas tava devadārau, sthātuṃ niyoktur na hi śakyam agre vināśya rakṣyaṃ svayam akṣatena.

#### <span class="box">2.57</span>

kim apy ahiṃsyas tava cen mato 'haṃ yaśaḥśarīre bhava me dayāluḥ, ekāntavidhaṃsiṣu madvidhānāṃ piṇḍeṣv anāsthā khalu bhautikeṣu.

#### <span class="box">2.58</span>

saṃbandham ābhāṣaṇapūrvam āhur vṛttaḥ sa nau saṃgatayor vanānte, tad bhūtanāthānuga nārhasi tvaṃ saṃbandhino me praṇayaṃ vihantum.

#### <span class="box">2.59</span>

tatheti gām uktavate dilīpaḥ sadyaḥ pratiṣṭambhavimuktabāhuḥ, sa nyasta śastro haraye svadeham upānayat piṇḍam ivāmiṣasya.

#### <span class="box">2.60</span>

tasmin kṣaṇe pālayituḥ prajānām utpaśyataḥ siṃhanipātam ugram, avāṅmukhasy'opari puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta vidyādharahastamuktā.

#### <span class="box">2.61</span>

uttiṣṭha vatsety amṛtāyamānaṃ vaco niśamyotthitam utthitaḥ san, dadarśa rājā jananīm iva svāṃ gām agrataḥ prasraviṇīṃ na siṃham.

#### <span class="box">2.62</span>

taṃ vismitaṃ dhenur uvāca sādho māyāṃ mayodhbhāvya parīkṣito 'si, ṛṣiprabhāvān mayi nāntako 'pi prabhuḥ prahartuṃ kim utānyahiṃsrāḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.63</span>

bhaktyā gurau mayy anukampāya ca prītāsmi te putra varaṃ vṛṇīṣva, na kevalānāṃ payasāṃ prasūtim avehi māṃ kāmadughāṃ prasannām.

#### <span class="box">2.64</span>

tataḥ samānīya samānitārthī hastau svahastārjitavīraśabdaḥ, vaṃśasya kartāram anantakīrtiṃ sudakṣiṇāyāṃ tanayaṃ yayāce.

#### <span class="box">2.65</span>

saṃtānakāmāya tatheti kāmaṃ rājñe pratiśrutya payasvinī sā, dugdhvā payaḥ pattrapuṭe madīyaṃ putr' opabhuṅkṣv' eti tam ādideśa.

#### <span class="box">2.66</span>

vatsasya homārthavidheś ca śeṣam ṛṣer anujñām adhigamya mātaḥ, ūdhasyam icchāmi tavopabhoktumyaṃ ṣaṣṭhāmśam urvyā iva rakṣitāyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.67</span>

itthaṃ kṣitīśena vasiṣṭhadhenur vijñāpitā prītatarā babhūva, tadanvitā haimavatāc ca kukṣeḥ pratyāyayāv āśramam aśrameṇa.

#### <span class="box">2.68</span>

tasyāḥ prasannendumukhaḥ prasādaṃ gurur nṛpāṇāṃ gurave nivedya, praharṣacihnānumitaṃ priyāyai śaśaṃsa vācā punaruktayeva.

#### <span class="box">2.69</span>

sa nandinīstanyam aninditātmā sadvatsalo vatsahutāvaśeṣam, papau vasiṣṭhena kṛtābhyanujñaḥ śubhraṃ yaśo mūrtam ivātitṛṣṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.70</span>

prātar yathoktavratapāraṇānte prāsthānikaṃ svastyayanaṃ prayuja, tau daṃpatī svāṃ prati rājadhānīṃ prasthāpayām āsa vaśī vasiṣṭhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.71</span>

pradakṣiṇīkṛtya hutaṃ hutāśam anantaraṃ bhartur arundhatīṃ ca, dhenuṃ savatsāṃ ca nṛpaḥ pratasthe sanmaṅgalodagrataraprabhāvaḥ.

#### <span class="box">2.72</span>

śrotābhirāmadhvaninā rathena sa dharmapatnīsahitaḥ sahiṣṇuḥ, yayāv anudghātasukhena mārgaṃ sveneva pūrṇena manorathena.

#### <span class="box">2.73</span>

tam āhitautsukyam adarśanena prajāḥ prajārthavratakarśitāṅgam, netraiḥ papus tṛptim anāpnuvadbhir navodayaṃ nātham ivauṣadhīnām.

#### <span class="box">2.74</span>

puraṃdaraśrīḥ puram utpatākaṃ praviśya paurair abhinandyamānaḥ, bhuje bhuaṃgendrasamānasāre bhūyaḥ sa bhūmer dhuram āsasañja.

#### <span class="box">2.75</span>

atha nayanasamutthaṃ jyotir atrer iva dyauḥ surasarid iva tejo vahniniṣṭhyūtam aiśam, narapatikulabhūtyai garbham ādhatta rājñī gurubhir abhiniviṣṭaṃ lokapālānubhāvaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.1</span>

athepsitaṃ bhartur upasthitodayaṃ sakhījanodvīkṣaṇakaumudīmukham, nidānam ikṣvākukulasya saṃtateḥ sudakṣiṇā daurhṛdalakṣaṇaṃ dadhau.

#### <span class="box">3.2</span>

śarīrasādād asamagrabhūṣaṇā mukhena sālakṣyata lodhrapāṇḍunā, tanuprakāśena viceyatārakā prabhātakalpā śaśineva śarvarī.

#### <span class="box">3.2A</span>

tato viśāṃpatyur ananyasaṃtater manorathaṃ kiṃcid ivodayonmukham, ananyasauhārdarasasya dohadaṃ priyā prapede prakṛtipriyaṃvadā.

#### <span class="box">3.2B</span>

mukhena sā ketakapattrapāṇḍunā kṛśāṅgayaṣṭiḥ parimeyabhūṣaṇā, sthitālpatārāṃ karuṇendumaṇḍalāṃ vibhātakalpāṃ rajanīṃ vyaḍambayat.

#### <span class="box">3.3</span>

tadānanaṃ mṛtsurabhi kṣitīśvaro rahasy upāghrāya na tṛptim āyayau, karīva siktaṃ pṛṣataiḥ payomucāṃ śucivyapāye vanarājipalvalam.

#### <span class="box">3.4</span>

divaṃ marutvān iva bhokṣyate bhuvaṃ digantaviśrāntaratho hi tat sutaḥ, ato 'bhilāṣe prathamaṃ tathāvidhe mano babandhānyarasān vilaṅghya sā.

#### <span class="box">3.5</span>

na me hriyā śaṃsati kiṃcid īpsitaṃ spṛhāvatī vastuṣu keṣu māgadhī, na hīṣṭam asya tridive 'pi bhūpater priyāsakhīr uttarakosaleśvaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.6</span>

upetya sā dohadaduḥkhaśīlatāṃ yad eva vavre tad apaśyad āhṛtam, na hīṣṭam asya tridive 'pi bhūpater abhūd anāsādyam adhijyadhanvanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.7</span>

krameṇa nistīrya ca dohadavyathāṃ pracīyamānāvayavā rarāja sā, purāṇapattrāpagamād anantaraṃ lateva saṃnaddhamanojñapallavā.

#### <span class="box">3.8</span>

dineṣu gacchatsu nitāntapīvaraṃ tadīyam ānīlamukhaṃ stanadvayam, tiraścakāra bhramarābhilīnayoḥ sujātayoḥ paṅkajakośayoḥ śriyam).

#### <span class="box">3.9</span>

nidhānagarbhām iva sāgarāmbarāṃ śamīm ivābhyantaralīnapāvakām, nadīm ivāntaḥsalilāṃ sarasvatīṃ nṛpaḥ sasattvāṃ mahiṣīm amanyata.

#### <span class="box">3.10</span>

priyānurāgasya manaḥsamunnater bhujārjitānāṃ ca digantasaṃpadām, yathākramaṃ puṃsavanādikāḥ kriyā dhṛteś ca dhīraḥ sadṛśīr vyadhatta saḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.11</span>

surendramātrāśritagarbhagauravāt prayatnamuktāsanayā gṛhāgataḥ, tayopacārāñjalikhinnahastayā nananda pāriplavanetrayā nṛpaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.12</span>

kumārabhṛtyākuśalair anuṣṭhite bhiṣagbhir āptair atha garbhabharmaṇi, patiḥ pratītaḥ prasavonmukhīm priyāṃ dadarśa kāle divam abhrītam iva.

#### <span class="box">3.13</span>

grahais tataḥ pañcabhir uccasaṃśrayair asūryagaiḥ sūcitabhāgyasaṃpadam, asūta putraṃ samaye śacīsamā trisādhanā śaktir ivārtham akṣayam.

#### <span class="box">3.14</span>

diśaḥ prasedur maruto vavuḥ sukhāḥ pradakṣiṇārcir havir agnir ādade, babhūva sarvaṃ śubhaśaṃsi tatkṣaṇaṃ bhavo hi lokābhyudayāya tādṛśām.

#### <span class="box">3.15</span>

ariṣṭaśayyāṃ parito visāriṇā sujanmanas tasya nijena tejasā, niśīthadīpāḥ sahasā hatatviṣo babhūvur ālekhyasamarpitā iva.

#### <span class="box">3.16</span>

janāya śuddhāntacarāya śaṃsate kumārajanmāmṛtasaṃmitākṣaram, adeyam āsīt trayam eva bhūpateḥ śaśiprabhaṃ chattram ubhe ca cāmare.

#### <span class="box">3.16*</span>

samīkṣya putrasya cirān mukhaṃ pitā nidhānakumbhasya yuveva durgataḥ, mudā śarīre prababhūva nātmanaḥ payodhir indūdayamūrchito yathā.

#### <span class="box">3.17</span>

nivātapadmastimitena cakṣuṣā nṛpasya kāntaṃ pibataḥ sutānanam, mahodadheḥ pūra ivendudarśanād guruḥ praharṣaḥ prababhūva nātmani.

#### <span class="box">3.18</span>

sa jātakarmaṇy akhile tapasvinā tapovanād etya purodhasā kṛte, dilīpasūnur maṇir ākarodbhavaḥ prayuktasaṃskāra ivādhikaṃ babhau.

#### <span class="box">3.19</span>

sukhaśravā maṅgalatūryanisvanāḥ pramodanṛtyaiḥ saha vārayoṣitām, na kevalaṃ sadmani māgadhīpateḥ pathi vyajṛmbhanta divaukasām api.

#### <span class="box">3.20</span>

na saṃyatas tasya babhūva rakṣitur visarjayed yaṃ sutajanmaharṣitaḥ, ṛṇābhidhānāt svayam eva kevalaṃ tadā pitḥṇāṃ mumuce sa bandhanāt.

#### <span class="box">3.21</span>

śutasya yāyād ayam antam arbhakas tathā pareṣāṃ yudhi ceti pārthivaḥ, avekṣya dhātor gamanārtham arthavic cakāra nāmnā raghum ātmasaṃbhavam.

#### <span class="box">3.22</span>

pituḥ prayatnāt sa samagrasaṃpadaḥ śubhaiḥ śarīrāvayavair dine dine, pupoṣa vṛddhiṃ haridaśvadīdhiter anupraveśād iva bālacandramāḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.23</span>

umāvṛṣāṅkau śarajanmanā yathā yathā jayantena śacīpuraṃdarau, tathā nṛpaḥ sā cu sutena māgadhī nanandatus tatsadṛśena tatsamau.

#### <span class="box">3.24</span>

rathāṅganāmnor iva bhāvabandhanaṃ babhūva yat prema parasparāśrayam, vibhaktam apy ekasutena tat tayoḥ parasparasyopari paryacīyata.

#### <span class="box">3.25</span>

uvāca dhātryā prathamoditaṃ vaco yayau tadīyām avalambya cāṅgulim, abhūc ca namraḥ praṇipātaśikṣayā pitur mudaṃ tena tatāna so 'rbhakaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.26</span>

tam aṅkam āropya śarīrayogajaiḥ sukhair niṣiñcantam ivāmṛtaṃ tvaci, upāntasaṃmīlitalocano nṛpaś cirāt sutasparśarasjñatāṃ yayau.

#### <span class="box">3.27</span>

tam aṅkam āropya śarīrayogajaiḥ sthiter abhettā sthitimantam anvayam, svamūrtibhedena guṇāgryavartinā patiḥ prajānām iva sargam ātmanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.28</span>

sa vṛttacaulaś calakākapakṣakair amātyaputraiḥ savayobhir anvitaḥ, liper yathāvadgrahaṇena vāṅmayaṃ nadīmukheneva samudram āviśat.

#### <span class="box">3.29</span>

athopanītaṃ vidhivad vipaścito vininyur enaṃ guravo gurupriyam, avandhyayatnāś ca babhūvur arbhake tatāra vidyāḥ pavanātipātibhir.

#### <span class="box">3.30</span>

dhiyaḥ samagraiḥ sa guṇair udāradhīḥ kramāc catasraś caturarṇavopamāḥ, tatāra vidyāḥ pavanātipātibhir diśo haridbhir haritām iveśvaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.31</span>

tvacaṃ sa medhyāṃ paridhāya rauravīm aśikṣatāstraṃ pitur eva mantravat, na kevalaṃ tadgurur ekapārthivaḥ kṣitāv abhūd ekadhanurdharo 'pi saḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.32</span>

mahokṣatāṃ vatsataraḥ spṛśann iva dvipendrabhāvaṃ kalabhaḥ śrayann iva, raghuḥ kramād yauvanabhinnaśaiśavaḥ pupoṣa gāmbhīryamanoharaṃ vapuḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.33</span>

athāsya godānavidher anantaraṃ vivāhadīkṣāṃ niravartayad guruḥ, narendrakanyās tam avāpya satpatiṃ tamonudaṃ dakṣasutā ivābabhuḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.34</span>

yuvā yugavyāyatabāhur aṃsalaḥ kapāṭavakṣāḥ pariṇaddhakaṃdharaḥ, vapuḥprakarṣād ajayad guruṃ raghus tathāpi nīcair vinayād adṛśyata.

#### <span class="box">3.35</span>

tataḥ prajānāṃ ciram ātmanā dhṛtāṃ nitāntagurvīṃ laghayiṣyatā dhuram, nisargasaṃskāravinīta ity asau nṛpeṇa cakre yuvarājaśabdabhāk.

#### <span class="box">3.36</span>

narendramūlāyatanād anantaraṃ ghanavyapāyena gabhastimān iva, agacchad aṃśena guṇābhilāṣiṇī navāvatāraṃ kamalād ivotpalam.

#### <span class="box">3.37</span>

vibhāvasuḥ sārathineva vāyunā ghanavyapāyena gabhastimān iva, babhūva tenātitarāṃ suduḥsahaḥ kaṭaprabhedena karīva pārthivaḥ.
#### <span class="box">3.38</span>

niyujya taṃ homaturaṃgarakṣaṇe dhanurdharaṃ rājasutair anudrutam, apūrṇam ekena śatakratūpamaḥ śataṃ kratūnā apavighnam āpa saḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.39</span>

tataḥ paraṃ tena makhāya vajvanā turaṃgam utsṛṣṭam anargalaṃ punaḥ, dhanurbhṛtām agrata eva rakṣiṇāṃ jahāra śakraḥ kila gūḍhavigrahaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.40</span>

viṣādaluptapratipatti vismitaṃ mamaiva yeneha turaṃgam īkṣase, dhenvā niśamyeti vacaḥ samīrtaṃ śrutaprabhāvā dadṛśe 'tha nandinī.

#### <span class="box">3.40*</span>

svedāmbunā mārjaya putra locane mamaiva yeneha turaṃgam īkṣase, dhenvā niśamyeti vacaḥ samīritaṃ mudaṃ parām āpa dilīpanandanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.41</span>

tadaṅganisyandajalena locane pramṛjya puṇyena puraskṛtaḥ satām, atīndriyeṣv apy upapannadarśano babhūva bhāveṣu dilīpanandanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.42</span>

sa pūrvataḥ parvatapakṣaśātanaṃ dadarśa devaṃ naradevasaṃbhavaḥ, punaḥ punaḥ sūtaniṣiddhacāpalaṃ harantam aśvaṃ ratharaśmisaṃyatam.

#### <span class="box">3.43</span>

sa pūrvataḥ parvatapakṣaśātanaṃ hariṃ viditvā haribhiś ca vājibhiḥ, avocad enaṃ gangaspṛśā raghuḥ svareṇa dhīreṇa nivartayann iva.

#### <span class="box">3.44</span>

makhāṃśabhājāṃ prathamo manīṣibhis tvam eva devendra sadā nigadyase, ajasradīkṣāprayatasya madguroḥ kriyāvighātāya kathaṃ pravartase.

#### <span class="box">3.45</span>

trilokanāthena sadā makhadviṣas tvayā niyamyā nanu divyacakṣuṣā, sa cet svayaṃ karamasu dharmacāriṇāṃ tvam antarāyo bhavasi cyuto vidhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.46</span>

tad aṅgam agryaṃ maghavan mahākrator amuṃ turaṃgaṃ pratimoktum arhasi, pataḥśruter darśayitāra īśvarā malīmasām ādadate na paddhatim.

#### <span class="box">3.47</span>

iti pragalbhaṃ raghuṇā samīritaṃ vaco niśamyādhipatir divaukasām, nivartayām āsa rathaṃ savismayaḥ pracakrame ca prativaktum uttaram.

#### <span class="box">3.48</span>

yad āttha rājanyakumāra tat tathā yaśas tu rakṣyaṃ parato yaśodhanaiḥ, jagatprakāśaṃ tad aśeṣam ijyayā bhavadgurur laṅghayituṃ mamodyataḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.49</span>

harir yathaikaḥ puruśottamaḥ smṛto maheśvaras tryambaka eva nāparaḥ, tathā vidur māṃ munayaḥ śatakratuṃ dvitīyagāmī na hi śabda eṣa naḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.50</span>

ato 'yam aśvaḥ kapilānukāriṇā pitus tvadīyasya mayāpahāritaḥ, alaṃ prayatnena tavātra mā nidhāḥ padaṃ padavyāṃ sagarasya saṃtateḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.51</span>

tataḥ prahasyāpabhayaḥ puraṃdaraṃ punar babhāṣe turagasya rakṣitā, gṛhāṇa śastraṃ yadi sarga eṣa te na khalv anirjitya raghuṃ kṛtī bhavān.

#### <span class="box">3.52</span>

sa evam uktvā maghavantam unmukhaḥ kariṣyamāṇaḥ saśaram śarāsanam, atiṣṭhad ālīḍhaviśeṣaśobhinā vapuḥprakarṣeṇa viḍambiteśvaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.53</span>

raghor avaṣṭambhamayena pattriṇā hṛdi kṣato gotrabhid apy amarṣaṇaḥ, navāmbudānīkamuhūrtalāñchane dhanuṣy amoghaṃ samadhatta sāyakam.

#### <span class="box">3.54</span>

dilīpasūnoḥ sa bṛhad (?) bhujāntaraṃ praviśya bhīmāsuraśoṇitocitaḥ, papāv anāsvāditapūrvam āśugaḥ kutūhaleneva manuṣyaśoṇitam.

#### <span class="box">3.55</span>

hareḥ kumāro 'pi kumāravikramaḥ suradvipāsphālanakarkaśāṅgulau, bhuje śacīpattraviśeṣakāṅkite svanāmacihnaṃ nicakhāna sāyakam.

#### <span class="box">3.56</span>

jahāra cānyena mayūrapattriṇā śareṇa śakrasya mahāśanidhvajam, cukopa tasmai sa bhṛśaṃ suraśriyaḥ prasahaya keśavyaparopaṇād iva.

#### <span class="box">3.57</span>

tayor upāntasthitasiddhasainikaṃ garutmadāśīviśabhīmadarśanaiḥ, babhūva yuddhaṃ tumuulaṃ jayaiṣiṇor adhomukhair ūrdhvamukhaiś ca pattribhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.58</span>

atiprabandhaprahitāstravṛṣṭibhis tam āśrayaṃ duṣprahasya tejasaḥ, śaśāka nirvāpayituṃ na vāsavaḥ svataś cyutaṃ vahnim ivādbhir ambudaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.59</span>

tataḥ prakoṣṭhe haricandanāṅkite pramathyamānārṇavadhīra, raghuḥ śaśāṅkārdhamukhena pattriṇā śarāsanajyām alunād viḍaujasaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.60</span>

sa cāpam utsṛjya vivṛddhamatsaraḥ praṇāśanāya prabalasya vidviṣaḥ, mahīdhrapakṣavyaparopaṇocitaṃ sphuratprabhāmaṇḍalam astram ādade.

#### <span class="box">3.61</span>

raghur bhṛśaṃ vakṣasi tena tāḍitaḥ papāta bhūmau saha sainikāśrubhiḥ, nimeṣamātrād avadhūya tad vyathāṃ sahotthitaḥ sainikaharṣanisvanaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.62</span>

tathāpi śastravyavahāraniṣṭhure bipakṣabhāve ciram asya tasthuṣaḥ, tutoṣa vīryātiśayena vṛtrahā padaṃ hi sarvatra guṇair nidhīyate.

#### <span class="box">3.63</span>

asaṅgam adriṣv api sāravattayā na me tvadanyena visoḍham āyudham, avehi māṃ prītam ṛte turaṃgamāt kim icchasīti sphuṭam āha vāsavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">3.64</span>

tato niṣaṅgād asamagram uddhṛtaṃ suvarṇapuṅkhadyutirañjitāṅgulim, narendrasūnuḥ pratisaṃharann iṣuṃ priyaṃvadaḥ pratyavadat sureśvaram.

#### <span class="box">3.65</span>

amocyam aśvaṃ yadi manyase prabho tataḥ samāpte vidhinaiva karmaṇi, ajasradīkṣāprayataḥ sa madguruḥ krator aśeṣeṇa phalena yujyatām.

#### <span class="box">3.66</span>

yathā ca vṛttāntam imaṃ sadogatas trilocanaikāṃśatayā durāsadaḥ, tavaiva saṃdeṣaharād viśaṃpatiḥ śṛṇoti lokeśa tathā vidhīyatām.

#### <span class="box">3.67</span>

tatheti kāmaṃ pratiśuśruvān raghor yathāgataṃ mātalisārathir yayau, nṛpasya nātipramanāḥ sadogṛhaṃ sudakṣināsūnur api nyavartata.

#### <span class="box">3.68</span>

tam abhyanandat prathamaṃ prabodhitaḥ prajeśvaraḥ śāsanahāriṇā hareḥ, parāmṛśan harṣajaḍena pāṇinā tadīyam aṅgaṃ kuliśavraṇāṅkitam.

#### <span class="box">3.69</span>

iti kṣitīśo navatiṃ navādhikāṃ mahākratūnāṃ mahanīyaśāsanaḥ, samāraurukṣur divam āyuṣaḥ kṣaye tatāna sopānaparaṃparām iva.

#### <span class="box">3.70</span>

atha sa viṣavyāvṛttātmā yathāvidhi sūnave nṛpatikakudaṃ dattvā yūne sitātapavāraṇam, munivanatarucchāyāṃ devyā tayā saha śiśriye galitavayasām ikṣvākūṇā idaṃ hi kulavrtam.

#### <span class="box">4.1</span>

sa rājyaṃ guruṇā dattaṃ pratipadyādhikaṃ babhau, dinānte nihitaṃ tejaḥ savitreva hutāśanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.1*</span>

nyastaśastraṃ dilīpaṃ ca taṃ ca śuśruvuṣāṃ patim, rājñām uddhṛtanārāce hṛdi śalyam ivārpitam.

#### <span class="box">4.2</span>

dilīpānantaraṃ rājye taṃ niśamya pratiṣṭhitam, pūrvaṃ pradūmito rājñāṃ hṛdaye 'gnir ivotthitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.3</span>

puruhūtadhvajasyeva tasyonnayanapaṅktayaḥ, navābhyutthānadarśinyo nananduḥ sa prajāḥ prajāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.4</span>

samam eva samākrāntaṃ tasyonnayanapaṅktayaḥ, tena siṃhāsanaṃ pitryam akhilaṃ cārimaṇḍalaṃ.

#### <span class="box">4.5</span>

chāyāmaṇḍalalakṣyena tam adṛśyā kila svayam, padmā padmātapatreṇa bheje sāmrājyadīkṣitam.

#### <span class="box">4.6</span>

parikalpitasāṃnidhyā kāle kāle ca bandiṣu, stutyaṃ stutibhir arthyābhir upatasthe sarasvatī.

#### <span class="box">4.7</span>

manuprabhṛtibhir mānyair bhuktā yady api rājabhiḥ, tathāpy ananyapūrveva tasminn āsīd vasuṃdharā.
#### <span class="box">4.8</span>

sa hi sarvasya lokasya yuktadaṇḍatayā manaḥ, ādade nātiśītoṣṇo nabhasvān iva dakṣiṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.9</span>

mandotkaṇṭaḥ kṛtās tena guṇādhikatayā gurau, phalena sahakārasya phuṣpodgama iva prajāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.10</span>

nayavidbhir nave rājñi sad asac copadarśitam, pūrva evābhavat pakṣas tasmin nābhavad uttaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.11</span>

pañcānām api bhūtānām utkarṣaṃ pupuṣur guṇāḥ, nave tasmin mahīpāle sarvaṃ navam ivābhavat.

#### <span class="box">4.12</span>

yathā prahlādanāc candraḥ pratāpāt tapano yathā, tathaiva so 'bhūd anvartho rājā prakṛtirañjanāt.

#### <span class="box">4.13</span>

kāmaṃ karṇāntaviṣrānte viśāle tasya locane, cakṣuṣmattā tu śāstreṇa sūkṣmakāryārthadarśinā.

#### <span class="box">4.14</span>

labdhapraśamanasvastham athainaṃ samupasthitā, pārthivaśrīr dvitīyeva śarat paṅkajalakṣaṇā.

#### <span class="box">4.15</span>

nirvṛṣṭalaghubhir meghair muktavartmā suduḥsahaḥ, svaṃ dhanuḥ śaṅkiteneva yugapad vyānaśe diśaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.15*</span>

adhijyam āyudhaṃ kartuṃ muktavartmā suduḥsahaḥ, svaṃ dhanuḥ śaṅkiteneva saṃjahre śatamanyunā.

#### <span class="box">4.16</span>

vārṣikaṃ saṃjahārendro dhanur jaitraṃ raghur dadhau, prajārthasādhane tau hi paryāyodyatakārmukau.

#### <span class="box">4.17</span>

puṇḍarīkātapatras taṃ vikasatkāśacāmaraḥ, ṛtur viḍambayām āsa āsīt samarasā dvayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.18</span>

prasādarīkātapatras taṃ candre ca viśadaprabhe, tadā cakṣuṣmatāṃ prītir āsīt samarasā dvayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.19</span>

haṃsaśreṇīṣu tārāsu kumudvatsu ca vāriṣu, vibhūtayays tadīyānāṃ paryastā yaśasām iva.

#### <span class="box">4.20</span>

ikṣucchāyaniṣādinyas tasya goptur guṇodayam, ākumārakathodghātaṃ śāligopyo jagur yaśaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.21</span>

prasasādodayād ambhaḥ kumbhayoner mahaujasaḥ, raghor abhibhavāśaṅki cukṣubhe dviṣatāṃ manaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.22</span>

madodagrāḥ kakudmantaḥ saritāṃ kūlamudrujāḥ, līlākhelam anuprāpur mohakṣās tasya vikramam.

#### <span class="box">4.23</span>

prasavaiḥ saptaparṇānāṃ madagandhibhir āhatāḥ, asūyayeva tannāgāḥ saptadhaiva prasusruvuḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.24</span>

saritaḥ kurvatī gādhāḥ pathaś cāśyānakardamān, yātrāyai codayām āsa taṃ śakteḥ prathamaṃ śarat.

#### <span class="box">4.25</span>

samyak tasmai ghuto vahnir vājinīrājanāvidhau, pradakṣiṇārcir vyājena hasteneva jayaṃ dadau.

#### <span class="box">4.26</span>

sa guptamūlapratyantaḥ śuddhapārṣṇir ayānvitaḥ, ṣaḍvidhaṃ balam ādāya pratasthe digjigīṣayā.

#### <span class="box">4.27</span>

avākiran vayovṛddhās taṃ lājaiḥ paurayoṣitaḥ, pṛṣatair mandaroddhūtaiḥ kṣīrormaya ivācyutam.

#### <span class="box">4.28</span>

sa yayau prathamaṃ prācīṃ tulyaḥ prācīnabarhiṣā, ahitān aniloddhūtais tarjayann iva ketubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.29</span>

rajobhiḥ syandanoddhūtair gajaiś ca ghanasaṃnibhaiḥ, bhuvas talam iva vyoma kurvan vyomeva bhūtalam.

#### <span class="box">4.30</span>

pratāpo 'gre tataḥ śabdaḥ parāgas tadantaram, yayau paścād rathādīti catuḥskandheva sā camūḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.31</span>

marupṛṣṭhāny udambhāṃsi nāvyāḥ supratarā nadīḥ, vipināni prakāśāni śaktimattvāc cakāra saḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.31*</span>

purogaiḥ kaluṣās tasya sahaprasthāyibhiḥ kṛśāḥ, paścātprayāyibhiḥ paṅkāś cakrire mārganimnagāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.32</span>

sa senāṃ mahatīṃ karṣan pūrvasāgaragāminīm, babhau harajaṭābhraṣṭāṃ gaṅgām iva bhagīrathaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.33</span>

tyājitaiḥ phalam utkhātair bhagnaiś ca bahudhā nṛpaiḥ, tasyāsīd ulbaṇo mārgaḥ pādapair iva dantinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.34</span>

paurastyān evam ākrāmaṃs tāṃs tāñ janapadāñ jayī, prāpa tālīvanśyāmam upakañṭhaṃ mahodadheḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.35</span>

anamrāṇāṃ samuddhartus tasmāt sindhurayād iva, ātmā saṃrakṣitaḥ suhmair vṛttim āśritya vaitasīm.

#### <span class="box">4.36</span>

vaṅgān utkhāya tarasā netā nausādhanoddhatān, nicakhāna jayastambhān gaṅgāsroto'ntareṣu saḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.37</span>

āpādapadmapraṇatāḥ kalamā iva te raghum, phalaiḥ saṃvardhayām āsur utkhātapratirpitāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.38</span>

sa tīrtvā kapiṣāṃ sainyair baddhadviradasetubhiḥ, utkalādarśitapathaḥ kaliṅgābhimukho yayau.

#### <span class="box">4.39</span>

sa pratāpaṃ mahendrasya mūrdhni tīkṣṇaṃ nyaveśayat, aṅkuśaṃ dviradasyeva yantā gambhīravedinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.40</span>

pratijagrāha kāliṅgas tam astrair gajasādhanaḥ, pakṣacchedodyataṃ śakraṃ śilāvarṣīva parvataḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.41</span>

dviṣāṃ viṣahya kākutsthas tatra nārācadurdinam, sanmaṅgalasnāta iva pratipede jayaśriyam.

#### <span class="box">4.41*</span>

vāyavyāstravinirdhūtāt pakṣāviddhān mahodadheḥ, gajānīkāt sa kāliṅgaṃ tārkṣyaḥ sarpam ivādade.

#### <span class="box">4.42</span>

tāmbūlīnāṃ dalais tatra racitāpānabhūmayaḥ, nalikerāsavaṃ yodhāḥ śātravaṃ ca papur yaśaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.43</span>

gṛhītapratimuktasya sa dharmavijayī nṛpaḥ, śriyaṃ mahendranāthasya jahāra na tu medinīm.

#### <span class="box">4.44</span>

tato velātaṭenaiva phalavatpūgamālinā, agastyācaritām āśām anāśāsyajayo yayau.

#### <span class="box">4.45</span>

sa sainyaparibhogeṇa gajadānasugandhinā, kāverīṃ saritāṃ patyuḥ śaṅkanīyām ivākarot.

#### <span class="box">4.46</span>

balair adhuṣitās tasya vijigīṣor gatādhvanaḥ, maricodbhrāntahārītā malayādrer upatyakāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.47</span>

sasañjur aśvakṣuṇṇānām elānām utpatiṣṇavaḥ, tulyagandhiṣu mattebhakaṭeṣu phalareṇavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.47*</span>

ājāneyakhurakṣuṇṇapakvailākṣetrasaṃbhavam, vyānaśe sapadi vyoma tripadīchedinām api.

#### <span class="box">4.48</span>

bhogiveṣṭanamārgeṣu candanānāṃ samarpitam, n'āsrasat kariṇāṃ graivaṃ tripadīchedinām api.

#### <span class="box">4.49</span>

diśi mandāyate tejo dakṣiṇasyāṃ raver api, tasyām eva raghoḥ pāṇḍyāḥ pratāpaṃ na viṣehire.

#### <span class="box">4.50</span>

tāmraparṇīsametasya muktāsāraṃ mahodadheḥ, te nipatya dadus tasmai yaśaḥ svam iva saṃcitam.

#### <span class="box">4.51</span>

sa nirviśya yathākāmaṃ taṭeṣv ālīnacandanau, stanāv iva diśas tasyāḥ śailau malayadardurau.

#### <span class="box">4.53</span>

tasyānīkair visarpadbhir aparāntajayodyataiḥ, rāmāstrotsārito 'py āsīt sahyalagna ivārṇavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.54</span>

bhayotsṛṣṭavibhūṣāṇāṃ tena keralayoṣitām, alakeṣu camūreṇuś cūrṇapratinidhīkṛtaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.55</span>

muralāmārutoddhūtam agamat kaitakaṃ rajaḥ, tadyodhavārabāṇānām ayatnapaṭavāsatām.

#### <span class="box">4.56</span>

abhyabhūyata vāhānāṃ caratāṃ gātraśiñjitaiḥ, varmabhiḥ pavanoddhūtarājatālīvanadvhvanaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.57</span>

kharjūrīskandhanaddhānāṃ madodgārtasugandhiṣu, kaṭeṣu kariṇāṃ petuḥ puṃnāgebhyaḥ śilīmukhāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.58</span>

avakāśaṃ kilodanvān rāmāyābhyarthito dadau, aparāntamahīpālavyājena raghave karam.

#### <span class="box">4.59</span>

mattebharadanotkīrṇavyaktavikramalakṣaṇam, trikūṭam eva tatroccair jayastambhaṃ cakāra saḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.60</span>

pārasīkāṃs tato jetuṃ pratasthe sthalavartmanā, indriyākhyān iva ripūṃs tattvajñānena saṃyamī.

#### <span class="box">4.61</span>

yavanīmukhapadmānāṃ sehe madhumadaṃ na saḥ, bālātapam ivābjānām akālajaladodayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.62</span>

saṃgrāmas tumulas tasya pāścātyair aśvasādhanaiḥ, śārṅgakūjitavijñeyapratiyodhe rajasy abhūt.

#### <span class="box">4.63</span>

bhallāpavarjitais teṣāṃ śirobhiḥ śmaśrulair mahīm, tastāra saraghāvyāptaiḥ sa kṣaudrapaṭalair iva.

#### <span class="box">4.64</span>

apanītaśirastrāṇāḥ śeṣās taṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ, praṇipātapratīkāraḥ saṃrambho hi mahātmanām.

#### <span class="box">4.65</span>

vinayante sma tadyodhā madhubhir vijayaśramam, āstīrṇājinaratnāsu drākṣāvalayabhūmiṣu.

#### <span class="box">4.66</span>

tataḥ pratasthe kauberīṃ bhāsvān iva raghur diśam, śarair usrair ivodīcyān uddhariṣyam rasān iva.

#### <span class="box">4.66*</span>

jitān ajayyas tān eva kṛtvā rathapuraḥsarān, mahārṇavam ivaurāgniḥ praviveśottarāpatham.

#### <span class="box">4.67</span>

vinītādhvaśramās tasya sindhutīraveceṣṭanaiḥ, dudhuvur vājinaḥ skandhāṃl lagnakuṅkumakesarān.

#### <span class="box">4.68</span>

tatra hūṇāvarodhānāṃ bhartṛśu vyaktavikramam, kapolapāṭalādeśi babhūva raghuceṣṭitam.

#### <span class="box">4.69</span>

kāmbojāḥ samare soḍhuṃ tasya vīryam anīśvarāḥ,  gajālānaparikliṣṭair akṣoṭaiḥ sārdham ānatāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.70</span>

teṣāṃ sadaśvabhūyiṣṭhās tuṅgā draviṇarāśayaḥ, upadā viviśuḥ śaśvan notsekāḥ kosaleśvaram.

#### <span class="box">4.71</span>

tato gaurīguruṃ śailam ārurohāśvasādhanaḥ, vardhayann iva tatkūṭān uddhūtair dhātureṇubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.72</span>

śaśaṃsa tulyasattvānāṃ sainyaghoṣe 'py asaṃbhramam, guhāśayānāṃ siṃhānāṃ parivṛtyāvalokitam.

#### <span class="box">4.73</span>

bhūrjeṣu marmarībhūtāḥ kīcakadhvanihetavaḥ, gaṅgāśīkariṇo mārge marutas taṃ siṣevire.

#### <span class="box">4.74</span>

viśaśramur namerūṇāṃ chāyāsv adhyāsya sainikāḥ, dṛṣado vāsitotsaṅgā niṣaṇṇamṛganābhibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.75</span>

saralāsaktamātaṅgagraiveyasphuritatviṣaḥ, āsannoṣadhayo netur naktam asnehadīpikāḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.76</span>

tasyotsṛṣṭanivāseṣu kaṇṭharajjukṣata tvacaḥ, gajavarṣma kirātebhyaḥ śaśaṃsur devadāravaḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.77</span>

tatra janyaṃ raghor ghoraṃ pārvatīyair gaṇair abhūt, nārācakṣepaṇīyāśmaniṣpeṣotpatitānalam.

#### <span class="box">4.78</span>

śarair utsavasaṃketān sa kṛtvā viratotsavān, jayodāharaṇaṃ bāhvor gāpayām āsa kiṃnarān.

#### <span class="box">4.79</span>

paraspareṇa vijñātas teṣūpāyanapāṇiṣu, rājñā himavataḥ sāro rājñaḥ sāro himādriṇā.

#### <span class="box">4.80</span>

tatrākṣobhyaṃ yaśorāśiṃ niveśyāvarurobha saḥ, paulastyatulitasyādrer ādadhāna iva hriyam.

#### <span class="box">4.81</span>

cakampe tīrṇalauhitye tasmin prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ, tadgālānatāṃ prāptaiḥ saha kālāgurudruamaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.82</span>

na prasehe sa ruddhārkam adhārāvarṣadurdinam, rathavartma rajo 'py asya kuta eva patākinīm.

#### <span class="box">4.83</span>

tam īśaḥ kāmarūpāṇām atyākhaṇḍalavikramam, bheje bhinnakaṭair nāgair anyān uparurodha yaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.84</span>

kāmarūpeśvaras tasya hemapīṭhādhidevatām, ratnapuṣpopahāreṇa cchāyām ānarca pādayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.85</span>

iti jitvā diṣo jiṣṇur nyavartata rathoddhatam, rajo viśrāmayan rājñāṃ chattraśūnyeṣu mauliṣu.

#### <span class="box">4.86</span>

sa viśvajitam ājahre yajñaṃ sarvasvadakṣiṇam, ādānaṃ hi visargāya sataṃ vārimucām iva.

#### <span class="box">4.87</span>

sattrānte sacivasakhaḥ puraskriyābhir gurvībhiḥ śamitaparājayavyalīkān, kākutsthaś ciravirahotsukāvarodhān rājanyān svapuranivṛttaye 'numene.

#### <span class="box">4.87*</span>

yajñānte tam avabhṛthābiṣekapūtaṃ satkāraiḥ śamitaparājayavyalīkān, āmantryotsukavanitātpatadvisṛṣṭāḥ svāni svāny avanibhujaḥ purāṇi jagmuḥ.

#### <span class="box">4.88</span>

te rekādhvajakuliśātapatraicihnaṃ samrājaś caraṇayugaṃ prasādalabhyam, prasthānapraṇatibhir aṅgulīṣu cakrur maulisrakcyutamakarandareṇugauram.

#### <span class="box">5.1</span>

tam adhvare viśvajiti kṣitīśaṃ niḥśeṣaviśrāṇitakośajātam, upāttavidyo gurudakṣinārthī kautsaḥ prapede varatantuśiṣyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.2</span>

sa mṛnmaye vītahiraṇmayatvāt pātre nidhāyārgahyam anarghyaśīlaḥ, śrutaprakāśaṃ yaśasā prakāśaḥ pratyujjagāmātithim ātitheyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.3</span>

tam arcayitvā vidhivad vidhijñas tapodhanaṃ mānadhanāgrayāyī, viśāṃpatir viṣṭarabhājam ārāt kṛtāñjaliḥ kṛtyavid ita uvāca.

#### <span class="box">5.4</span>

apy agraṇīr mantrakṛtām ṛṣīṇāṃ kuśāgrabuddhe kuśalī gurus te, yatas tvayā jñānam aśeṣam āptam lokena caitanyam ivoṣṇaraśmeḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.5</span>

kāyena vācā manasāpi śaśvad yat saṃbhṛtaṃ vāsavadhairyalopi, āpādyate na vyayam antarāyaiḥ kaccin maharṣes trividhaṃ tapas tat.

#### <span class="box">5.6</span>

ādhārabandhapramukhaiḥ prayatnaiḥ saṃvardhitānāṃ sutanirviśeṣam, kaccin na vāyvādir upaplavo vaḥ śramacchidaṃ āśramapādapānām.

#### <span class="box">5.7</span>

kriyānimitteṣv api vatsalatvād abhagnakāmā munibhiḥ kuśeṣu, tadaṅkaśayyācyutanābhinālā kaccin mṛgīṇām anaghā prasūtiḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.8</span>

nirvartyate yair niyamābhiṣeko yebhyo nivāpāñjalayaḥ pitḥṇām, tāny uñchaṣaṣṭhāṅkitasaikatāni śivāni vas tīrthajalāni kaccit.

#### <span class="box">5.9</span>

nīvārapākādi kaḍamgarīyair āmṛśyate jānapadair na kaccit, kālopapannātithikalpabhāgaṃ vanyaṃ śarīrasthitisādhanaṃ vaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.10</span>

api prasannena maharṣiṇā tvaṃ samyag vinīyānumato gṛhāya, kālo hy ayaṃ saṃkramituṃ dvitīyaṃ sarvopakārakṣamam āśramaṃ te.

#### <span class="box">5.11</span>

tavārhato nābhigamena tṛptaṃ mano niyogakriyayotsukaṃ me, apy ājñayā śāsitur ātmanā vā prāpto 'si saṃbhāvayituṃ vanān mām.

#### <span class="box">5.12</span>

ity arghyapātrānumitavyayasya raghor udārām api gāṃ niśamya, svārthopapattiṃ prati durbalāśas tam ity avocad varatantuśiṣyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.13</span>

sarvatra no vārttam avehi rājan nāthe kutas tvavy aśubhaṃ prajānām, sūrye tapaty āvaraṇāya dṛṣṭeḥ kalpeta lokasya kathaṃ tamisrā.

#### <span class="box">5.14</span>

bhaktiḥ pratīkṣyeṣu kulocitā te pūrvān mahābhāga tayā 'tiśeṣe, vyatītakālas tv aham abhyupetas tvām arthibhāvād iti me viṣādaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.15</span>

śarīramātreṇa narendra tiṣṭhann ābhāsi tīrthapratipāditarddhiḥ, āraṇyakopāttaphalaprasūtiḥ stambena nīvāra ivāvaśiṣṭaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.16</span>

sthāne bhavān ekanarādhipaḥ sann akiṃcanatvaṃ makhajaṃ vyanakti, paryāyapītasya surair himāṃśoḥ kalākṣayaḥ ślāghyataro hi vṛddheḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.17</span>

tadanyatas tāvad ananyakāryo gurvartham āhartum ahaṃ yatiṣye, svasty astu te nirgalitāmbugarbhaṃ śaradghanaṃ nārdati cātako 'pi.

#### <span class="box">5.18</span>

etāvad uktvā pratiyātukāmaṃ śiṣyaṃ maharṣer nṛpatir niṣidhya, kiṃ vastu vidvan gurave pradeyaṃ tvayā kiyad veti tam anvayuṅkta.

#### <span class="box">5.19</span>

tato yathāvadvihitādhvarāya tasmai smayāveśavivarjitāya, varṇāśramāṇāṃ gurave sa varṇī vicakṣaṇaḥ prastutam ācacakṣe.

#### <span class="box">5.20</span>

samāptavidyena mayā maharṣir vijñāpito 'bhūd gurudakṣiṇāyai, sa me cirāyāskhalitopacārāṃ tāṃ bhaktim evāgaṇayat purastāt.

#### <span class="box">5.21</span>

nirbandhasaṃjātaruṣārthakārśyam acintayitvā guruṇāham uktaḥ, vittasya vidyāparisaṃkhyayā me koṭīṣ catasro daśa cāhareti.

#### <span class="box">5.22</span>

so 'haṃ saparyāvidhibhājanena matvā bahvantaṃ prabhuśabdaśeṣam, abhyutsahe saṃprati noparoddhum alpetaratvāc chrutaniṣkrayasya.

#### <span class="box">5.23</span>

itthaṃ dvijena dvijarākāntir āvedito vedavidāṃ vareṇa, enonivṛttendriyavṛttir enaṃ jagāda bhūyo jagadekanāthaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.24</span>

gurvartham arthī śrutapāradṛśvā raghoḥ sakāśād anavāpya kāmam, gato vadāyāntaram ity ayaṃ me mā bhūt parīvādanavāvatāraḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.25</span>

sa tvaṃ praśaste mahite madīye vasaṃś caturtho 'gnir ivāgnyagāre, dvitrāṇy ahāny arhasi soḍhum arhan yāvad yate sādhayituṃ tvadartham.

#### <span class="box">5.26</span>

tatheti tasy' āvitathaṃ pratītaḥ pratyagrahīt saṃgaram agrajanmā, gām āttasārāṃ raghur apy avekṣya niṣkaṣṭum arthaṃ cakame kuberāt.

#### <span class="box">5.27</span>

vasiṣṭhamantrokṣaṇajāt prabhāvād udanvadākāśamahīdhareṣu, marutsakhasyeva balāhakasya gatir vijaghne na hi tadrathasya.

#### <span class="box">5.28</span>

athādhiśiśye prayathaḥ pradoṣe rathaṃ raghuḥ kalpitaśastragarbham, sāmantasaṃbhāvanayaiva dhīraḥ kailāsanāthaṃ tarasā jigīṣuḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.29</span>

prātaḥ prayāṇābhimukhāya tasmai savismayāḥ kośagṛhe niyuktāḥ, hiraṇmayīṃ kośagṛhasya madhye vṛṣṭiṃ śaśaṃsuḥ patitāṃ nabhastaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.30</span>

taṃ bhūpatir bhāsurahemarāśiṃ labdhaṃ kuberād abhiyāsyamānāt, dideśa kautasya samastam eva pādaṃ sumeror iva vajrabhinnam.

#### <span class="box">5.31</span>

janasya sāketanivāsinas tau dvāv apy abhūtām abhinandyasattvau, gurupradeyādhikanīḥspṛho 'rthī nṛpo 'rthikāmād adhikapradaś ca.

#### <span class="box">5.32</span>

athoṣṭravāmīśatavāhitārthaṃ prajeṣvaraṃ prītamanā maharṣiḥ, spṛṣan kareṇānatapūrvakāyaṃ saṃprasthito vācam uvāca kautsaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.33</span>

kim atra citraṃ yadi kāmasūr bhūr vṛtte sthitasyādhipateḥ prajānām, acintanīyas tu tava prabhāvo manīṣitaṃ dyaur api yena dugdhā.

#### <span class="box">5.34</span>

āśāsyam anyat punaruktabhūtaṃ śreyāṃsi sarvāṇy adhijagmuṣas te, putraṃ labhasvātmaguṇānurūpaṃ bhavantam īḍaṃ bhavataḥ piteva.

#### <span class="box">5.35</span>

itthaṃ prayujyāśiṣam agrajanmā rājñe pratīyāya guroḥ sakāśam, rājāpi lebhe sutam āśu tasmād ālokam arkād iva jīvalokaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.36</span>

brāhme muhūrte kila tasya devī kumārakalpaṃ suṣuve kumāram, ataḥ pitā brahmaṇa eva nāmnā tam ātmajanmānam ajaṃ cakāra.

#### <span class="box">5.37</span>

rūpaṃ tad ojasvi tad eva vīryaṃ tadaiva naisargikam unnatatvam, na kāraṇāt svād bibhide kumāraḥ pravartito dīpa iva pradīpāt.

#### <span class="box">5.38</span>

upāttavidyaṃ vidhivad gurubhyas taṃ yauvanodbhedaviśeṣakāntam, śrīr gantukāmāpi guror anujñāṃ dhīreva kanyā pitur ācakāṅkṣa.

#### <span class="box">5.39</span>

atheśvareṇa krathakaiśikānāṃ svayaṃvarārthaṃ svasur indumatyāḥ, āptaḥ kumārānayanotsukena bhojena dūto raghave visṛṣṭaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.40</span>

taṃ ślāghyasaṃbandham asau vicintya dārakriyāyogyadaśaṃ ca putram, prasthāpayām āsa sasainyam enam ṛddhāṃ vidarbhādhiparājadhānīm.

#### <span class="box">5.41</span>

tasyopakāryāracitopakārā vanyetarā jānapadopadābhiḥ, mārge nivāsā manujendrasūnor babhūvur udyānavihārakalpāḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.42</span>

sa narmadārodhasi śīkarārdrair marudbhir ānartitanaktamāle, niveśayām āsa vilaṅghitādhvā klāntaṃ rajodhūsaraketu sainyam.

#### <span class="box">5.43</span>

athopariṣṭād bhramarair bhramadbhiḥ prāk sūcitāntaḥsalilapraveśaḥ, nirdhauta dānāmalagaṇḍabhittir yanyaḥ saritto gaja unmamajja.

#### <span class="box">5.44</span>

niḥśeṣavikṣālitadhātunāpi vaprakriyām ṛkṣavatas taṭeṣu, nīlordhvarekhāśabalena śaṃsan dantadvayenāśmavikuṇṭhitena.

#### <span class="box">5.45</span>

saṃhāravikṣepalaghukriyeṇa hastena tīrābhimukhaḥ saśabdam, babhau sa bhindan bṛhatas taraṅgān vāryargalābhaṅga iva pravṛttaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.45*</span>

sa bhogibhogādhikapīvareṇa hastena tīrābhimukhaḥ saśabdam, saṃvardhitārtdhaprahitena dīrghān cikṣepa vārīparighān ivormīn.

#### <span class="box">5.46</span>

śailopamaḥ śaivalamañjarīṇāṃ jālāni karṣann urasā sa paścāt, pūrvaṃ tadutpīḍitavārirāśiḥ saritpravāhas taṭam utsasarpa.

#### <span class="box">5.46*</span>

kāraṇḍavotsṛṣṭamṛdupratnānāḥ pulindayoṣāmbuvihārakāñcīḥ, karṣan sa śaivālalatā nadīṣaḥ skandhāvalagnās taṭam utsasarpa.

#### <span class="box">5.47</span>

tasyaikanāgasya kapolabhittyor jalāvagāhakṣaṇamātraśāntā, vanyetarānekapadarśanena punar didīpe madadurdinaśrīḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.48</span>

saptacchadakṣīrakaṭupravāham asahyam āghrāya madaṃ tadīyam, vilaṅghitādhoraṇatīvrayatnāḥ senāgajendrā vimukhā babhūvuḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.49</span>

sa cchinnabandhadrutayugyaśūnyaṃ bhagnākṣaparyastarathaṃ kṣaṇena, rāmāparitāṇavihastayodhaṃ senāniveśaṃ tumulaṃ cakāra.

#### <span class="box">5.50</span>

tam āpatantaṃ nṛpater avadhyo vanyaḥ karīti śrutavān kumāraḥ, nivartayiṣyan viśikhena kumbhe jaghāna nātyāyatakṛṣṭaśārṅgaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.51</span>

sa viddhamātraḥ kila nāgarūpam utsṛjya tadvismitasainyadṛṣṭaḥ, sphuratprabhāmaṇḍalamadhyavarti kāntaṃ vapur vyomacaraṃ prapede.

#### <span class="box">5.52</span>

atha prabhāvopanataiḥ kumāraṃ kalpadrumotthair avakīrya puṣpaiḥ, uvāca vāgmī daśanaprabhābhiḥ saṃvardhitoraḥsthalatārahāraḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.53</span>

mataṅgaśāpād avalepamūlād avāptavān asmi mataṅgajatvam, avehi gandharvapates tanūjaṃ priyaṃvadaṃ māṃ priyadarśanasya.

#### <span class="box">5.54</span>

sa cānunītaḥ praṇatena paścān mayā maharṣir mṛdutām agacchat, uṣṇatvam agnyātapasaṃprayogāc chaityaṃ hi yat sā prakṛtir jalasya.

#### <span class="box">5.55</span>

ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhavo yadā te bhetsyaty ajaḥ kumbham ayomukhena, saṃyokṣyase svena vapurmahimnā tadety avocat sa taponidhir mām.

#### <span class="box">5.56</span>

saṃmocitaḥ sattvavatā tvayāhaṃ śāpāc ciraprārthitadarśanena, pratipriyaṃ ced bhavato na kuryāṃ vṛthā hi me syāt svapadopalabdhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.57</span>

saṃmohanaṃ nāma sakhe mamāstraṃ prayogasaṃhāravibhaktamantram, gāndharvam ādhatsva yataḥ prayoktur na cārihiṃsā vijayaś ca haste.

#### <span class="box">5.58</span>

alaṃ hriyā māṃ prati yan muhūrtaṃ dayāparo 'bhuḥ praharann api tvam, tasmād upacchandayati prayojaṃ mayi tvayā na pratiśedharaukṣyam.

#### <span class="box">5.59</span>

tathety upaspṛśya payaḥ pavitraṃ somodhbavāyāḥ sarito nṛsomaḥ, udaṅmukhaḥ so 'stravid astramantraṃ jagrāha tasmān nigṛhītaśāpāt.

#### <span class="box">5.60</span>

evaṃ tayor adhvani daivayogād āseduṣoḥ sakhyam acintyahetu, eko yayau caitrarathapadeśān saurājyaramyān aparo vidarbhān.

#### <span class="box">5.61</span>

taṃ tasthivāṃsaṃ nagaropakaṇṭhe tadāgamārūḍhagurupraharṣaḥ, pratyujjagāma krathakaiśikendraś candraṃ pravṛddhormir ivormimālī.

#### <span class="box">5.62</span>

praveśya cainaṃ puram agrayāyī nīcais tathopācarad arpitaśrīḥ, mene yathā tatra janaḥ sameto vaidarbham āgantum ajaṃ gṛheśam.

#### <span class="box">5.63</span>

tasy' ādhikārapuruṣaiḥ praṇataiḥ pradiṣṭāṃ prāgdvāravediviniveśitapūrṇa kumbhām, mene yathā tatra janaḥ sameto bālyāt parām iva daśāṃ madano 'dhyuvāsa.

#### <span class="box">5.64</span>

tatra svayaṃvarasamāhṛtarājalokaṃ kanyālalāma kamanīyam ajasya lipsoḥ, bhāvāvabodhakaluṣā dayiteva rātrau nidrā cireṇa nayanābhimukhī babhūva.

#### <span class="box">5.65</span>

taṃ karṇabhūṣaṇanipīḍitapīvarāṃsaṃ śayyottaracchadavimardakṛśāṅgarāgam, sūtātmajāḥ savayasaḥ prathitaprabodhaṃ) prābodhayann uṣasi vāgbhir udāravācaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.66</span>

rātrir gatā matimatāṃ vara muñca śayyāṃ dhātrā dvidhaiva nanu dhūr jagato vibhaktā, tām ekatas tava bibharti gurur vinidras tasyā bhavān aparadhuryapadāvalambī.

#### <span class="box">5.67</span>

nidrāvaśena bhavatāpy anapekṣamāṇā paryutsukatvam abalā niśi khaṇḍiteva, lakṣmīr vinodayati yena digantalambī so 'pi tvadānanaruciṃ vijahāti candraḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.68</span>

tad valgunā yugapadunmiṣitena tāvat sadyaḥ paraparatulām adhirohatāṃ dve, praspandamānaparuṣetaratāram antaś cakṣus tava pracalitabhramaraṃ ca padmam.

#### <span class="box">5.69</span>

vṛntāc chlathaṃ harati puṣpam anokahānāṃ saṃsṛjyate sarasijair aruṇāmśubhinnaiḥ, svābhāvikaṃ paraguṇena vibhātavāyuḥ saurabhyam īpsur iva te mukhamārutasya.

#### <span class="box">5.70</span>

tāmrodareṣu paitaṃ tarupallaveṣu nirdhauta hāragulikāviśadaṃ himāmbhaḥ, ābhāti labdhaparabhāgatayādharoṣṭhe līlāsmitaṃ sadaśanārcir iva tvadīyam.

#### <span class="box">5.71</span>

yāvat pratāpanidhir ākramate na bhānur ahnāya tāvad aruṇena tamo nirastam, āyodhanāgrasaratāṃ tvayi vīra yāte kiṃ vā ripūṃs tava guruḥ svayam ucchinatti.

#### <span class="box">5.72</span>

śayyāṃ jahaty ubhayapakṣavinītanidrāḥ stamberamā mukharaśṛṅkhalakarṣiṇas te, yeṣāṃ vibhānti taruṇāruṇarāgayogād bhinnādrigairikataṭā iva dantakoṣāḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.73</span>

dīrgheṣv amī niyamitāḥ paṭamaṇḍapeṣu nidrāṃ vihāya vanajākṣa vanāyudeśyāḥ, vaktroṣmaṇā malinayanti purogatāni lehyāni saindhavaśilāśakalāni vāhāḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.74</span>

bhavati viralabhaktir mlānapuṣpopahāraḥ svakiraṇpariveṣodhbedaśūnyāḥ pradīpāḥ, ayam api ca giraṃ nas tvatprabodhaprayuktām anuvadati śukas te mañjuvāk pañjarasthaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.75</span>

iti viracitavāgbhir bandiputraiḥ kumāraḥ sapadi vigatanidras talpam ujjhāṃ cakāra, madapaṭu ninadadbhir bodhito rājahaṃsaiḥ suragaja iva gāṅgaṃ saikataṃ supratīkaḥ.

#### <span class="box">5.76</span>

atha vidhim avasāyya śāstradṛṣṭaṃ divasamukhocitam añcitākṣipakṣmā, kuśalaviracitānukūlaveṣaḥ kṣitipasamājam agāt svayaṃvarastham.

#### <span class="box">6.1</span>

sa tatra mañceṣu manojñaveṣān siṃhāsanasthān upacāravastu, vaimānikānāṃ marutām apaśyad ākṛṣṭalīlān naralokapālān.

#### <span class="box">6.2</span>

rater gṛhītānunayena kāmaṃ pratyarpitasvāṅgam iveśvareṇa, kākutstham ālokayatāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ mano babhūvendumatīnirāśam.

#### <span class="box">6.3</span>

vaidarbhanirdiṣṭam asau kumāraḥ kḷptena sopānapathena mañcam, śilāvibhaṅgair mṛgarājaśāvas tuṅgaṃ nagotsaṅgam ivāruroha.

#### <span class="box">6.4</span>

parārdhyavarṇāstaraṇopapannam āsedivān ratnavad (?) āsanaṃ saḥ, bhūyiṣṭham āsīd upameyakāntir mayūrapṛṣṭhāśrayiṇā guhena.

#### <span class="box">6.5</span>

tāsu śriyā rājaparaṃparāsu prabhāviśeṣodayadurnirīkṣyaḥ, sahasradhātmā vyarucad vibhaktaḥ payomucāṃ paṅktiṣu vidyuteva.

#### <span class="box">6.6</span>

teṣāṃ mahārhāsanasaṃsthitānām udāranepathyabhṛtāṃ sa madhye, rarāja dhāmnā raghusūnur eva kalpadrumāṇām iva pārijātaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.7</span>

netravrajāḥ paurajanasya tasmin vihāya sarvān nṛpatīn nipetuḥ, madotkaṭe recitapuṣpavṛkṣā gandhadvipe vanya iva dvirephāḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.8</span>

atha stute bandibhir anvayajñaiḥ somārkavaṃśye naradevaloke, saṃcārite c' āgārusārayonau dhūpe samutsarpati vaijayantīḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.9</span>

puropakaṇṭhopavanāśrayāṇāṃ kalāpinām uddhatanṛtyahetau, pradhmātaśaṅkhe parito digantāṃs tūryasvane mūrchati maṅgalārthe.
#### <span class="box">6.10</span>

manuṣyavāhyaṃ caturaśrayānam adhyāsya kanyā parivāraśobhi, viveśa mañcāntararājamārgaṃ patiṃvarā kḷptavivāhaveṣā.

#### <span class="box">6.11</span>

tasmin vidhānātiśaye vidhātuḥ kanyāmaye netraśataikalakṣye, nipetur antaḥkaraṇair narendrā dehaiḥ sthitāḥ kevalam āsaneṣu.

#### <span class="box">6.12</span>

tāṃ praty abhivyaktamanorathānāṃ mahīpatīnāṃ praṇayāgradūtyaḥ, pravālośobhā iva pādapānāṃ śṛṅgāraceṣṭa vividhā babhūvuḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.13</span>

kaścit karābhyām upagūḍhanālam ālolapattrābhihatadvirepham, rajobhir antaḥ pariveṣabandhi līlāravindaṃ bhramayāṃ cakāra.

#### <span class="box">6.14</span>

visrastam aṃsād aparo vilāsī ratnānuviddhāṅgadakoṭilagnam, prālambam utkṛṣya yathāvakaśaṃ nināya sācīkṛtacāruvaktraḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.15</span>

ākuñcitāgrāṅgulinā tato 'nyaḥ kiṃcitsamāvarjitanetraśobhaḥ, tiryagvisaṃsarpinakhaprabheṇa pādena haimaṃ vililekha pīṭham.

#### <span class="box">6.16</span>

niveśya vāmaṃ bhujam āsanārdhe tatasaṃniveśād adhikonnatāṃsaḥ, kaścid vivṛttatrikabhinnahāraḥ suhṛtsamābhāṣaṇatatparo 'bhūt.

#### <span class="box">6.17</span>

vilāsinīvibhramadantapattram āpāṇḍu raṃ ketakabarham anyaḥ, priyāitambocitasaṃniveśair vipāṭayām āsa yuvā nakhāgraiḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.18</span>

kuśeśayātāmratalena kaścit kareṇa rekhādhvajalāñchanena, ratnāṅgulīyaprabhayānuviddhān udīrayām āsa salīlam akṣān.

#### <span class="box">6.19</span>

kaścid yathābhāgam avasthite 'pi svasaṃniveśād vyatilaṅghinīva, vajrāṃśugarbhāṅgulirandhram ekaṃ vyāpārayām āsa karaṃ kirīṭe.

#### <span class="box">6.20</span>

tato nṛpāṇāṃ śrutavṛttavaṃśā puṃvat pragalbhā pratihārarakṣī, prāk saṃnikarṣaṃ magadheśvarasya nītvā kumārīm avadat sunandā.

#### <span class="box">6.21</span>

asau śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇonmukhānām agādhasattvo magadhapratiṣṭhaḥ, rājā prajārañjanalabdhavarṇaḥ paraṃtapo nāma yathārthanāmā.

#### <span class="box">6.22</span>

kāmaṃ ṇrpāḥ santu saharaśo 'nye rājanvatīm āhur anena bhūmim, nakṣatratārāgrahasaṃkulāpi jyotiṣmatī candramasaiva rātriḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.23</span>

kriyāprabandhād ayam adhvarāṇām ajasram āhūtasahasranetraḥ, śacyāś ciraṃ pāṇdukapolalambān mandāraśūnyān alakāṃś cakāra.

#### <span class="box">6.24</span>

anena ced icchasi gṛhyamāṇaṃ pāṇiṃ vareṇyena kuru praveśe, prāsādavātāyanasaṃśritānāṃ netrotsatvaṃ puṣpapurāṅganānām.

#### <span class="box">6.25</span>

evaṃ tayokte tam avekṣya kiṃcid (?) visraṃsidūrvāṅkamadhūkamālā, ṛjupraṇāmakriyayaiva tanvī pratyādideśainam abhāṣamāṇā.

#### <span class="box">6.26</span>

tāṃ saiva vetragrahaṇe niyuktā rājāntaraṃ rājasutāṃ nināya, samīraṇottheva taraṅgalekhā padmāntaraṃ mānasarājahaṃsīm.

#### <span class="box">6.27</span>

jagāda cainām ayam aṅganāthaḥ surāṅganāprārthitayauvanaśrīḥ, vinītanāgaḥ kila sūtrakārair aindraṃ padaṃ bhūmigato 'pi bhuṅkte.

#### <span class="box">6.28</span>

anena paryāsayatāsrabindūn muktāphalsthūlatamān staneṣu, pratyarpitāḥ śatruvilāsinīnām unmucya sūtreṇa vinaiva hārāḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.29</span>

nisargabhinnāspadam ekasaṃstham asmin dvayaṃ śrīś ca sarasvatī ca, kāntyā girā sūnṛtayā ca yogyā tvam eva kalyāṇi tayos tṛtīyā.

#### <span class="box">6.30</span>

athāṅgarājād avatārya cakṣur yāh janyām avadat kumārī, nāsau na kāmyo na ca veda samyag draṣṭuṃ na sā bhinnarucir hi lokaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.31</span>

tataḥ paraṃ duṣprasahaṃ dviṣadbhir nṛpaṃ niyuktā pratihārabhūmau, nidarśayām āsa viśeṣadṛśyam induṃ navotthānam ivendumatyai.

#### <span class="box">6.32</span>

avantinātho 'yam udagrabāhur viśālavakṣās tanuvṛttamadhyaḥ, āropya cakrabhrahmam uṣṇatejās tvaṣṭreva yatnollikhito vibhāti.

#### <span class="box">6.33</span>

asya prayāṇeṣu samagraśakter agresarair vājibhir utthitāni, kurvanti sāmantaśikhāmaṇīnāṃ prabhāprarohāstamayaṃ rajāṃsi.

#### <span class="box">6.34</span>

asau mahākālaniketanasya vasann adūre kila candramauleḥ, tamisrapakṣe 'pi saha priyābhir jyotsnāvato nirviśati pradoṣān.

#### <span class="box">6.35</span>

anena yūnā saha pārthivena rambhoru kaccin manaso rucis te, siprātaraṅgānilakampitāsu vihartum udyānaparaṃparāsu.

#### <span class="box">6.36</span>

tasminn abhidyotitabandhupadme pratāpasaṃśoṣitaśatrupaṅke, babandha sā nottamasaukumāryā kumudvatī bhānumatīva bhāvam.

#### <span class="box">6.37</span>

tām agratas tāmarasāntarābhām anūparājasya guṇair anūnām, vidhāya sṛṣṭiṃ lalitām vidhātur jagāda bhūyaḥ sudatīṃ sunandā.

#### <span class="box">6.38</span>

saṃgrāmanirviṣṭasahasrabāhur aṣṭadāsadvīpanikhātayūpaḥ, ananyasādhāraṇarājaśabdo babhūva yogī kila kārtavīryaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.39</span>

akāryacintāsamakālam eva prādurbhavaṃś cāpadharaḥ purastāt, antaḥśarīreṣv api yaḥ prajānāṃ pratyādideśāvinayaṃ vinetā.

#### <span class="box">6.40</span>

jyābandhaniṣpandabhujena yasya viniśvasadvaktraparaṃpareṇa, kārāgṛhe nirjitavāsavena laṅkeśvareṇoṣitam ā prasādāt.

#### <span class="box">6.41</span>

tasyānvaye bhūpatir eṣa jātaḥ pratīpa ity āgamavṛddhasevī, yena śriyaḥ saṃśrayadoṣarūḍhaṃ svabhāvalolety ayaśaḥ pramṛśṭam.

#### <span class="box">6.42</span>

āyodhane kṛṣṇagatiṃ sahāyam avāpya yaḥ kṣatriyakālarātrim, dhārāṃ śitāṃ rāmaparaśvadhasya saṃbhāvayaty utpalapattrasārām.

#### <span class="box">6.43</span>

asyāṅkalakṣmīr bhava dīrghabāhor māhiṣmatīvapranitambakāñcīm, prāsādajālair jalveṇiramyāṃ revāṃ yadi prekṣitum asti kāmaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.44</span>

tasyāḥ prakāmaṃ priyadarśano 'pi na sa kṣitīśo rucaye babhūva, śaratpramṛṣṭāmbudharoparodhaḥ śaśīva paryāptakalo nalinyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.45</span>

sā śūrasendādhipatiṃ suṣeṇam uddiśya lokāntaragītakīrtim, ācāraśuddhobhayavaṃśadīpaṃ śuddhāntarakṣyā jagade kumārī.

#### <span class="box">6.46</span>

nīpānvayaḥ pārthiva eṣa vajvā guṇair yam āśritya paraspareṇa, siddhāśramaṃ śāntam ivaitya sattvair naisargiko 'py utsasṛje virodhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.47</span>

yasy' ātmagehe nayanābhirāmā kāntir himāṃśor iva saṃniviṣṭa, harmyāgrasaṃrūḍhatṛṇāṅkureṣu tejo 'viśahyaṃ ripumandireṣu.

#### <span class="box">6.48</span>

yasyāvarodhastanacandanānāṃ prakṣālanād vārivihārakāle, kalindakanyā mathurāṃ gatā 'pi gaṅgormisaṃsakta jaleva bhāti.

#### <span class="box">6.49</span>

trastena tākrṣyāt kila kāliyena maṇiṃ visṛṣṭaṃ yamunaukasā yaḥ, vakṣaḥsthalavyāpirucaṃ dadhānaḥ sakaustubhaṃ hrepayatīva kṛṣnam.

#### <span class="box">6.50</span>

saṃbhāvya bhartāram amuṃ yuvānaṃ mṛdupravālottarapuṣpaśayye, vṛndāvane caitrarathād anūne nirviśyatāṃ sundari yuvanaśrīḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.51</span>

adhyāsya cāmbhaḥpṛṣatokṣitāni śaileyagandhīni śilātalāni, kalāpināṃ prāvṛṣi paśya nṛtyaṃ kāntāsu govardhanakandarāsu.

#### <span class="box">6.52</span>

nṛpaṃ tam āvartamanojñanābhiḥ sā vyatyagād anyavadhūr bhavitrī, mahīdharaṃ mārgavaśād upetaṃ srotovahā sāgaragāminīva.

#### <span class="box">6.53</span>

athāṅgadāśliṣṭabhujaṃ bhujiṣyā hemāṅgadaṃ nāma kaliṅganātham, āseduṣīṃ sāditaśatrupakṣaṃ bālām abālendumukhīṃ babhāṣe.

#### <span class="box">6.54</span>

asau mahendrādrisamānasāraḥ patir mahendrasya mahodadheś ca, yasya kṣaratsainyagajacchalena yātrāsu yātīva puro mahendraḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.55</span>

jyāghātarekhe subhujo bhujābhyāṃ bibharti yaś cāpabhṛtāṃ purogaḥ, ripuśriyāṃ sāñjanabhāṣpaseke bandīkṛṭānām iva paddhatī dve.

#### <span class="box">6.55*</span>

raṇe 'mitatrīṇatayā prakāśaḥ śarāsanajyānikaṣau bhujābhyām, viśiṣṭarekhau ripuvikramāgner nirvāṇamārgāv iva yo bibharti.

#### <span class="box">6.56</span>

yam ātmanaḥ sadmani saṃnikṛṣṭo mandradhvanityājitayāmatūryaḥ, prāsādavātāyanadṛṣyavīciḥ prabodhayaty arṇava eva suptam.

#### <span class="box">6.57</span>

anena sārdhaṃ viharāmburāśes tīreṣu tālīvanamarmareṣu, dvīpānatarānītalavaṅgapuṣpair apākṛtasvedalavā marudbhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.58</span>

pralobhitāpy ākṛtilobhanīyā patiṃ purasyorugapūrvanāmnaḥ, tasmād apāvartata dūrakṛṣṭā nītyeva lakṣmīḥ pratikūladaivāt.

#### <span class="box">6.58*</span>

athādhigamyābhuvarājakalpaṃ patiṃ purasyorugapūrvanāmnaḥ, ācārapūtobhayavaṃśadīpaṃ śuddhāntarakṣyā jagade kumārī.

#### <span class="box">6.59</span>

athorākhyasya purasya nāthaṃ dauvārikī devasarūpam, itaś cakorākṣi vilokayeti pūrvānuśiṣṭāṃ nijagāda bhojyām.

#### <span class="box">6.60</span>

pāṇḍyo 'yam aṃsārpitalambahāraḥ kḷptāṅgarāgo haricandanena, ābhāti bālātaparaktasānuḥ sanirjharodgāra ivādrirājaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.61</span>

vindhyasya saṃstambhayitā mahādrer niḥśeṣapītojjhitasindhurājaḥ, prītyāśvamedhāvabhṛthārdramūrteḥ sausnātiko yasya bhavaty agastyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.62</span>

astraṃ harād āptavatā durāpaṃ yenendralokāva jayāya dṛptaḥ, purā janasthānavimardaśaṅkī saṃdhāya laḥkādhipatiḥ pratasthe.

#### <span class="box">6.63</span>

anena pāṇau vidhivad (?) gṛhīte mahākulīnena mahīva gurvī, ratnānuviddhārṇavamekhalāyā diśaḥ sapatnī bhava dakṣiṇasyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.64</span>

tāmbūlavallīpariṇaddhapūgāsv elālatāliṅgitacandanāsu, tamālapattrāstaraṇāsu rantuṃ prasīda śaśvan malayasthalīṣu.

#### <span class="box">6.65</span>

indīvaraśyāmatanaur nṛpo 'sau tvaṃ rocanāgauraśarīrayaṣṭiḥ, anyonyaśobhāparivṛddhaye vāṃ yogas taḍittoyadayor ivāstu.

#### <span class="box">6.66</span>

svasur vidarbhādhipates tadīyo lebhe 'ntaraṃ cetasi nopadeśaḥ, divākarādarśanabaddhakośe nakśatranāthāṃśur ivāravinde.

#### <span class="box">6.67</span>

saṃcāriṇī dīpaśikheva rātrau yaṃ yaṃ vyatīyāya patiṃvarā sā, narendramārgāṭṭa iva prapede vivarṇabhāvaṃ sa sa bhūmipālaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.68</span>

tasyāṃ raghoḥ sūnur upasthitāyāṃ vṛṇīta māṃ neti samākulo 'bhūt, vāmetaraḥ saṃśayam asya bāhuḥ keyūrabandhocchavasitair nunoda.

#### <span class="box">6.69</span>

taṃ prāpya sarvāvayavānavadyaṃ vyāvartatānyopagamāt kumārī, na hi praphullaṃ sahakāram etya vṛksāntaraṃ kāṅkṣati ṣaṭpadālī.

#### <span class="box">6.70</span>

tasmin samāveśitacittavṛttim induprabhām indumatīm avekṣya, pracakrame vaktum anukramajñā savistaraṃ vākyam idaṃ sunandā.

#### <span class="box">6.71</span>

ikṣvākuvaṃśyaḥ kakudaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ kakutstha ity āhitalakṣaṇo 'bhūt, kākutsthaśabdaṃ yata unnatecchāḥ ślāghyaṃ dadhaty uttarakosalendrāḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.72</span>

mahendram āsthāya mahokṣarūpaṃ yaḥ saṃyati prāptapināki līlaḥ, cakāra bāṇair asurāṅganānāṃ gaṇḍasthalīḥ proṣitapattralekhāḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.73</span>

airāvatāsphālanaviślathaṃ yaḥ saṃghaṭṭayann aṅgadam aṅgadena, upeyuśaḥ svām api mūrtim agryām ardhāsanaṃ gotrabhido 'dhitaṣṭhau.

#### <span class="box">6.74</span>

jātaḥ kule tasya kilorukīrtiḥ kulapradīpo nṛpatir dilīpaḥ, atiṣṭhad ekonaśatakratutve śakrābhyasūyāvinivṛttaye yaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.75</span>

yasmin mahīṃ śāsati vāṇinīnāṃ nidrāṃ vihārārdhapathe gatānām, vāto 'pi nāsaraṃsayad aṃśukāni ko lambayed āharaṇāya hastam.

#### <span class="box">6.76</span>

putro raghus tasya padaṃ praśāsti mahākrator viśvajitaḥ prayoktā, caturdigāvarjitasaṃbhṛtāṃ yo mṛtpātraśeṣām akarod vibhūtim.

#### <span class="box">6.77</span>

ārūḍham adrīn udadhīn vitīrṇaṃ bhujaṃgamānāṃ vasatiṃ praviṣṭam, ūrdhvaṃ gataṃ yasya na cānubandhi yaśaḥ paricchettum iyattayālam.

#### <span class="box">6.78</span>

asau kumāras tam ajo 'nujātas triviṣṭapasyeva patiṃ jayantaḥ, gurvīṃ dhuraṃ yo bhuvanasya pitrā dhuryeṇa damyaḥ sadṛśaṃ bibharti.

#### <span class="box">6.79</span>

kulena kāntyā vayasā navena guṇaiś ca tais tair vinayapradhānaiḥ, tvam ātmanas tulyam amuṃ vṛṇīṣva ratnaṃ samāgacchatu kāñcanena.

#### <span class="box">6.80</span>

tataḥ sunandāvacanāvasāne lajjāṃ tanū kṛtya narendrakanyā, dṛṣṭyā prasādāmalayā kumāraṃ pratyagrahīt saṃvaraṇasrajeva.

#### <span class="box">6.81</span>

sā yūni tasminn abhilāṣabandhaṃ śaśāka śālīnatayā na vaktum, romāñcalakṣyeṇa sa gātrayaṣṭiṃ bhittvā nirākrāmad arālakeśyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.82</span>

tathāgatāyāṃ parihāsapūrvaṃ sakhyāṃ sakhī vetradharā babhāṣe, ārye vrajāmo 'nyata ity athaināṃ vadhūr asūyākuṭilaṃ dadarśa.

#### <span class="box">6.83</span>

sā cūrṇagauraṃ raghunandanasya dhātrīkarābhyāṃ karabhopamorūḥ, āsañjayām āsa yathāpradeśaṃ kaṇṭhe guṇaṃ mūrtam ivānurāgam.

#### <span class="box">6.84</span>

tayā srajā maṅgalapuṣpamayyā viśālavakṣaḥsthalalambayā saḥ, amaṃsta kaṇṭhārpitabāhupāśāṃ vidarbharājāvarajāṃ vareṇyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.85</span>

śaśinam upagateyaṃ kaumudī meghamuktaṃ jalanidhim anurūpaṃ, iti samaguṇayogaprītayas tatra paurāḥ śravaṇakaṭu nṛpāṇām ekavākyaṃ vivavruḥ.

#### <span class="box">6.86</span>

pramuditavarapakṣam ekatas tat (?) kṣitipatimaṇḍalam anyato vitānam, uṣasi sara iva praphullapadmaṃ kumudavanapratipannanidram āsīt.

#### <span class="box">7.1</span>

athopayantrā sadṛśena yuktāṃ skandena sākṣād iva devasenām, svasāram ādāya vidarbhanāthaḥ purapraveśābhimukho babhūva.

#### <span class="box">7.2</span>

senāniveśān pṛthivīkṣito 'pi jagmur vibhātagrahamandabhāsaḥ, bhojyāṃ prati vyarthamanorathatvād rūpeṣu veṣeṣu ca sābhyasūyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.3</span>

sāṃnidhyayogāt kila tatra śacyāḥ svayaṃvarakṣobhakṛtām abhāvaḥ, kākutstham uddiśya samatsaro 'pi śaśāma tena kṣitipālalokaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.4</span>

tāvat prakīrṇābhinavopacāram indrāyudhadyotitatoraṇāṅkam, varaḥ sa vadhvā saha rājamārgaṃ prāpa dhvajacchāyanivāritoṣṇam.

#### <span class="box">7.5</span>

tatas tadālokanatatparāṇāṃ saudheṣu cāmīkarajālavatsu, babhūvur itthaṃ purasundarīṇāṃ tyaktānyakāryāṇi viceṣṭitāni.

#### <span class="box">7.6</span>

ālokamārgaṃ sahasā vrajantyā kayācid udveṣṭanavāntamālyaḥ, baddhuṃ na saṃbhāvita eva tāvat kareṇa ruddho 'pi hi keśapāśaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.7</span>

prasādhikālambitam agrapādam ākṣipya kācid dravarāgam eva, utṣṛṣṛalīlāgatir ā gavākṣād yayau śalākām aparā vahantī.
#### <span class="box">7.8</span>

vilocanaṃ dakṣiṇam añjanena saṃbhāvya tadvañcitavāmanetrā, tathaiva vātāyanasaṃnikarṣaṃ yayau śalākām aparā vahantī.

#### <span class="box">7.9</span>

jālāntarapreṣitadṛṣṭir anyā prasthānabhinnāṃ na babandha nīvīm, nābhipraviṣṭābharaṇaprabheṇa hastena tasthāv avalambya vāsaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.10</span>

ardhācitā satvaram utthitāyāḥ pade pade durnimite galantī, kasyāścid āsīd raśanā tadānīm aṅguṣṭhamāulārpitasūtraśeṣā.

#### <span class="box">7.10*</span>

stanaṃdhayantaṃ tanayaṃ vihāya vilokanāya tvarayā vrajantī, saṃprasnutābhyāṃ padavīṃ stanābhyāṃ siṣeca kācit payas'' ā gavākṣāt.

#### <span class="box">7.11</span>

tāsāṃ mukhair āsavagandhagarbhair vyāptāntarāḥ sāndrakutūhalānām, vilolanetrabhramarair gavākṣāḥ sahasrapattrābharaṇā ivāsan.

#### <span class="box">7.12</span>

tā rāghavaṃ dṛṣṭibhir āpibantyo nāryo na jagmur viṣayāntarāṇi, tathā hi śeṣendriyavṛttir āsāṃ sarvātmanā cakṣur iva praviṣṭā.

#### <span class="box">7.13</span>

sthāne vṛtā bhūpatibhiḥ parokṣaiḥ svayaṃvaraṃ sādhum amaṃsta bhojyā, padmeva nārāyaṇam anyathāsau labheta kāntaṃ katham ātmatulyam.

#### <span class="box">7.14</span>

paraspareṇa spṛhaṇīyaśobhaṃ na ced idaṃ dvandvam ayojayiṣyat, asmin dvaye rūpavidhānayatnaḥ patyuḥ prajānāṃ vitatho 'bhaviṣyat.

#### <span class="box">7.15</span>

ratismarau nūnam imāv abhūtāṃ rājñāṃ sahareṣu tathā hi bālā, gateyam ātmapratirūpam eva mano hi janmāntarasaṃgatijñam.

#### <span class="box">7.16</span>
