ity udgatāḥ pauravadhūmukhebhyaḥ śṛṇvan kathāḥ śrotasukhāḥ kumāraḥ, udbhāsitaṃ maṅgalasaṃvidhābhiḥ saṃbandhinaḥ sadma samāsasāda.

#### <span class="box">7.17</span>

tato 'vatīryāśu kareṇukāyāḥ sa kāmarūpeśvaradattahastaḥ, vaidarbhanirdiṣṭam atho viveśa nārīmanāṃsīva catuṣkam antaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.18</span>

mahārhasiṃhāsanasaṃsthito 'sau saratnam arghyaṃ madhuparkamiśram, bhojopanītaṃ ca dukūlayugmaṃ jagrāha sārdhaṃ vanitākaṭākṣaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.19</span>

dukūlavāsāḥ sa vadhūsamīpaṃ ninye vinītair avarodharakṣaiḥ, velāsākśaṃ sphuṭapeharājir navair udanvān iva candrapādaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.20</span>

tatrārcito bhojapateḥ purodhā hutvāgnim ājyādibhir agnikalpaḥ, tam eva cādhāya vivāhasākṣye vadhūvarau saṃgamayāṃ cakāra.

#### <span class="box">7.21</span>

hastena hastaṃ parigṛhya vadhvāḥ sa rājasūnuḥ sutarāṃ cakāśe, anantarāśokalatāpravālaṃ prāpyeva cūtaḥ pratipallavena.

#### <span class="box">7.22</span>

āsīd varaḥ kaṇṭakitaprakoṣṭaḥ svinnāṅguliḥ saṃvavṛte kumārī, vṛttis tayoḥ pāṇisamāgamena samaṃ vibhakteva maobhavasya.

#### <span class="box">7.23</span>

tayor apāṅga-pratisāritāni kriyāsamāpattivartitāni, hrīyantraṇām ānaśire manojñām anyonyalolāni vilocanāni.

#### <span class="box">7.24</span>

pradakṣiṇaprakramaṇāt kṛṣānor udarciṣas tan (?) mithunaṃ cakāśe, meror upānteṣv iva vartamānam anyonyasaṃsaktam ahastriyāmam.

#### <span class="box">7.25</span>

nitambagurvī guruṇā prayuktā vadhūr vidhātṛpratimena tena, cakāra sā mattacakoranetrā lajjāvatī lājavisargam agnau.

#### <span class="box">7.26</span>

haviḥśamīpallavalājagandhiḥ puṇyaḥ kṛśānor udiyāya dhūmaḥ, kapolasaṃsarpiśikhaḥ sa tasyā muhūrtakarṇotpalatāṃ prapede.

#### <span class="box">7.27</span>

tad añjanakledasamākulākṣaṃ pramlānabhījāṅkurakarṇapūram, vadhūmukhaṃ pāṭalagaṇḍalekham ācāradhūmagrahaṇād babhūva.

#### <span class="box">7.28</span>

tau snātakair bandhumatā ca rājñā puraṃdhribhiś ca kramaśaḥ prayuktam, kanyākumārau kanakāsanasthāv ārdrākṣatāropaṇam anvabhūtām.

#### <span class="box">7.29</span>

iti svasur bhojakulapradīpaḥ saṃpādya pāṇigrahaṇaṃ sa rājā, mahīpatīnāṃ pṛthagarhaṇārthaṃ samādideśādhikṛtān adhiśrīḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.30</span>

liṅgair mudaḥ saṃvṛtavikriyās te hradāḥ prasannā iva gūḍhanakrāḥ, vaidarbham āmantrya yayus tadīyāṃ pratyarpya pūjām aupdāchalena.

#### <span class="box">7.31</span>

sa rājalokaḥ kṛtapūrvasaṃvid ārambhasiddhau samayopalabhyam), ādāsyamānaḥ pramdāmiṣaṃ tad āvṛtya panthānam ajasya tasthau.

#### <span class="box">7.32</span>

bhartāpi tāvat krathakaiṣikānām anuṣṭhitānantarajāvivāhaḥ, sattvānurūpāharaṇī kṛtaśrīḥ prāsthāpayad rāghavam anvagāc ca.

#### <span class="box">7.33</span>

tisras trilokī prathitena sārdham ajena mārge vasatīr uṣitvā, tasmād apāvartata kuṇḍineśaḥ parvātyaye soma ivoṣṇaraśmeḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.34</span>

pramanyavaḥ prāg api kosalendre pratyekam āttasvatayā babhūvuḥ, ato nṛpāś cakṣamire sametāḥ strīratnalābhaṃ na tadātmajasya.

#### <span class="box">7.35</span>

tam udvahantaṃ pathi bhojakanyāṃ rurodha rājanyagaṇaḥ sa dṛptaḥ, balipradiṣṭaṃ śriyam ādadānaṃ traivikramaṃ pādam ivendraśatruḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.36</span>

tasyaḥ sa rakṣārtham analpayodham ādiṣya pitryaṃ sacivaṃ kumāraḥ, pratyagrahīt pārthivavāhinīṃ tāṃ jyotīrathāṃ śoṇa ivottaraṅgaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.37</span>

pattiḥ padātiṃ rathinaṃ ratheśas turaṃgasādī turagādhirūḍham, yantā gajasyābhyapatad gajasthaṃ tulyapratidvandvi babhūva yuddham.

#### <span class="box">7.38</span>

nadatsu tūryeṣv avibhāvyavāco nodīrayanti sma kulopadeśān, bāṇākṣarair eva parasparasya nāmorjitaṃ cāpabhṛtaḥ śaśaṃsuḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.39</span>

utthāpitaḥ saṃyati reṇur aśvaiḥ sāndrīkṛtaḥ syandanavaṃśacakraiḥ, cistāritaḥ kuñjarakarṇatālair netrakrameṇoparurodha sūryam.

#### <span class="box">7.40</span>

matsyadhvajā vāyuvaśād vidīrṇair mukhaiḥ pravṛddhadvajinīrajāṃsi, babhuḥ pibantaḥ paramārthamatsyāḥ paryāvilānīva navodakāni.

#### <span class="box">7.41</span>

ratho rathāṅgadhvaninā vijajñe vilolaghaṇṭākvaṇitena nāgaḥ, svabhartṛnāmagrahaṇād babhūva sāndre rajasy ātmaparāvabodhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.42</span>

āvṛṇvato locanamārgam ājau rajo'ndhakārasya vijṛmbhitasya, śastrakṣatāśvadvipavīrajanmā bālāruṇo 'bhūd rudhirapravāhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.43</span>

sa cchinnamūlaḥ kṣatajena reṇus tasyopariṣṭāt pavanāvadhūtaḥ, aṅgāraśeṣasya hutāśanasya pūrvotthito dhūma ivābabhāse.

#### <span class="box">7.44</span>

prahāramūrchāpagame rathasthān yantḥn upālabhya nivartitāśvāḥ, yaiḥ sāditā lakṣitapūrvaketūṃs tān eva sāmarṣatayā nijaghnuḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.45</span>

apy ardhamārge parabāṇalūnā dhanurbhṛtāṃ hastavatāṃ pṛṣatkāḥ, saṃprāpur evātmajavānuvṛttyā pūrvārdhabhāgaiḥ phalibhiḥ śaravyam.

#### <span class="box">7.46</span>

ādhoraṇānāṃ gajasaṃnipāte śirāṃsi cakrair niśitaiḥ kṣurāgraiḥ, hatāny api āyenanakhāgrakoṭivyāsaktakeśāni cireṇa petuḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.47</span>

pūrvaṃ prahartā na jaghāna bhūyaḥ pratiprahārākṣamam aśvasādī, turaṃgamaskandhaniṣaṇṇadehaṃ pratyāśvasantaṃ ripum ācakāṅkṣa.

#### <span class="box">7.48</span>

tanutyajāṃ varmabhṛtāṃ vikośair bṛhatsu danteṣv asibhiḥ patadbhiḥ, raṇakṣitiḥ śoṇitamadyakulyā gajā vivignāḥ karaśīkareṇa.

#### <span class="box">7.49</span>

śilīmukhotkṛttaśiraḥphalāḍhyā cyutaiḥ śiratraiś caṣakottareva, raṇakṣitiḥ śoṇitamadyakulyā rarāja mṛtyor iva pānabhūmiḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.50</span>

upāntayor niṣkuṣitaṃ vihaṃgair ākṣipya tebhyaḥ piśitapriyāpi, keyūrakoṭikṣatatāludeśā śivā bhujacchedam apācakāra.

#### <span class="box">7.51</span>

kaścid dviṣatkhaḍgahṛtottamāṅgaḥ sadyo vimānaprabhutām upetya, vāmāṅgasaṃsaktasurāṅganaḥ svaṃ nṛtyat kabandhaṃ samare dadarśa.

#### <span class="box">7.52</span>

anyonyasūtonmathanād abhūtāṃ tāv eva sūtau rathinau ca kaucit, vyaśvau gadāvyāyatasaṃprahārau bagnāyudhau bāhuvimardaniṣṭhau.

#### <span class="box">7.53</span>

paraspareṇa kṣatayoḥ prahartror utkrāntavāyvoḥ samakālam eva, amartyabhāve 'pi kayościd āsīd ekāsaraḥprārthitayor vivādaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.54</span>

vyūhāv ubhau tāv itaretarasmād bhaṅgaṃ jayaṃ cāpatur avyavastham, paścātpuromārutayoḥ pravṛddhau paryāyavṛttyeva mahārṇavormī.

#### <span class="box">7.55</span>

pareṇa bhagne 'pi bale mahaujā yayāv ajaḥ praty arisainyam eva, dhūmo nivarteta samīraṇena yato hi kakṣas tata eva vahniḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.56</span>

rathī niṣaṅgī kavacī dhanuṣmān dṛptaḥ sa rājanyakam ekavīraḥ, nivārayām āsa mahāvarāhaḥ kalpakṣayoddhūtam ivārṇavāmbhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.57</span>

sa dakṣiṇaṃ tūṇa-mukhena vāmaṃ vyāpārayan hastam alakṣyatājau, ākarṇakṛṣṭā sakṛd asya yoddhur maurvīva bāṇān suṣuve riguphnān.

#### <span class="box">7.58</span>

sa roṣadaṣṭādhikalohitoṣṭhair vyaktordhvarekā bhṛkuṭīr vahadbhiḥ, tastāra gāṃ bhallanikṛttakaṇṭhair huṃkāragarbhair dviṣatāṃ śirobhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.59</span>

sarvair balāṅgair dviradapradhānaiḥ sarvāyudhaiḥ kaṅkaṭabhedibhiś ca, sarvaprayatnene ca bhūmipālās tasmin prajahrur yudhi sarva eva.

#### <span class="box">7.60</span>

so 'stravrajaiś channarathaḥ pareṣāṃ dhvajāgramātreṇa babhūva lakṣyaḥ, nīhāramagno dinapūrvabhāgaḥ kiṃcitprakāśena vivasvateva.

#### <span class="box">7.61</span>

priyaṃvadāt prāpam asau kumāraḥ prāyuṅkta rājasv adhirājasūnuḥ, gāndharvam astraṃ kusumāstrakāntaḥ prasvāpanaṃ svapanivṛttalaulyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.62</span>

tato dhanuṣkarṣaṇamūḍhahastam ekāṃsaparyastaśirastrajālam, tasthau dhvajastambhaniṣaṇṇadehaṃ nidrāvidheyaṃ naradevasainyam.

#### <span class="box">7.63</span>

tataḥ priyopāttarase 'dharoṣṭhe niveśya dadhmau jalaṃ kumāraḥ, yena svahastārjitam ekavīraḥ piban yaśo mūrtam ivābhāse.

#### <span class="box">7.64</span>

śaṅkhasvanābhijñatayā nivṛttās taṃ sannaśatruṃ dadṛśuḥ svayodhāḥ, nimīlitānām iva paṅkajānāṃ madhye sphurantaṃ pratimāśaśāṅkam.

#### <span class="box">7.65</span>

saśoṇitais tena śilīmukhāgrair nikṣepitāḥ ketuṣu pārthivānām, yaśo hṛtam saṃprati rāghaveṇa na jīvitaṃ vaḥ kṛpayeti varṇāḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.66</span>

sa cāpakoṭīnihitaikabāhuḥ śirastaniṣkarṣaṇabhinnamuliḥ, lalāṭabaddhaśramavāribindur bhītāṃ priyām etya vaco babhāṣe.

#### <span class="box">7.67</span>

itaḥ parān arbhakahāryaśastrān vaidarbhi paśyānumatā mayāsi, evaṃvidhenāhavaceṣṭitena tvaṃ prārthyase hastagatā mamabhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.68</span>

tasyāḥ pratidvandvibhavād viṣādāt sadyo vimuktaṃ mukham ābabhāse, niśvāsabāṣpāpagamāt prapannaḥ prasādam ātmīyam ivātmadarṣāḥ.

#### <span class="box">7.69</span>

hṛṣṭāpi sā hrīvijitā na sākṣād vāgbhiḥ sakhīnāṃ priyam abhyanandat, sthalī navāmbhaḥpṛṣatābhivṛṣṭā mayūrakekābhir ivābhravṛndam.

#### <span class="box">7.70</span>

iti śirasi sa vāmaṃ pādam ādhāya rājñām udavahad anavadyāṃ tām avadyād apetah, rathaturagarajobhis tasya rūkṣālakāgrā samaravijayalaṣmīḥ saiva mūrtā babhūva.

#### <span class="box">7.71</span>

prathamaparigatārthas taṃ raghuḥ saṃnivṛttaṃ vijayinam abhinandya ślāghyajāyāsametam, tadupahitakuṭumbaḥ śāntimārgotusko 'bhūn na hi sati kuladhurye sūryavaṃśyā gṛhāya.

#### <span class="box">8.1</span>

atha tasya vivāhakautukaṃ lalitaṃ bibhrata eva pārthivaḥ, vasudhām api hastagāminīm akarod indumatīm ivāparām.

#### <span class="box">8.2</span>

duritair api kartum ātmasāt prayatante nṛpasūnavo hi yat, tad upasthitam agrahīd ajaḥ pitur ājñeti na bhogatṛṣṇayā.

#### <span class="box">8.3</span>

anubhūya vasiṣṭhasaṃbhṛtaiḥ salilais tena sahābhiṣecanam, viśadocchavasitena medinī kathayām āsa kṛtārthatām iva.

#### <span class="box">8.4</span>

sa babhūva durāsadaḥ parair guruṇātharvavidā kṛtakriyaḥ, pavanāgnisamāgamo hy ayaṃ sahitaṃ brahma yad astratejasā.

#### <span class="box">8.5</span>

raghum eva nivṛttayauvanaṃ tam amanyanta naveśvaraṃ prajāḥ, sa hi tasya na kevalāṃ śriyaṃ pratipede sakalān guṇān api.

#### <span class="box">8.6</span>

adhikaṃ śuśubhe śubhaṃyunā dvitayena dvayam eva saṃgatam, padam ṛddham ajena paitṛkaṃ vinayenāsya navaṃ ca yauvanam.

#### <span class="box">8.7</span>

sadayaṃ bubhuje mahābhujaḥ sahasodvegam iyaṃ vrajed iti, aciropanatāṃ sa medinīṃ navapāṇigrahaṇāṃ vadhūm iva.

#### <span class="box">8.8</span>

aham eva mato mahīpater iti sarvaḥ prakṛtiṣv acintayat, udadher iva nimagāśateṣv abhavan nāsya vimānanā kvacit.

#### <span class="box">8.9</span>

na kharo na ca bhūyasā mṛduḥ pavamānaḥ pṛthivīruhān iva, sa puraskṛtamadhyamakramo namayām āsa nṛpān anuddharan.

#### <span class="box">8.10</span>

atha vīksya raghuḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ prakṛtiṣv ātmajam ātmavat tayā, viṣayeṣu vināśadharmasu tridivasteṣv api niḥspṛho 'bhavat.

#### <span class="box">8.11</span>

guṇavatsutaropitaśriyaḥ pariṇāme hi dilīpavaṃśajāḥ, padavīṃ taruvalkavāsasāṃ prayatāḥ saṃyamināṃ prapedire.

#### <span class="box">8.12</span>

tam araṇyasamāśrayonmukhaṃ śirasā veṣṭanaśobhinā sutaḥ, pitaraṃ praṇipatya pādayor aparityāgam ayācatātmanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.13</span>

raghur aśrumukhasya tasya tat kṛtavān īpsitam ātmajapriyaḥ, na tu sarpa iva tvacaṃ punaḥ pratipede vyapavarjitāṃ śriyam.

#### <span class="box">8.14</span>

sa kīlaśramam antyam āśrito nivasann āvasathe purād bahiḥ, samupāsyata putrabhogyayā snūṣayevāvikṛtendriyaḥ śriyā.

#### <span class="box">8.15</span>

praśamasthitapūrvapārthivaṃ kulam abhyudyata nūtaneśvaram, nabhasā nibhṛtendunā tulām uditārkeṇa samāruroha tat.

#### <span class="box">8.16</span>

yatipārthivaliṅgadhāriṇau dadṛśate raghurāghavau janaiḥ, apavargamahodayārthayor bhuvam aṃśāv iva dharmayor gatau.

#### <span class="box">8.17</span>

ajitādhigamāya mantribhir yuyuje nītiviśaradair ajaḥ, anapāyipadopalabdhaye raghur āptaiḥ samiyāya yogibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.17*</span>

samayujayta bhūpatir yuvā sacivaiḥ pratyaham arthasiddhaye, apunarjananopattaye prayayāḥ saṃyamibhir manīṣibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.18</span>

nṛpatiḥ prakṛtīr avekṣitum vyavahārāsanam ādade yuvā, paricetum upāṃśu dhāraṇāṃ kuśapūtaṃ pravayās tu viṣṭaram.

#### <span class="box">8.18*</span>

anuraṇjayituṃ prajāḥ prabhur vyahārāsanam ādade navaḥ, aparaḥ śuciviṣṭarasthitaḥ paricetuṃ yatate sma dhāraṇāḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.19</span>

anayat prabhuśaktisaṃpadā vaśam eko nṛpatīn anantarān, aparaḥ praṇidhānayogyayā marutaḥ pañca śarīragocarān.

#### <span class="box">8.19*</span>

nayacakṣur ajo didṛkṣayā pararandhrasya tatāna maṇḍale, hṛdaye samaropayan manaḥ paramaṃ jyotir avekṣituṃ raghuḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.20</span>

akarod acireśvaraḥ kṣitau dviṣadārambhaphalāni bhasmasāt, aparo dahane svakarmaṇāṃ vavṛte jñānamayena vahninā.

#### <span class="box">8.21</span>

paṇabandhamukhān guṇān ajaḥ ṣaḍ upāyuṅkta samīkṣya tatphalam, raghur apy ajayad guṇatrayaṃ prakṛtisthaṃ samaloṣṭakāñcanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.22</span>

na navaḥ prabhur ā phalodayāt sthirakarmā virarāma karmaṇaḥ, na ca yogavidher navetaraḥ sthiradhīr ā paramātmadarśanāt.

#### <span class="box">8.23</span>

iti śatruṣu cendriyeṣu ca pratiṣiddhaprasareṣu jāgratau, prasitāv udayāpavargayor ubhayīṃ siddhim ubhāv avāpatuḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.24</span>

atha kāścid ajavyapekṣayā gamayitvā samdarśanaḥ samāḥ, tamasaḥ param āpad avyayaṃ puruṣaṃ yogasamādhinā raghuḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.25</span>

śutadehavisarjanaḥ pituś ciram aśrūṇi vimucya rāghavaḥ, vidadhe vidhim asya naiṣṭhikaṃ yatibhiḥ sārdham anagnim agnicit.

#### <span class="box">8.26</span>

akarot sa tadaurdhvadaihikaṃ pitṛbhaktyā pitṛkāryakalpavit, na hi tena pathā tanutyajas tanayāvarjitapiṇḍakāṅkṣiṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.27</span>

sa parārdhyagater aśocyatāṃ pitur uddiśya sadarthavedibhiḥ, śamitādhir adhijyakārmukaḥ kṛtavān apratiśāsanaṃ jagat.

#### <span class="box">8.28</span>

kṣitir indumatī ca bhāminī patim āsādya tam agryapauruṣam, prathamā bahuratnasūr abhūd aparā vīram ajījanat sutam.

#### <span class="box">8.29</span>

daśarāsmiśatopamadyutiṃ yaśasā dikṣu daśav api śrutam, daśapūrvarathaṃ yam ākhyayā daśakaṇṭhāriguruṃ vidur budhāḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.30</span>

ṛṣidevagaṇasvadhābhujāṃ śrutayāgaprasvaiḥ sa pārthivaḥ, anṛṇatvam upeyivān babhau paridher mukta ivoṣṇadīdhitiḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.31</span>

balam ārtabhayopaśāntaye viduṣāṃ saṃnataye bahu śrutam, vasu tasya na kevalaṃ guṇavattāpi paraprayojanā.

#### <span class="box">8.32</span>

sa kadācid aveṣitaprajaḥ saha devyā vijahāra suprajāḥ, nagaropavane śacīsakho marutāṃ pālayiteva nandane.

#### <span class="box">8.33</span>

atha rodhasi dakṣiṇodadheḥ śrita gokarṇaniketam īśvaram, upavīṇayituṃ yayau raver udagāvṛttipathena nāradaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.34</span>

kusumair grathitām apārthivaiḥ srajam ātodyaśironiveśitām, aharat kila tasya vegavān adhivāsaspṛhayeva mārutaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.35</span>

bhramaraiḥ kusumānusāribhiḥ parikīrṇā parivādinī muneḥ, dadṛśe pavanāvalepajaṃ sṛjatī bāṣpam ivāñjanāvilam.

#### <span class="box">8.36</span>

abhibhūya vibhūtim ārtavīṃ madhugandhātiśayena vīrudhām, nṛpater amarasrag āpa sā dayitorustanakoṭisusthitim.

#### <span class="box">8.37</span>

kṣaṇamātrasakhīṃ sujātayoḥ stanayos tām avalokya vihalā, nimimīla narottamapriyā hṛtacandrā tamaseva kaumudī.

#### <span class="box">8.38</span>

vapuṣā karaṇojjhitena sā nipatantī patim apy apātayat, nanu tailaniṣekabindunā saha dīpārcir upaiti medinīm.

#### <span class="box">8.38*</span>

samam eva narādhipena sā gurusaṃmohaviluptacetanā, gurusaṃmohaviluptacetanā navadīpārcir iva kṣites talam.

#### <span class="box">8.39</span>

ubhayor api pārśvavartināṃ tumu lenārtaraveṇa vejitāḥ, vihagāḥ kamalākarālayāḥ samaduḥkhā iva tatra cukruśuḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.40</span>

nṛpater vyajanādibhis tamo nunude sā tu tathaiva saṃsthitā, pratikāravidhānam āyuṣaḥ sati śeṣe hi phalāya kalpate.

#### <span class="box">8.41</span>

pratiyojayitavyavallakīsamavasthām atha sattvaviplavāt, sa nināya nitāntavatsalaḥ parigṛhyocitam aṅkam aṅganām.

#### <span class="box">8.41*</span>

sa nināya nitāntavatsalaḥ parivṛttaprathamacchaviṃ kṣaṇāt, saliloddhṛtapadminīnibhāṃ dayitām aṅkam udaśulocanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.42</span>

sa nināya nitāntavatsalaḥ karaṇāpāyavibhinnavarṇayā, samalakṣyata bibhrad āvilāṃ mṛgalekhām uṣasīva candramāḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.43</span>

vilalāpa sa bāṣpagadgadaṃ sahajām apy apahāya dhīratām, abhitaptam ayo 'pi mārdavaṃ bhajate kaiva kathā śarīriṣu.

#### <span class="box">8.44</span>

kusumāny api gātrasaṃgamāt prabhavanty āyur apohituṃ yadi, na bhaviṣyati hanta sādhanaṃ kim ivānayat prahariṣyato vidheḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.45</span>

atha vā mṛdu vastu hiṃsituṃ mṛdunaivārabhate prajāntakaḥ, himasekavipattir atra me nalinī pūrvanidarśanaṃ matā.

#### <span class="box">8.46</span>

srag iyaṃ yadi jīvitāpahā hṛdaye kiṃ nihitā na hanti mām, viṣam apy amṛtaṃ kvacid bhaved amṛtaṃ vā viṣam īśvarecchayā.

#### <span class="box">8.47</span>

atha vā mama bhāgyaviplavād aśaniḥ kalpita eṣa vedhasā, yad anena tarur na pātitas kṣapitā tadviṭapāśritalatā.

#### <span class="box">8.48</span>

kṛtavaty asi nāvadhīraṇām aparāddhe 'pi yadā ciraṃ mayi, katham ekapade nirāgasaṃ janam ābhāṣyam imaṃ na manyase.

#### <span class="box">8.49</span>

dhruvam asmi śaṭhaḥ śucismite vidhitaḥ kaitavavatsalas tava, paralokam asaṃnivṛttaye yad anāpṛcchya gatāsi mām itaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.50</span>

dayitāṃ yadi tāvad anvagād vinivṛttaṃ kim idaṃ tayā vinā, sahatāṃ hatajīvitaṃ mama prabalām ātmakṛtena vedanām.

#### <span class="box">8.51</span>

surataśramasaṃbhṛto mukhe dhriyate svedalavodgamo 'pi te, atha cāstamitā 'sy aho bata dhig imāṃ dehabhṛtām asāratām.

#### <span class="box">8.51*</span>

surataśramavāribindavo na hi tāvad viramanti te mukhe, katham astamitā 'sy aho bata dhig imām dehavatām asāratām.

#### <span class="box">8.52</span>

manasāpi na vipriyaṃ mayā kṛtapūrvaṃ tava kiṃ jahāsi mām, nanu śabdapatiḥ kṣiter ahaṃ tvayi me bhāvanibandhanā ratiḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.53</span>

kusumotkacitān valīmataś calayan bhṛṅgarucas tavālakān, karabhoru karoti mārutas tvadupāvartanśaṅki me manaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.54</span>

tad apohitum arhasi priye pratibodhena viṣādam āṣu me, jvalitena guhāgataṃ tamas tuhinādrer iva natam oṣadhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.55</span>

idam ucchvasitālakaṃ mukhaṃ viśrāntakathaṃ dunoti mām, niśi suptam ivaikapaṅkajaṃ viratābhyantaraṣaṭpadasvanam.

#### <span class="box">8.56</span>

śaśinaṃ punar eti śārvarī dayitā dvandvacaraṃ patatriṇam, iti tau virhāntarakṣamau katham atyantagatā na māṃ daheḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.57</span>

navapallavasaṃstare 'pi te mṛdu dūyeta yad aṅgam arpitam, tad idaṃ viṣahiṣyate kathaṃ vada vāmoru citādhirohaṇam.

#### <span class="box">8.58</span>

iyam apratibodhaśāyinīṃ raśanā tvāṃ prathamā rahaḥsakhī, gativibhramasāda nīravā na śucā nānumṛteva lakṣyte.

#### <span class="box">8.59</span>

kalam anyabhṛtāsu bhāṣitaṃ kalahaṃsīṣu gataṃ madālasaṃ, pṛṭatīṣu vilolam īkṣitaṃ pavanādhūtalatāsu vibhramaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.60</span>

tridivotsukayāpy avekṣya māṃ nihitāḥ satyam amī guṇās tvayā, virahe tava me guruvyathaṃ hṛdayaṃ na tv avalambituṃ kṣamāḥ.
#### <span class="box">8.61</span>

mithunaṃ parikalpitaṃ tvayā sahakāraḥ phalinī ca nanv imau, avidhāya vivāhasatkriyām anayor gamyata ivy asāṃpratam.

#### <span class="box">8.62</span>

kusumaṃ kṛtadohadas tvayā yad aśoko 'yam udīrayiṣyati, alakābharaṇaṃ kathaṃ nu tat tava neṣyāmi nivāpalālyatām.

#### <span class="box">8.63</span>

smarateva saśabdanūpuraṃ caraṇānugraham anyadurlabham, amunā kusumāśruvarṣiṇā tvam aśokena sugātri śocyase.

#### <span class="box">8.64</span>

tava niḥśvasitānukāribhir bakulair ardhacitāṃ samaṃ mayā, asamāpya vilāsamekhalāṃ kim idaṃ kiṃnarakaṇṭhi supyate.

#### <span class="box">8.65</span>

samaduḥkhasukhaḥ sakhījanaḥ pratipaccandranibho 'yam ātmajaḥ, aham ekarasas tathāpi te vyavasāyaḥ pratipattiniṣṭhuraḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.66</span>

dhṛtir astamitā ratiś cyutā virataṃ geyam ṛtur nirutsavaḥ, gatam ābharaṇaprayojanaṃ pariśūnyaṃ śayanīyam adya me.

#### <span class="box">8.67</span>

gṛhiṇī sacivaḥ sakhī mithaḥ priyaśiṣyā lalite kalāvidhau, karuṇāvimukhena mṛtyunā haratā tvāṃ vada kiṃ na me hṛtam.

#### <span class="box">8.68</span>

madirākṣi madānanārpitaṃ madhu pītvā rasavat kathaṃ nu me, anupāsyasi bāṣpadūṣitaṃ paralokopanataṃ jalāñjalim.

#### <span class="box">8.69</span>

vibhave 'pi sati tvayā vinā sukham etāvad ajasya gaṇyatām, ahṛtasya vilobhanāntarair mama sarve viṣayās tadāśrayāḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.70</span>

vilapann iti kosalādhipaḥ karuṇārthagrathitaṃ priyāṃ prati, akarot pṛthivīruhān api srutaśākhārasabhāṣpadurdinān.

#### <span class="box">8.71</span>

atha tasya kathaṃcid aṅkataḥ svajanas tām apanīya sundarīṃ, visasarja kṛtāntyamaṇḍanām analāy' āgurucandanadihase.

#### <span class="box">8.72</span>

pramadām anu saṃsthitaḥ śucā nṛpatiḥ sann iti vācyadarśanāt, na cakāra śarīram agnisāt saha devyā na tu jīvitāśayā.

#### <span class="box">8.73</span>

atha tena daśāhataḥ pare guṇaśeṣāṃ upadiṣya gehinīm, viduṣā vidhayo maharddhayaḥ pura evopavane samāpitāḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.74</span>

sa viveśa purīṃ tayā vinā kṣaṇadāpāyaśaśāṅkadarśanaḥ, parivāham ivāvalokayan svaśucaḥ pauravadhūmukhāśruṣu.

#### <span class="box">8.75</span>

atha taṃ savanāya diṣitaḥ praṇidhānād gurur āśramasthitaḥ, abhiṣaṅgajaḍaṃ vijajñivān iti śiṣyeṇa kilānvabodhayat.

#### <span class="box">8.76</span>

asamāptavidhir yato munis tava vidvān api tāpakāraṇam, na bhavantam upasthitaḥ svayaṃ prakṛtau sthāpayituṃ kṛtasthitiḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.77</span>

mayi tasya suvṛtta vartate laghusaṃdeśapadā sarasvatī, śṛṇu viśrutasattvasāra tāṃ hṛdi cainām upadhātum arhasi.

#### <span class="box">8.78</span>

puruṣasya padeṣv ajanmanaḥ samatītaṃ ca bhavac ca bhāvi ca, sa hi niṣpratighena cakṣuṣā tritayaṃ jñānamayena paśyati.

#### <span class="box">8.79</span>

carataḥ kila duścaraṃ tapas tṛṇabindoḥ pariśaṅkitaḥ purā, prajighāya samādhibedinīṃ harir asmai hariṇīṃ surāṅganām.

#### <span class="box">8.80</span>

sa tapaḥpratibandhamanyunā pramukhāviṣkṛtacāruvibhramām, aśapad bhava mānuṣīti tāṃ śamavelāpralayormiṇā muniḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.81</span>

bhagavan paravān ayaṃ janaḥ pratikūlācaritaṃ kṣamasva me, iti copanatāṃ kṣitipṛśaṃ vivaśā śāpanivṛttikāraṇam.

#### <span class="box">8.82</span>

krathakaiśikavaṃśasaṃbhavā tava bhūtvā mahiṣī cirāya sā, upalabdhavatī divaś cyutaṃ vivaśā śāpanivṛttikāraṇam.

#### <span class="box">8.83</span>

tad alaṃ tadapāyacintayā vipad utpattimatām upasthitā, vasudheyam avekṣyatāṃ tvayā vasumatyā hi nṛpāḥ kalatriṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.84</span>

udaye madavācyam ujjhatā śrutam āviṣkṛtam ātmavattayā, manasas tad upasthite jvare punar aklībatayā prakāśyatāṃ.

#### <span class="box">8.85</span>

rudatā kuta eva sā punar bhavatā nānumṛtāpi labhyate, paralokajuṣāṃ svakarmabhir gatayo bhinnapathā hi dehinām.

#### <span class="box">8.85*</span>

ruditena na sā nivartate nṛpa tat tāvad anrthakaṃ tava, na bhavān anusaṃsthito 'pi tāṃ labhate karmavaśā hi dehinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.86</span>

apaśokamanāḥ kuṭumbinīm anugṛhṇīṣva nivāpadattibhiḥ, svajanāśru kilātrisaṃtataṃ dahati pretam iti pracakṣate.

#### <span class="box">8.87</span>

maraṇaṃ prakṛtiḥ śarīriṇāṃ vikṛtir jīvitam ucyate budhaiḥ, kṣaṇam apy avatiṣṭhate śvasan yadi jantur nanu lābhavān asau.

#### <span class="box">8.88</span>

avagacchati mūḍhacetanaḥ priyanāśaṃ hṛdi śalyam arpitam, sthiradhīs tu tad eva manyate kuśaladvāratayā samuddhṛtam.

#### <span class="box">8.89</span>

avagacchati mūḍhacetanaḥ śruta dhṛtasaṃyogaviparyayau yadā, virahaḥ kim ivānutāpayed vada bāhyair viṣayair vipaścitam.

#### <span class="box">8.90</span>

na pṛthagjanavac chuco vaśaṃ vaśinām uttama gantum arhasi, drumasānumatāṃ kim antaraṃ yadi vāyau dvitaye 'pi te calāḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.91</span>

sa tatheti vinetur udāramateḥ pratigṛhya vaco visasarja munim, tad alabdhapadaṃ hṛdi śokaghane pratiyātam ivāntikam asya guroḥ.

#### <span class="box">8.92</span>

tenāṣṭau parigamitāḥ samāḥ kathaṃcid bālatvād avitathasūnṛtena sūnoḥ, sādṛśyapratikṛtidarśanaiḥ priyāyāḥ svapneṣu kṣaṇikasamāgamtosavaiś ca.

#### <span class="box">8.93</span>

tasya prasahya hṛdayaṃ kila śokaśaṅkuḥ plakṣapraroha iva saudhatalaṃ bibheda, prāṇāntahetum api taṃ bhiṣajām asādhyaṃ lābhaṃ priyānugamane tvarayā sa mene.

#### <span class="box">8.94</span>

samyagvinītam atha varmaharaṃ kumāram ādiśya rakṣaṇavidhau vidhivat prajānām, rogopasṛṣṭatanudurvasatiṃ mumukṣuḥ prāyopaveśanamatir nṛpatir babhūva.

#### <span class="box">8.95</span>

tīrthe toyavyatikarabhave jahnukanyāsaryvor dehatyāgād amaragaṇanālekhyam āsādya sadyaḥ, pūrvākārādhikatararucā saṃgataḥ kāntayāsau līlāgāreṣv aramata punar nandanābhyantareṣu.

#### <span class="box">9.1</span>

pitur anantaram uttarkosalān samadhigamya samādhijitendriyaḥ, daśarathaḥ praśaśāsa mahāratho yamavatām avatāṃ ca dhuri sthitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.2</span>

adhigataṃ vidhivad yad apālayat prakṛtimaṇḍalam ātmakulocitam, abhavad asya tato guṇavattaraṃ sanagaraṃ nagarandhrakaraujasaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.3</span>

ubhayam eva vadanti manīṣiṇaḥ samayavarṣitayā kṛtakarmaṇām, valaniṣūdanam arthpatiṃ ca taṃ śramanudaṃ manudaṇḍaharānvayam.

#### <span class="box">9.4</span>

janapade na gadaḥ padam ādadhāv abhibhavaḥ kuta eva sapatnajaḥ, kṣitir abhūt phalavaty ajanandane śamarate 'maratejasi pārthive.

#### <span class="box">9.5</span>

daśadigantajitā raghuṇā yathā śriyam apuṣyad ajena tataḥ param, tam adhigamya tathaiva punar babhau na na mahī 'nam ahīnaparākramam.

#### <span class="box">9.6</span>

samatayā vasuvṛṭivisarjanair niyamanād asatāṃ ca narādhipaḥ, anuyayau yamapuṇyajaneśvarau savaruṇāv aruṇāgrasaraṃ rucā.

#### <span class="box">9.7</span>

na mṛgayābhiratir na durodaraṃ na ca śaśipratimābharaṇaṃ madhu, tam udayāya na vā navayauvanā priyatamā yatamānam apāharā.

#### <span class="box">9.8</span>

na kṛpaṇā prabhavaty api vāsave na vitathā parihāsakathāsv api, na ca sapatnajaneṣv api tena vāg aparuṣā paruṣākṣaram īritā.

#### <span class="box">9.9</span>

udayam astamayaṃ ca raghūdvahād ubhayam ānaśire vasudhādhipāḥ, sa hi nideśam alaṅghayatām abhūt suhṛd ayohṛdayaḥ pratigarjatām.

#### <span class="box">9.10</span>

ajayad ekarathena sa medinīm udadhinemim adhijyaśarāsanaḥ, jayam aghoṣayad asya tu kevalaṃ gajavatī javatīrahayā camūḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.10*</span>

jaghananirviṣayīkṛtamekhalān anucitāśruviluptaviśeṣakān, sa ripudāragaṇān akarod balād analakān alakādhipavikramaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.11</span>

avanim ekarathena varūthinā jitavataḥ kila tasya dhanurbhṛtaḥ, vijayadundubhitāṃ yayur arṇavā ghanaravā naravāhanasaṃpadaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.12</span>

śamitapakṣabalaḥ śitakoṭinā śikhariṇāṃ kuliśena puraṃdaraḥ, sa sāravṛṣṭimucā dhanuṣā dviṣāṃ svanavatā navatāmarasānanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.12*</span>

sphuritakoṭisahasramarīcinā samacinot kuliśena harir yaśaḥ, sa dhanuṣā yudhi sāyakavarṣiṇā svanavatā navatāmarasānanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.13</span>

caraṇayor nakharāgasamṛddhibhir mukuṭaratnamarīcibhir aspṛśan, sa dhanuṣā yudhi sāyakavarṣiṇā śatamakhaṃ tam akhaṇḍitapauruṣam.

#### <span class="box">9.14</span>

nivavṛte sa mahārṇavarodhasaḥ sacivakāritabālasutāñjalīn, samanukampya sapatnaparigrahān analakān alakānavamāṃ purīm.

#### <span class="box">9.15</span>

upagato 'pi ca maṇḍalanābhitām anuditānyasitātapavāraṇaḥ, ajitam asti nṛpāspadam ity abhūd analaso 'nalasomasamadyutiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.16</span>

kratuṣu tena visarjitamaulinā bhujasamāhṛtadigvasunā kṛtāḥ, kanakayūpasamucchrayaśobhino vitamasā tamasārasyūtaṭāḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.17</span>

ajinadaṇḍabhṛtaṃ kuśamekhalāṃ yatagiraṃ mṛgaśṛṅgaparigrahām, adhivasaṃs tanum adhvaradīkṣitām asambhāsam abhāsayad īśvaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.18</span>

avabhṛtaprayato niyatendriyaḥ surasamājasamākramaṇocitaḥ, namayati sma sa kevalam unnataṃ vanamuce namucer araye śiraḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.19</span>

tam apahāya kakutsthakulodbhavaṃ puruṣam ātmabhuvaṃ ca pativratā, nṛpatim anyam asevata devatā sakamalā kam alāghavam arthiṣu.

#### <span class="box">9.20</span>

sa kila saṃyugamūrdhni sahāyatāṃ maghavataḥ pratipadya mahārathaḥ, svabhujavīryam agāpayad ucchritaṃ suravadhūr avadhūtabhayāḥ śaraiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.21</span>

asakṛd ekarathena tarasvinā harihayāgrasareṇa dhanurbhṛtā, dinakarābhimukhā raṇareṇavo rurudhire rudhireṇa suradviṣām.

#### <span class="box">9.22</span>

tam alabhanta patiṃ patidevatāḥ śikhariṇāṃ iva sāgaram āpagāḥ, magadhakosalakekayaśasināṃ duhitaro 'hitaropitamārgaṇam.

#### <span class="box">9.23</span>

priyatamābhir asau tiṛbhir babhau tisṛbhir eva bhuvaṃ saha śaktibhiḥ, upagato vininīṣur iva prajā harihayo 'rihayogavicakṣaṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.24</span>

atha samāvavṛte kusumair navais tam iva sevitum ekanarādhipam, yamakuberjaleśvaravajriṇāṃ samadhuraṃ madhur añcitavikramam.

#### <span class="box">9.25</span>

jigamiṣur dhanadādhyuṣitāṃ diśaṃ rathayujā parivartitavāhanaḥ, dinamukhāni ravir himanirgrahair vimalayan malayaṃ nagam atyajat.

#### <span class="box">9.25*</span>

himavivarṇitacandanapallavaṃ virahayan malayādrim udaṅmukhaḥ, vihagayoḥ kṛpayeva śanair yayau ravir aharvirahadhruvabhedayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.26</span>

kusumajanma tato navapallavās tadanu ṣaṭpadakokilakūjitam, iti yathākramam āvirabhūn madhur drumavatīm avatīrya vanasthalīm.

#### <span class="box">9.26*</span>

surabhisaṃgamajaṃ vanamālayā navapalāśam adhāryata bhaṅguram, ramaṇadattam ivārdranakhakṣataṃ pramadayā madayāpitalajjayā.

#### <span class="box">9.27</span>

upahitaṃ śiśirāpagamaśriyā mukulajālam aśobhata kiṃśuke, praṇayinīva nakhakṣatamaṇḍanaṃ pramadayā madayāpitalajjayā.

#### <span class="box">9.27*</span>

parabhṛtā madanakṣatacetasāṃ priyasakhī laghuvāg iva yoṣitām, priyatamān akarot kalahāntare mṛduravā duravāpasamāgamān.

#### <span class="box">9.28</span>

vraṇagurupramadādharaduḥsahaṃ jaghananirviṣayīkṛtamekhalam, na khalu tāvad aśeṣam apohituṃ ravir alaṃ viralaṃ kṛtavān himam.

#### <span class="box">9.28*</span>

viśadacandrakaraṃ sukhamārutaṃ kusumitadrumam unmadakokilam, tad upabhogarasaṃ himavarṣiṇaḥ param ṛtor viralaṃ kṛtavān himam.

#### <span class="box">9.29</span>

abhinayān paricetum ivodyatā malayamārutakampitapallavā, amadayat sahakāralatā manaḥ sakalikā kalikāmajitām api.

#### <span class="box">9.30</span>

nayaguṇopacitām iva bhūpateḥ sadupakāraphalāṃ śriyam arthinaḥ, abhiyayuḥ saraso madhusaṃbhṛtāṃ kamalinīm alinīrapatriṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.30*</span>

daśanacandrikayā vyabhāsitaṃ hasitam āsavagandhi madhor iva, bakulapuṣpam asevyata ṣaṭpadaiḥ śucirasaṃ cirasaṃcitam īpsubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.31</span>

kusumam eva na kevalam ārtavaṃ navam aśokataroḥ smaradīpanam, kisalayaprasavo 'pi vilāsināṃ madayitā dayitāśravaṇārpitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.32</span>

viracitā madhunopavanśriyām abhinavā iva pattraviśeṣakāḥ, madhulihāṃ madhudānaviśāradāḥ kurabakā ravakāraṇatāṃ yayuḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.33</span>

suvadanāvadanāsavasaṃbhṛtas tadanuvādiguṇaḥ kusumodgamaḥ, madhukarair akaron madhulolupair bakulam ākulam āyatapaṅktibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.33*</span>

suvadanāvadanāsavasaṃbhṛtas tadanuvādiguṇaḥ kusumodgamaḥ, iti dayāta ivābhavad āyatā na rajanī rajanīśavatī madhau.

#### <span class="box">9.34</span>

prathamam anyabhṛtābhir udīritāḥ praviralā iva mugdhavadhūkathāḥ, surabhigandhiṣu śuśruvire giraḥ kusumitāsu mitā vanarājiṣu.

#### <span class="box">9.35</span>

śrutisukhabhramarasvanagītayaḥ kusumakomaladantaruco babhuḥ, upavanāntalatāḥ pavanāhataiḥ kisalayaiḥ salayair iva pāṇibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.36</span>

lalitavibhramabandhavicakṣaṇaṃ surabhigandhaparājitakesaram, patiṣu nirviviśur madhum aṅganāḥ smarasakhaṃ rasakhaṇḍanavarjitam.

#### <span class="box">9.36*</span>

tilakamastakaharmyakṛtāspadaiḥ kusumamadhvanuṣaṅgasugandhibhiḥ, kalam agīyata bhṛṅgavilāsināṃ smarayutair ayutair abalāsakhaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.37</span>

śuśubhire smitacārutarānanāḥ striya iva ślathaśiñjitamekhalāḥ, vikacatāmarasā gṛhadīrghikā madakalodakalolavihaṃgamāḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.37*</span>

laghayati sma na patyaparādhajaṃ na sahakāratarus taruṇīdhṛtam, kusumito namito 'libhir unmadaiḥ smarasamādhisamādhikaroṣitam.

#### <span class="box">9.38</span>

upayayau tanutāṃ madhukhaṇḍitā himakarodayapāṇḍumukhacchaviḥ, sadṛśam iṣṭasamāgamanirvṛtiṃ vanitayā 'nitayā rajanīvadhūḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.39</span>

apatuṣāratayā viśadaprabhaiḥ suratarāga pariśramanodibhiḥ, kusumacāpam atejayad aṃśubhir himakaro makarojitaketanam.

#### <span class="box">9.40</span>

hutahutāśanadīpti vanśriyaḥ pratinidhiḥ kanakābharaṇasya yat, yuvatayaḥ kusumaṃ dadhur āhitaṃ tad (?) alake dalakesarapeśalam.

#### <span class="box">9.41</span>

alibhir añjanabindumaoharaiḥ kusumapaṅktinipātibhir aṅkitaḥ, na khalu śobahayit sma vanasthalīṃ na tilakas tilakaḥ pramadām iva.

#### <span class="box">9.42</span>

amadayan madghugandhasanāthayā kisalayādharasaṃgatayā manaḥ, kusumasaṃbhṭtayā navamallikā smitarucā tarucāruvilāsinī.

#### <span class="box">9.42*</span>

analasānyabhṛtā 'nalasān manaḥ kamaladhūlibhṛtā maruteritā, kusumabhāranatādhvagayoṣitām asamaśokam aśokalatā 'karot.

#### <span class="box">9.43</span>

aruṇarāganiṣedhibhir aṃśukaiḥ śravaṇalabdhapadaiś ca yavāṅkuraiḥ, parabhṛtāvirutaiś ca vilāsinaḥ smarabalair abalaikarasāḥ kṛtāḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.44</span>

upacitāvayavā śucibhiḥ kaṇair alikadambakayogam upeyuṣī, sadṛśakāntir alakṣyata mañjarī tilakajā 'lakajālakamauktikaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.45</span>

dhvajapaṭaṃ madanasya dhanurbhṛtaś chavikaraṃ mukhacūrṇam ṛtuśriyaḥ, kusumakesarareṇum alivrajāḥ sapavanopavanotthitam anvayuḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.46</span>

anubhavan navadolam ṛtūtsavaṃ paṭur pai priyakaṇṭhajigṛkṣayā, anayad āsanarajjuparigrahe bhujalatāṃ jaḍatām abalājanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.47</span>

tyajata mānam alaṃ bata bigrahair na punar eti gataṃ caturaṃ vayaḥ, parabhṛtābhir itīva nivedite smaramate ramate sma vadhūjanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.48</span>

atha yathāsukham ārtavam utsavaṃ samanubhūya vilāsavatīsakhaḥ, narapatiś cakame mṛgayāratiṃ sa madhumanmadhumanmathasaṃnibhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.49</span>

paricayaṃ calakṣyanipātane bhayaruṣoś ca tadiṅgitabodhanam, śramajayāt praguṇāṃ ca karoty asau tanum ato 'numataḥ sacivair yayau.

#### <span class="box">9.50</span>

mṛgavanopagamakṣamaveṣabhṛd vipulakaṇṭhaniṣaktaśarāsanaḥ, gaganam aśvakhuroddhuta reṇubhir nṛsavitā savitānam ivākarot.

#### <span class="box">9.51</span>

grathitamaulir asau vanamālayā taru palāśasavarṇatanucchadaḥ, turagavalganacaṇcalakuṇḍalo viruruce ruruceṣṭitabhūmiṣu.

#### <span class="box">9.52</span>

tanulatāviniveśitavigrahā bhramarasaṃkramitekṣaṇavṛttayaḥ, dadṛṣur adhvani taṃ vanadevatāḥ sunayanaṃ nayananditakosalam.

#### <span class="box">9.53</span>

śvagaṇvāgurikaiḥ prathamāsthitaṃ vyapagatānaladasyu viveśa saḥ, sthiraturaṃgamabhūmi nipānavan mṛgavayogavayopacitaṃ vanam.

#### <span class="box">9.54</span>

atha nabhasya iva tridaśāyudhaṃ kanakapiṅgataḍidguṇasaṃyutam, dhanur radhijyam anādhir upādade naravaro ravaroṣitakesarī.

#### <span class="box">9.55</span>

tasya stanapraṇayibhir muhur eṇaśāvair vyāhanyamānahariṇīgamanaṃ purastāt, āvirbabhūva kuśagarbhamukhaṃ mṛgāṇāṃ yūthaṃ tadagrasaragarvitakṛṣnasāram.

#### <span class="box">9.56</span>

tat prārthitaṃ javanvājigatena rājñā tūṇīmukhoddhṛtaśareṇa viśīrṇapaṅkti, śyāmīcakāra vanam ākuladṛśṭipātair vateritotpaladalaprakarair ivāmbhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.57</span>

lakṣyīkṛtasya hariṇasya hariprabhāvaḥ prekṣya sthitāṃ sahacarīṃ vyavadhāya deham, ākarṇakṛṣṭam api kāmitayā sa dhanvī bāṇaṃ kṛpāmṛdhumanāḥ pratisaṃjahāra.

#### <span class="box">9.58</span>

tasyāpareṣv api mṛgeṣu śarān mumukṣoḥ karṇāntam etya bibhide nibiḍo 'pi muṣṭiḥ, trāsātimātracaṭulaiḥ smarayatsu netraiḥ prauḍhapriyānayanavibhramaceṣṭitāni.

#### <span class="box">9.59</span>

uttasthuṣaḥ śiśirapalvalapaṅkamadhyān mustāprarohakavalāvayavānukīrṇam, jagrāha sa drutavarāhakulasya mārgaṃ suvyaktam ārdrapadapaṅktibhir āyatābhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.60</span>

taṃ vāhanād avanatottarakāyam īṣad vidhyantam uddhatasaṭāḥ pratihantum īṣuḥ, nātmānam asya vividuḥ sahasā varāhā vṛkeṣu viddham iṣubhir jaghanāśrayeṣu.

#### <span class="box">9.61</span>

tenābhighātarabhasasya vikṛṣya pattrī vanyasya netravivare mahiṣasya muktaḥ, nirbhidya vigraham aśoṇitaliptapuṅkhas taṃ pātayāṃ prathamam āsa papāta paścāt.

#### <span class="box">9.62</span>

prāyo viṣāṇaparimoṣalaghūttamāṅgān khaḍgāṃś cakāra nṛpatir niśitaiḥ kṣurapraiḥ, śṛṇgaṃ sa dṛptavinayādhikṛtaḥ pareṣām abhyucchritaṃ na mamṛṣe na tu dīrgham āyuḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.63</span>

vyāghrān abhīr abhimukhopatitān guhābhyaḥ phullāsanāgraviṭapān iva vāyurugṇān, śikṣāviśeṣalaghuhastatayā nimeṣāt tūṇīcakāra śarapūritavaktrarandhrān.

#### <span class="box">9.64</span>

nirghātograiḥ kuñjalīnāñ jighāṃsur jyānirghoṣaiḥ kṣobhayām āsa siṃhān, nūnaṃ teṣām abhyasūyāparo 'bhūd vīryodagre rājaśabde mṛgeṣu.

#### <span class="box">9.65</span>

tān hatvā gajakulabaddhatīvravairān kākutsthaḥ kuṭilanakhāgralagnamuktān, ātmānaṃ raṇakṛtakarmaṇāṃ gajānām ānṛṇyaṃ gatam iva mārgaṇair amaṃsta.

#### <span class="box">9.65</span>

tān hatvā gajakulabaddhatīvravairān kākutsthaḥ kuṭilanakhāgralagnamuktān, ātmānaṃ raṇakṛtakarmaṇāṃ gajānām ānṛṇyaṃ gatam iva mārgaṇair amaṃsta.

#### <span class="box">9.66</span>

camarān paritaḥ pravartitāśvaḥ kvacid ākarṇavikṛṣṭabhallavarṣī, nṛpatīn iva tān viyojya sadyaḥ sitavālavyajanair jagāma śāntim.

#### <span class="box">9.67</span>

api turagasamīpād utpatantaṃ mayūraṃ na sa rucirakalāpaṃ bāṇalakṣyī cakāra, sapadi gatamanaskaś citramālyānukīrṇe rativigalitabandhe keśapāśe priyāyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.68</span>

tasya karkaśavihārsaṃbhavaṃ svedam ānanavilagnajālakam, ācacāma satuṣāraśīkaro bhinnapallavapuṭo vanānilaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.69</span>

iti vismṛtānyakaraṇīyam ātmanaḥ sacivāvalambitadhuraṃ narādhipam, parivṛddharāgam anubhandhasevayā mṛgayā jahāra catureva kāminī.

#### <span class="box">9.70</span>

sa lalitakusumapravālaśayyāṃ jvalitamahauṣadhidīpikāsanāthām, narapatir ativāhayāṃ babhūva kvacid asametaparicchadas triyāmām.

#### <span class="box">9.71</span>

uṣasi sa gajayūthakarṇatālaiḥ paṭupaṭadhavanibhir vinītanidraḥ, aramata madhurāṇi tatra śṛṇvan vihagavikūjitabandimaṅgalāni.

#### <span class="box">9.72</span>

atha jātu ruror gṛhītavartmā vipine pārśvacarair alakṣyamāṇaḥ, śramaphenamucā tapasvigāḍhāṃ tamasāṃ prāpa nadīṃ turaṃgameṇa.

#### <span class="box">9.73</span>

kumbhapūraṇabhavaḥ paṭur uccair uccacāra nando 'mbhasi tasyāḥ, tatra sa dviradabṛṃhitaśaṅkī śabdapātinam iṣuṃ visasarja.

#### <span class="box">9.74</span>

nṛpateḥ pratiṣiddham eva tat kṛtavān paṅktiratho vilaṅghya yat, apathe padam arpayanti hi śrutavanto 'pi rajonimīlitāḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.75</span>

hā tāteti kranditam ākarṇya viṣaṇṇas tasyānviṣyan vetasagūḍhaṃ prabhavaṃ saḥ, śalyaprotaṃ prekṣya sakumbhaṃ muniputraṃ tāpād antaḥśalya ivāsīt kśitipo 'pi.

#### <span class="box">9.76</span>

tenāvatīrya turagāt prathitāngvayena pṛṣṭānvayaḥ sa jalakumbhaniṣaṇṇadehaḥ, tasmai dvijetaratapasvisutaṃ skhaladbhir ātmānam akṣarapadaiḥ kathayāṃ babhūva.

#### <span class="box">9.77</span>

taccoditaḥ ca tam anuddhrṛtaśalyam eva pitroḥ sakāśam avasannadṛśor nināya, tābhyāṃ tathāgatam upetya tam ekaputram ajñānataḥ svacaritaṃ nṛpatiḥ śaśaṃsa.

#### <span class="box">9.78</span>

tau daṃpatī bahu vilapya śiśoḥ prahartrā śalyaṃ nikhātam udahārayatām urastaḥ, so 'bhūt parāsur atha bhūmipatiṃ śaśāpa hastārpitair nayanvāribhir eva vṛddhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.79</span>

diṣṭāntam āpsyati bhavān api putraśokād ante vayasy aham iveti tam uktavantam, ākrāntapūrvam iva muktaviṣaṃ bhujaṃgaṃ provāca kosalapatiḥ prathamāparāddhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.80</span>

śāpo 'py adṛṣṭatanayānanapadmaśobhe sānugraho bhagavatā mayi pātito 'yam, kṛṣyāṃ dahann api khalu kṣitim indhaneddho bījaprarohajananīṃ jvalanaḥ karoti.

#### <span class="box">9.81</span>

itthaṃ gate gataghṛṇaḥ kim ayaṃ vidhattāṃ vadhyas tavety abhitite vasudhādhipena, edhān hutāśanavataḥ sa munir yayāce putraṃ parāsum anugantumanāḥ sadāraḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.82</span>

prātānugaḥ sapadi śāsanam asya rājā saṃpādya pātakaviluptadhṛtir nivṛttaḥ, antarniviṣṭapadam ātmavināśahetuṃ śāpaṃ dadhaj jvalanam aurvam ivāmburāśiḥ.

#### <span class="box">9.82A</span>

tadartham arthajñagate gatatrapaḥ kim eṣa te vadhyajano 'nusiṣṭhatu, sa vahnisaṃskāram ayācatātmanaḥ sadārasūnor vidadhe ca tan nṛpaḥ.
#### <span class="box">9.82B</span>

sameyivān raghuvṛṣabhaḥ svasainikaiḥ svamandiraṃ śithiladhṛtir nivartitaḥ, manogataṃ guruṃ ṛṣiśāpam udvahan kṣayānalaṃ jaladhir ivāntakāspadam.

#### <span class="box">10.1</span>

pṛthivīṃ śāsatas tasya pākaśāsanatejasaḥ, kiṃcidūnam anūnarddheḥ śaradām ayutaṃ yayau.

#### <span class="box">10.2</span>

na copalebhe pūrveṣām ṛṇanirmokṣasādhanam, sutābhidhānaṃ sa jyotiḥ śaradām ayutaṃ yayau.

#### <span class="box">10.2*</span>

manor vaṃśaś ciraṃ tasminn anabhivyaktasaṃtatiḥ, nimajjya punar utthāsyan nadaḥ śoṇa ivābhavat.

#### <span class="box">10.3</span>

atiṣṭhat pratyayāpekṣasaṃtatiḥ sa ciraṃ nṛpaḥ, prāṅ manthād anabhivyaktaratnotpattir ivārṇavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.4</span>

ṛṣyaśṛṅgādayas tasya santaḥ saṃtānakāṅkṣiṇaḥ, ārebhire jitātmānaḥ putrīyām iṣṭim ṛtvijaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.5</span>

tasminn avasare devāḥ paulastyopaplutā harim, abhijagmur nidāghārtāś chāyāvṛkṣam ivādhvagāḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.6</span>

te ca prāpur udanvataṃ bubudhe cādipūruṣaḥ, avyākṣepo bhaviṣyantyāḥ kāryasiddher hi lakṣaṇam.

#### <span class="box">10.7</span>

bhogibhogādanāsīnaṃ dadṛśus taṃ divaukasaḥ, tatphaṇāmaṇḍalodarcirmaṇidyotitavigraham.

#### <span class="box">10.8</span>

śriyaḥ padmaniṣaṇṇāyāḥ kṣaumāntaritamekhale, aṅke nikṣiptacaraṇam āstīrṇakarapallave.

#### <span class="box">10.9</span>

prabuddhapuṇḍarīkākṣaṃ bālātapanibhāṃśukam, divasaṃ śāradam iva prārambhasukhadarśanam.

#### <span class="box">10.10</span>

prabhānuliptaśrīvatsaṃ lakṣmīvibhramadarpaṇam, kautsubhākhyam apāṃ sāraṃ bibhrāṇaṃ bṛhatorasā.

#### <span class="box">10.11</span>

bāhubhir viṭapākārair divyābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ, āvirbhūtam apāṃ madhye pārijātam ivāparam.

#### <span class="box">10.12</span>

daityastrīgaṇḍalekhānāṃ madarāgavilopibhiḥ, hetibhiś cetanāvadbhir udīritajayasvanam.

#### <span class="box">10.13</span>

muktaśeṣavirodhena kuliśavraṇalakṣmaṇā, upasthitaṃ prāñjalinā vinītena garutmatā.

#### <span class="box">10.14</span>

yoganidrāntaviśadaiḥ pāvanair avalokanaiḥ, bhṛgvādīn anugṛhṇantaṃ saukha śāyanikān ṛṣīn.

#### <span class="box">10.15</span>

praṇipatya surās tasmai śamayitre suradviṣām, athainaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ stutyam avāṅmanasagocaram.

#### <span class="box">10.16</span>

namo viśvasṛje pūrvaṃ viśvaṃ tadanu bibhrate, atha viśvasya saṃhartre tubhyaṃ tredhāsthitātmane.

#### <span class="box">10.17</span>

rasāntarāṇy ekarasaṃ yathā divyaṃ payo 'śnute, deśe deśe guṇeṣv evam avasthās tvam avikriyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.18</span>

ameyo mitalokas tvam anarthī prārthanāvahaḥ, ajito jiṣṇur atyantam avyakto vyaktakāraṇam.

#### <span class="box">10.19</span>

ekaḥ kāraṇatas tāṃ tām avasthāṃ pratipadyase, nānātvaṃ rāgasaṃyogāt sphaṭikasy'eva te smṛtam.

#### <span class="box">10.20</span>

hṛdayastham anāsannam akāmaṃ tvāṃ tapasvinam, dayālum anaghaspṛṣṭaṃ purāṇam ajaraṃ viduḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.21</span>

sarvajñas tvam avijñātaḥ sarvayonis tvam ātmabhūḥ, sarvaprabhur anīśas tvam ekas tvaṃ sarvarūpabhāk.

#### <span class="box">10.22</span>

saptasāmopagītaṃ tvāṃ saptārṇavajaleśayam, saptārcirmukham ācakhyuḥ saptalokaikasaṃśrayam.

#### <span class="box">10.23</span>

caturvargaphalaṃ jñānaṃ kālāvasthā caturyugā, caturvarṇamayo lokas tvattaḥ sarvaṃ caturmukhāt.

#### <span class="box">10.24</span>

abhyāsanigṛhītena manasā hṛdayāśrayam, jyotirmayaṃ vicinvanti yoginas tvāṃ vimuktaye.

#### <span class="box">10.25</span>

ajasya gṛhṇato janma nirīhasya hatadviṣaḥ, svapato jāgarūkasya yāthātmyaṃ veda kas tava.

#### <span class="box">10.26</span>

śabdādīn viṣayān bhoktuṃ carituṃ duścaraṃ tapaḥ, paryāpto 'si prajāḥ pātum audāsīnyena vartitum.

#### <span class="box">10.27</span>

bahudhāpy āgamair bhinnāḥ panthānaḥ siddhihetavaḥ, tvayy eva nipatanty oghā jāhnavīyā ivārṇave.

#### <span class="box">10.28</span>

tvayy āveśitacittānāṃ tvatsamarpitakarmaṇām, gatis tvaṃ vītarāgāṇām abhūyaḥsaṃnivṛttaye.

#### <span class="box">10.29</span>

pratyakṣo 'py aparicchedyo mahyādir mahimā tava, āptavāganumānābhyāṃ sādhyaṃ tvāṃ prati kā kathā.

#### <span class="box">10.30</span>

kevalaṃ smaraṇenaiva punāsi puruṣaṃ yataḥ, anena vṛttayaḥ śeṣā niveditaphalās tvayi.

#### <span class="box">10.31</span>

udadher iva ratnāni tejāṃsīva vivasvataḥ, stutibhyo vyatiricyante dūreṇa caritāni te.

#### <span class="box">10.32</span>

anavāptam avāptavyaṃ na te kiṃcana vidyate, lokānugraha evaiko hetus te janmakaramaṇoḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.33</span>

mahimānaṃ yad utkīrtya tava saṃhriyate vacaḥ, śrameṇa tad aśaktyā vā na guṇānām iyattayā.

#### <span class="box">10.34</span>

iti prasādayām āsus tava saṃhriyate vacaḥ, bhūtārthavyāhṛtiḥ sā hi na stutiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.35</span>

tasmai kuśalasaṃpraśnavyañjitaprītaye surāḥ, bhayam apralayodvelād ācakhyur nairṛtodadheḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.36</span>

atha velāsamāsannaśailarandhrānunādinā, svareṇovāca bhagavān paribhūtārṇavadhvaniḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.37</span>

purāṇasya kaves tasya varṇasthānasamīritā, babhūva kṛtasaṃskārā caritārthaiva bhāratī.

#### <span class="box">10.38</span>

babhau sa daśanajyotsnā sā vibhor vadanodgatā, niryātaśeṣā caraṇād gaṅgevordhvapravartinī.

#### <span class="box">10.39</span>

jāne vo rakṣasākrāntāv anubhāvaparākramau, aṅgināṃ tamasevobhau guṇau prathmamadhyamau.

#### <span class="box">10.40</span>

viditaṃ tapyamānaṃ ca tena me bhuvantrayam, akāmopanateneva sādhor hṛdayam enasā.

#### <span class="box">10.41</span>

kāryeṣu caikakāryatvād abhyarthyo 'smi na vajriṇā, svayam eva hi vāto 'gneḥ sārathyaṃ pratipadyate.

#### <span class="box">10.42</span>

svāsidhārāparihṛtaḥ kāmaṃ cakrasya tena me, sthāpito daśamo mūrdhā lavyāṃśa iva rakṣasā.

#### <span class="box">10.43</span>

sraṣṭur varātisargāt tu mayā tasya durātmanaḥ, atyārūḍhaṃ ripoḥ soḍhaṃ candaneva bhoginaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.44</span>

dhātāraṃ tapasā prītaṃ yayāce sa hi rākṣasaḥ, daivāt sargād avadhyatvaṃ martyeṣv āsthāparāṅmukhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.45</span>

so 'haṃ dāśarathir bhūtvā raṇabhūmer balikṣamam, kariṣyāmi śarais tīkṣṇais tacchiraḥkamaloccayam.

#### <span class="box">10.46</span>

acirād vajvabhir bhāgaṃ kalpitaṃ vidhivat punaḥ, māyāvibhir anālīḍham ādāsyadhve miśācaraiḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.47</span>

vaimānikāḥ puṇyakṛtas tyajantu marutāṃ pathi, puṣpakālokasaṃkṣobhaṃ meghāvaraṇatatparāḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.48</span>

moṣyadhve svargabandīnāṃ veṇībandhān adūṣitān, śāpayantritapaulastyabalātkārakacagrahaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.49</span>

rāvaṇāvagrahaklāntam iti vāgamṛtena saḥ, abhivṛṣya marutsasyaṃ kṛṣṇameghas tirodadhe.

#### <span class="box">10.50</span>

puruhūtaprabhṛtayaḥ surakāryodyataṃ surāḥ, aṃśair anuyayur viṣṇuṃ puṣpair vāyum iva drumāḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.51</span>

atha tasya viśāṃpatyur ante kāmyasya karmaṇaḥ, puruṣaḥ prababhūvāgner vismayena sahartvijām.

#### <span class="box">10.52</span>

hemapātragataṃ dorbhyām ādadhānaḥ payaścarum, anupraveśād ādyasya puṃsas tenāpi durvaham.

#### <span class="box">10.53</span>

prājāpatyopanītaṃ tad (?) annaṃ pratyagrahīn nṛpaḥ, vṛṣeva payasāṃ sāram āviṣkṛtam udanvatā.

#### <span class="box">10.54</span>

anena kathitā rājño guṇās tasyānyadurlabhāḥ, prasūtiṃ cakame tasmiṃs trailokyaprabhavo 'pi yat.

#### <span class="box">10.55</span>

sa tejo vaiśnavaṃ patnyor vibheje carusaṃjñitam, dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ pratyagram aharpatir ivātapam.

#### <span class="box">10.56</span>

arcitā tasya kausalyā priyā kekayavaṃśajā, ataḥ saṃbhāvitāṃ tābhyāṃ sumitrām aicchad īśvaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.57</span>

te bahujñasya cittajñe patnyau patyur mahīṣitaḥ, caror ardhārdhabhāgābhyāṃ tām ayojayatām ubhe.

#### <span class="box">10.58</span>

sāpi praṇayavaty āsīt sapatnyor ubhayor api, bhramarī vāraṇasyeva madanisyandalekhayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.59</span>

tābhir garbhaḥ prajābhūtyai dadhre devāṃśasambhavaḥ, saurībhir iva nāḍībhir amṛtākhyābhir ammayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.60</span>

samam āpannasattvās tā rejur āpāṇḍuratviṣaḥ, antargataphalārambhāḥ sasyānām iva saṃpadaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.61</span>

guptaṃ dadṛśur ātmānaṃ sarvāḥ svapneṣu vāmanaiḥ, jalajāsigadāśārṅgacakralāñchitamūrtibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.62</span>

hemapakṣaprabhājālaṃ gagane ca vitanvatā, uhyante sma suparṇena vegākṛṣṭapayomucā.

#### <span class="box">10.63</span>

bibhratyā kaustubhaṃ nyāsaṃ stanāntaravilambinam, paryupāsyanta lakṣmyā ca padmavyajanahastayā.

#### <span class="box">10.64</span>

kṛtābhiṣekair divyāyāṃ trisrotasi ca saptabhiḥ, brahma rṣibhiḥ paraṃ brahma gṛṇadhbir upatasthire.

#### <span class="box">10.65</span>

tābhyas tathāvidhān svapnāñ chrutvā prīto hi pārthivaḥ, mene parārdhyam ātmānaṃ gurutvena jagdguroḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.66</span>

vibhaktātmā vibhus tāsām ekaḥ kuṣiṣv anekadhā, uvāsa pratimācandraḥ prasannānām apām iva.

#### <span class="box">10.67</span>

athāgramahiṣī rājñaḥ prasūtisamaye satī, putraṃ tamo'pahaṃ lebhe naktaṃ jyotir ivauṣadhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.68</span>

rāma ity abhirāmeṇa tenāpratima tejasā, nāmadheyaṃ guruś cakre jagatprathamamaṅgalam.

#### <span class="box">10.69</span>

raghuvaṃśapradīpena tenāpratima tejasā, rakṣāgṛhagatā dīpāḥ pratyādiṣṭa ivābhavan.

#### <span class="box">10.70</span>

śayyāgatena rāmeṇa mātā śātodarī babhau, saikatāmbhojabalinā jāhnavīva śaratkṛśā.

#### <span class="box">10.71</span>

kaikeyyās tanayo jajñe bharato nāma śīlavān, janayitrīm alaṃcakre yaḥ praśraya iva śriyam.

#### <span class="box">10.72</span>

sutau lakṣmaṇaśatrughnau sumitrā suṣuve yamau, samyagāgamitā vidyā prabodhavinayāv iva.

#### <span class="box">10.73</span>

nirdoṣam abhavat sarvam āviṣkṛtaguṇaṃ jagat, anvagād iva hi svargo gāṃ gataṃ puruṣottamam.

#### <span class="box">10.74</span>

tasyodaye caturmūrteḥ paulastyacakiteśvarāḥ, virajaskair nabhasvadbhir diśa ucchvasitā iva.

#### <span class="box">10.75</span>

kṛśānur apadhūmatvāt prasannatvāt prabhākaraḥ, rakṣiviprakṛtāv āstām apaviddhaśucāv iva.

#### <span class="box">10.76</span>

daśānanakirīṭebhyas tatkṣaṇaṃ rākṣasaśriyaḥ, maṇivyājena paryastāḥ pṛthivyām aśrubindavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.77</span>

putrajanmapraveśyānāṃ tūryāṇām tasya putriṇaḥ, ārambhaṃ prathamaṃ cakrur devadhundubhayo divi.

#### <span class="box">10.78</span>

saṃtānakamayī vṛṣṭir bhavane cāsya petuṣī, samaṅgalopacārāṇāṃ saivādiracanābhavat.

#### <span class="box">10.79</span>

kumārāḥ kṛtasaṃskārās te dhātristanya pāyinaḥ, ānandenāgrajeneva samaṃ vavṛdhire pituḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.80</span>

svābhāvikaṃ vinītatvaṃ teṣaṃ vinayakarmaṇā, mumūrcha sahajaṃ tejo haviṣeva havirbhujām.

#### <span class="box">10.81</span>

parasparāviruddhās te tad raghor anaghaṃ kulam, alam uddyotayām āsur devāraṇyam ivartavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.82</span>

samāne 'pi hi saubhrātre yathobhau rāmalakṣmaṇau, tathā bharataśatrughnau prītyā dvandvaṃ babhūvatuḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.83</span>

teṣāṃ dvayor dvayor aikyaṃ bibhide na kadācana, yathā vāyuvibhāvasvor yathā candrasamudrayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.84</span>

te prajānāṃ prajānāthās tejasā praśrayeṇa ca, mano jahrur nidāghānte śyāmābhrā divasā iva.

#### <span class="box">10.85</span>

sa caturdhā babhau vyastaḥ prasavaḥ pṛthivīpateḥ, dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇām avatāra ivāṅgabhāk.

#### <span class="box">10.86</span>

guṇair ārādhayām āsus te guruṃ guruvatsalāḥ, tam eva caturnateśaṃ ratnair iva mahārṇavāḥ.

#### <span class="box">10.87</span>

suragaja iva dantair bhagnadaityāsidhārair naya iva paṇabandhavyaktayogair upāyaiḥ, harir iva yugadīrghair dorbhir aṃṣais tadīyaiḥ patir avanipatīnāṃ taiś cakāśe.

#### <span class="box">11.1</span>

kauśikena sa kila kṣitīśvaro rāmam adhvaravighātaśāntaye, kākapakṣadharam etya yācitas tejasāṃ hi na vayaḥ samīkṣyate.

#### <span class="box">11.2</span>

kṛcchralabdham api labdhavarṇabhāk taṃ dideśa munaye salakṣmaṇam, apy asupraṇayināṃ raghoḥ kule na vyahanyata kadācid arthitā.

#### <span class="box">11.3</span>

yāvad ādiśati pārthivas tayor nirgamāya puramārgasatkriyām, tāvad āśu vidadhe marutsakhaiḥ sā sapuṣpajalavarṣibhir ghanaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.4</span>

tau nideśakaraṇodyatau pitur dhanvinau caraṇayor nipetatuḥ, bhūpater api tayoḥ pravatsyator namrayor upari bāṣpabindavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.5</span>

tau pitur nayanajena vāriṇā kiṃcidukṣitaśikhaṇḍakāv ubhau, dhanvinau tam ṛṣim anvagacchatāṃ pauradṛṣṭikṛtamārgatoraṇau.

#### <span class="box">11.6</span>

lakṣmaṇānucaram eva rāghavaṃ netum aicchad ṛṣir ity asau nṛpaḥ, āśiṣaṃ prayuyuje na vāhinīṃ sā hi rakṣaṇavidhau tayoḥ kṣamā.

#### <span class="box">11.6*</span>

rejatuś ca sutarāṃ mahaujasaḥ kauśikasya padavīm anudrutau, uttarāṃ prati diśaṃ vivasvataḥ prasthitasya madhumādhavāv iva.

#### <span class="box">11.7</span>

mātṛvargacaraṇaspṛṣau munes tau prapadya padavīṃ mahaujasaḥ, rejatur gativaśāt pravartinau bhāskarasya madhumādhavāv iva.

#### <span class="box">11.8</span>

vīcilolabhujayos tayor gataṃ śaiśavāc capalam apy aśobhata, toyadāgama ivoddhyabhidyayor nāmadheyasadṛśaṃ viceṣṭitam.

#### <span class="box">11.9</span>

tau balātibalayoḥ prabhāvato vidyayoḥ pathi munipradiṣṭayoḥ, mamlatur na maṇikuṭṭimocitau mātṛpārśvaparivartināv iva.

#### <span class="box">11.10</span>

pūrvavṛttakathitaiḥ purāvidaḥ sānujaḥ pitṛsakhasya rāghavaḥ, uhyamāna iva vāhanocitaḥ pādacāram api na vyabhāvayat.

#### <span class="box">11.11</span>

tau sarāṃsi rasavadbhir ambubhiḥ kūjitaiḥ śrutisukhaiḥ patatriṇaḥ, vāyavaḥ surabhipuṣpareṇubhiś chāyayā ca jaladāḥ siṣevire.

#### <span class="box">11.12</span>

nāmbhasāṃ kamalaśobhināṃ tathā śākhināṃ na ca pariśramacchidām, darśanena laghunā yathā tayoḥ prītim āpur ubhayos tapasvinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.13</span>

sthāṇudagdhavapuṣas tapovanaṃ prāpya dāśarathir āttakārmukaḥ, vigraheṇa madanasya cāruṇā so 'bhavat pratinidhir na karmaṇā.

#### <span class="box">11.14</span>

tau suketusutayā khilīkṛte kauśikād viditaśāpayā pathi, ninyatuḥ sthalaniveśitātaṭanī līlayaiva dhanuṣī adhijyatām.

#### <span class="box">11.15</span>

jyāniniādam atha gṛhṇatī tayoḥ prādurāsa bahūlakṣapā chaviḥ, tāḍakā calakapālakuṇḍalā kālikeva nibiḍā balākinī.

#### <span class="box">11.16</span>

tīvravegadhutamārgavṛkṣayā pretacīvaravasā svanograyā, abhyabhāvi bharatāgrajas tayā vātyayeva pitṛkānanotthayā.

#### <span class="box">11.17</span>

udyataikabhujayaṣṭim āyatīṃ śroṇilambipuruṣāntramekhalām, tāṃ vilokya vanitāvadhe ghṛṇāṃ pattriṇā saha mumoca rāghavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.18</span>

yac cakāra vivaraṃ śilāghane tāḍakorasi sa rāmasāyakaḥ, apraviṣṭaviṣayasya rakṣasāṃ dvāratām agamad antakasya tat.

#### <span class="box">11.19</span>

bāṇabhinnahṛdayā nipetuṣī sā svakānabhuvaṃ na kevalām, viṣṭapatrayaparājayasthirāṃ rāvaṇaśriyam api vyakampayat.

#### <span class="box">11.20</span>

rāmamanmathaśareṇa tāḍitā duḥsahena dṛdaye niśācarī, gandhavadrudhiracandanokṣitā jīviteśavasatiṃ jagāma sā.

#### <span class="box">11.21</span>

nairṛtaghnam atha mantravan muneḥ prāpad astram avadānatoṣitāt, jyotir indhanaipāti bhāskarāt sūryakānta iva tāḍakāntakaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.22</span>

vāmanāśramapadaṃ tataḥ paraṃ pāvanaṃ śruam ṛṣer upeyivān, unmanāḥ prathamajanmaceṣṭitāny asmarann api babhūva rāghavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.23</span>

āsasāda munir ātmanas tataḥ śiṣyavargaparikalpitārhaṇam, baddhapallavapuṭāñjalidrumaṃ darśanonmukha mṛgaṃ tapovanam.

#### <span class="box">11.24</span>

tatra dīkṣitam ṛṣiṃ rakaṣatur vighnato daśarathātmajau śaraiḥ, lokam andhatamasāt kramoditau raśāmibhiḥ śaśidivākarāv iva.

#### <span class="box">11.25</span>

vīkṣya vedim atha raktabindubhir bandhujīvapṛthubhiḥ pradūṣitām, saṃbhramo 'bhavad apoḍhakarmaṇām ṛtvijāṃ cyutavikaṅkatasrucām.

#### <span class="box">11.26</span>

unmukhaḥ sapadi lakṣmaṇāgrajo bāṇam āśrayamukhāt samuddharan, rakṣasāṃ balam apaśyad ambare gṛdhrapakṣapavaneritadhvajam.

#### <span class="box">11.27</span>

tatra yāv adhipatī makhadviṣāṃ tau śaravyam akarot sa netarān, kiṃ mahoragavisarpivikramo rājileṣu garuḍaḥ pravartate.

#### <span class="box">11.28</span>

so 'stram ugrajavam astrakovidaḥ saṃdadhe dhanuṣi vāyudaivatam, tena śailagurum apy apātayat pāṇḍupattram iva tāḍakāsutam.

#### <span class="box">11.29</span>

yaḥ subāhur iti rākṣaso 'paras tatra tatra visasarpa māyayā, taṃ kṣurapraśakalīkṛtām kṛtī pattriṇāṃ vyabhajad āśramād bahiḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.30</span>

ity apāstamakhavighnayos tayoḥ sāṃyugīnam abhinandya vikramam, ṛtvijaḥ kulapater yathākramaṃ vāgyatasya niravartayan kriyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.31</span>

tau praṇāmacalakākapakṣakau bhrātarāv abhṛthāpluto muniḥ, āśiṣām anupadaṃ samaspṛśad darbhapāṭitatalena pāṇinā.

#### <span class="box">11.32</span>

taṃ nyamantrayata saṃbhṛtakratur maithilaḥ sa mighilāṃ vrajan vaśī, rāghavāv api nināya bibhratau taddhanuḥśravaṇajaṃ kutūhalam.

#### <span class="box">11.33</span>

taiḥ śiveṣu vasatir gatādhvabhiḥ sāyam āśramataruṣv agṛhyata, yeṣu dīrghatapasaḥ parigraho vāsavakṣaṇakalatratāṃ yayau.

#### <span class="box">11.34</span>

pratyapadyata cirāya yat punaś cāru gautamavadhūḥ śilāmayī, svaṃ vapuḥ sa kila kilibiṣacchidāṃ rāmapādarajasām anugrahaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.35</span>

rāghavānvitam upasthitaṃ muniṃ taṃ niśamya janako janeśvaraḥ, arthakāmasahitaṃ saparyayā dehabaddham iva dharmam abhyagāt.

#### <span class="box">11.36</span>

tau videhanagarīnivāsināṃ gāṃ gatāv iva divaḥ punarvasū, manyate sma pibatāṃ vilocanaiḥ pakṣmapātam api vañcanāṃ manaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.37</span>

yūpavaty avasite kiryāvidhau kālavit kuśikavaṃśavardhanaḥ, rāmam iṣvasanadarśanotsukaṃ maithilāya kathayāṃ bvabhūva saḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.38</span>

tasya vīkṣya lalitaṃ vapuḥ śiśoḥ pārthivaḥ prathitavaṃśajanmanaḥ, svaṃ vicintya ca dhanur durānamaṃ pīḍito duhiṭśulkasaṃsthayā.

#### <span class="box">11.39</span>

abravīc ca bhagavan mataṅgajair yad bṛhadbhir api karma duṣkaram, tatra nāham anumantum utsahe moghavṛtti kalabhasya ceṣṭitam.

#### <span class="box">11.40</span>

hrepitā hi bahavo nareśvarās tena tāta dhanuṣā dhanurbhṛtaḥ, jyānighātakaṭhinatvaco bhujān svān vidhūya dhig iti pratasthire.

#### <span class="box">11.41</span>

pratyuvāca tam ṛṣir niśamyatāṃ sārato 'yam atha vā kṛtaṃ girā, cāpa eva bhavato bhaviṣyati vyaktaśaktir aśanir girāv iva.

#### <span class="box">11.42</span>

evam āptavacanāt sa pauruṣaṃ kākapakṣakadhare 'pi rāghave, śraddadhe tridaśagopamātrake dāhaśaktim iva kṛṣṇavartmani.

#### <span class="box">11.43</span>

vyādideśa gaṇaḥ sapārśvagān karmukābharaṇāya maithilaḥ, taijasaya dhanuṣaḥ pravṛttaye toyadān iva sahasralocanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.44</span>

tat prasuptabhujagendrabhīṣaṇaṃ vīkṣya dāśarathir ādade dhanuḥ, vidrutakratumṛgānausāriṇaṃ yena bāṇam asṛjad vṛṣadhvajaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.45</span>

ātatajyam akarot sa saṃsadā vismayastimitanetram īkṣitaḥ, śailasāram api nātiyatnataḥ puṣpacāpam iva peśalaṃ smaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.46</span>

bhajyamānam atimātrakarṣaṇāt tena vajraparuṣasvanaṃ dhanuḥ, bhārgavāya dṛḍhamanyave punaḥ kṣatram udyatam iti nyavedayat.

#### <span class="box">11.47</span>

dṛṣṭasāram atha rudrakārmuke vīryaśulkam abhinandya maithilaḥ, rāghavāya tanayām ayonijāṃ rūpiṇīṃ śriyam iva nyavedayat.

#### <span class="box">11.48</span>

maithilaḥ sapadi satyasaṃgaro rāghavāya tanayām ayonijāṃ, saṃnidhau dyutimatas taponidher agnisākṣika ivātisṛṣṭavān.

#### <span class="box">11.49</span>

prāhiṇoc ca mahitaṃ mahādyutiḥ kosalādhipataye purodhasam, bhṛtyabhāvi duhituḥ parigrahād diśyatāṃ kulam idaṃ nimer iti.

#### <span class="box">11.49*</span>

utsukaś ca sutadārakarmaṇā so 'bhavad gurur upāgataś ca tam, gautamasya tanayo 'nukūlavāk prārthitaṃ hi sukṛtām akālahṛt.

#### <span class="box">11.50</span>

anviyeṣa sadṛśīṃ sa ca snuṣāṃ prāpa cainam anukūlavāg dvijaḥ, sadya eva sukṛtāṃ hi pacyate kalpavṛkṣaphala dharmi kāṅkṣitam.

#### <span class="box">11.51</span>

tasya kalpitapuraskriyāvidheḥ śuśruvān vacanam agrajanmanaḥ, uccacāla valabhitasakho vaśī sainyareṇumuṣitārkadīdhitiḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.52</span>

āsasāda mithilāṃ sa veṣṭayan piḍitopavanapādapāṃ balaiḥ, prītirodham asahiṣṭa sā purī strīva kāntaparibhogam āyatam.

#### <span class="box">11.53</span>

tau sametya samayasthitāv ubhau bhūpatī varuṇavāsavopamau, kanyakātanayakautukakriyāṃ svaprabhāvasadṛśīṃ vitenatuḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.54</span>

pārthivīm udavahad raghūdvaho lakṣmaṇas tadanujām athormilām, yau tayor avarajau varaujasau tau kuśadhvajasute sumadhyame.

#### <span class="box">11.55</span>

te caturthasahitās trayo babhuḥ sūnavo navavadhūparigrahāḥ, sāmadānavidhibhedavigrahāḥ siddhimanta iva tasya bhūpateḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.56</span>

tā narādhipasutā nṛpātmajais te ca tābhir agaman kṛtārthatām, so 'bhavad varavadhūsamāgamaḥ pratyayaprakṛtiyogsaṃnibhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.57</span>

evam āttaratir ātmasaṃbhavāṃs tān niveśya caturo 'pi tatra saḥ, adhvasu triṣu visṛṣṭamaithilaḥ svāṃ purīṃ daśaratho nyavartata.

#### <span class="box">11.58</span>

tasya jātu marutaḥ pratīpagā vartmasu dhavjatarupramāthinaḥ, cikliśur bhṛśatayā varūthinīm uttaṭā iva nadīrayāḥ sthalīm.

#### <span class="box">11.59</span>

lakṣyate sma tadanantaraṃ ravir baddhabhīmapairveṣamaṇḍalaḥ, vainateyaśamitasya bhogino bhogaveṣṭita iva cyuto maṇiḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.60</span>

śyenapakṣaparidhūsarālakāḥ sāṃdhyamegharudhirārdravāsasaḥ, aṅganā iva rajasvalā diśo no babhūvur avalokanakṣamāḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.61</span>

bhāskaraś ca diśam adhyuvāsa yāṃ tāṃ śritāḥ pratibhayaṃ vavāśire, kṣatraśoṇitapitṛkriyocitaṃ codayantya iva bhārgavaṃ śivāḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.62</span>

tat pratīpapavanādi vaikṛtaṃ prekṣya śāntim adhikṛtya kṛtyavit  / , anvayuṅkta gurum īśvaraḥ kṣiteḥ svantam ity alaghayat sa tadvyathām.

#### <span class="box">11.63</span>

tejasaḥ sapadi rāśir utthitaḥ prādurāsa kila vāhinīmukhe, yaḥ pramṛjya nayanāni sainikair lakṣaṇīyapuruṣākṛtiś cirāt.

#### <span class="box">11.64</span>

pitryam aṃśam upavītalakṣaṇaṃ mātṛkaṃ ca dhanur ūrjitaṃ dadhat, yaḥ sasoma iva gharmadīdhitiḥ sadvijihva iva candanadrumaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.65</span>

yena roṣaparuṣātmanaḥ pituḥ śāsane sthibhido 'pi tasthuṣā, vepamānajananīśiraśchidā prāg ajīyata ghṛṇā tato mahī.

#### <span class="box">11.66</span>

akṣabhījavalayena nibabhau dakṣiṇaśravaṇasaṃsthitena yaḥ, kṣatriyāntakaraṇaikaviṃśater vyājapūrvagaṇanām ivodvahan.

#### <span class="box">11.67</span>

taṃ pitur vadhabhavena manyunā rājavaṃśanidhanāya dīkṣitam, bālasūnur avalokya bhārgavaṃ svāṃ daśāṃ ca viṣasāda pārthivaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.68</span>

rāmanāma iti tulyam ātmaje vartamānam ahite ca dāruṇe, hṛdyam asya bhayadāyi cābhavad ratnajātam iva hārasarpayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.69</span>

arghyam arghyam iti vādinaṃ nṛpaṃ so 'navekṣya bharatāgrajo yataḥ, kṣatrakopadahanārciṣaṃ tataḥ saṃdadhe dṛśam udagratārakām.

#### <span class="box">11.70</span>

tena kārmukaniṣaktamuṣṭinā rāghavo vigatabhīḥ purogataḥ, aṅgulīvivaracāriṇaṃ śaraṃ kurvatā nijagade yuyutsunā.

#### <span class="box">11.71</span>

kṣatrajātam apakāri vairi me tan nihatya bahuśaḥ śamaṃ gataḥ, suptasarpa iva daṇḍaghaṭṭanād roṣito 'smi tava vikramaśravāt.

#### <span class="box">11.72</span>

maithilasya dhanur anyapārthivais tvaṃ kilānamitapūrvam akṣaṇoḥ, tan niśamya bahavatā samarthaye vīryaśṛṅgam iva bhagnam ātmanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.73</span>

anyadā jagati rāma ity ayaṃ śabda uccarita eva mām agāt, vrīḍam āvahati me sa saṃprati vyastavṛttir udayonmukhe tvayi.

#### <span class="box">11.74</span>

bibhrato 'stram acale 'py akuṇṭhitaṃ dvau matau mama ripū samāgasau, homa-dhenu-haraṇāc ca haihayas tvaṃ ca irtim apahartum udyataḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.75</span>

kṣatriyāntakaraṇo 'pi vikramas tena mām avati nājite tvayi, pāvakasya mahimā sa gaṇyate kakṣavaj jvalati sāgare 'pi yaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.76</span>

viddhi cāttabalam ojasā harer aiśvaraṃ dhanur abhāji yat tvayā, khātamūlam anilo nadīrayaiḥ pātayaty api mṛdus taṭadrumam.

#### <span class="box">11.77</span>

tan madīyam idam āyudhaṃ jyayā saṃgamayya saśaraṃ vikṛṣyatām, tiṣṭhatu pradhanam evam apy ahaṃ tulyabāhutarasā jitas tvayā.

#### <span class="box">11.78</span>

kātaro 'si yadi vodgatārciṣā tarjitaḥ paraśudhārayā mama, jyānighātakaṭhināṅgulir vṛthā badhyatām abhayayācanāñjaliḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.79</span>

evam uktavati bhīmadarśane bhārgave smitavikampitādharaḥ, taddhanurgrahaṇam eva rāghavaḥ pratyapadyata samartham uttaram.

#### <span class="box">11.80</span>

pūrvajanmadhanuṣā samāgataḥ so 'timātralaghudarśano 'bhavat, kevalo 'pi subhago navāmbudaḥ kiṃ punas tridaśacāpalāñchitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.81</span>

tena bhūminihitaikakoṭi tat kārmukaṃ ca balinādhiropitam, niṣprabhaś ca ripur āsa bhūbhṛtāṃ dhūmaśeṣa iva dhūmaketanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.82</span>

tāv ubhāv api paraspara-sthitau vardhamānaparihīnatejasau, paśyati sma janatā dinātyaye pārvaṇau śaśidivākarāv iva.
#### <span class="box">11.83</span>

taṃ kṛpāmṛdur avekṣya bhārgavaṃ rāghavaḥ skhalitavīryam ātmani, svaṃ ca saṃhitam amogham āśugaṃ vyājahāra harasūnasaṃnibhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.84</span>

na prahartum alam asmi nidayaṃ vipra ity abhibhavaty api tvayi, śaṃṣa kiṃ gatim anena pattriṇā hanmi lokam uta te makhārjitam.

#### <span class="box">11.85</span>

pratyuvāca tam ṛṣir na tattvatas tvāṃ na vedmi puruṣaṃ purātanam, gāṃ gatasya tava dhāma vaiṣṇavaṃ kopito hy asi mayā didṛkṣuṇā.

#### <span class="box">11.86</span>

bhasmasāt kṛtavataḥ pitṛdviṣaḥ pātrasāc ca vasudhāṃ sasāgarām, āhito jayaviparyayo 'pi me ślāghya eva parameṣṭhinā tvayā.

#### <span class="box">11.87</span>

tad gatiṃ matimatāṃ varepsitāṃ puṇyatīrthagamanāya rakṣa me, pīḍayiṣyati na māṃ khilīkṛtā svargapaddhatir abhogalolupam.

#### <span class="box">11.88</span>

pratyapadyata tatheti rāghavaḥ prāṅmukhaś ca visasarja sāyakam, bhārgavasya sukṛto 'pi so 'bhavat svargamārgaparigho duratyayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.89</span>

rāghavo 'pi caraṇau taponidheḥ kṣamyatām iti vadan samaspṛṣat, nirjiteṣu tarasā tarasvināṃ śatruṣu praṇatir eva kīrtaye.

#### <span class="box">11.90</span>

rājasatvam avadhūya mātṛkaṃ pitryam asmi gamitaḥ śamaṃ yadā, nanv aninditaphalo mama tvayā nigraho 'py ayam anugrahīkṛtaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.91</span>

sādhu yāmy aham avighnam astu te devakāryam upapādayiṣyataḥ, ūcivān iti vacaḥ salakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajam ṛṣis tirodadhe.

#### <span class="box">11.91*</span>

svaṃ niveśya kila dhāma rāghave vaiṣṇavaṃ viditaviṣṇutejasi, svastidānam adhikṛtya cākṣayaṃ bhārgavo 'tha nijam āśramaṃ yayau.

#### <span class="box">11.92</span>

tasmin gate vijayinaṃ parirabhya rāmaṃ snehād amanyata pitā punar eva jātam, tasyābhavat kṣaṇaśucaḥ paritoṣalābhaḥ kakṣāgnilaṅghitataror iva vṛṣṭipātaḥ.

#### <span class="box">11.93</span>

atha pathi gamayitvā kḷparamyopakārye katicid avanipālaḥ śarvarīḥ śarvakalpah, puram aviśad ayodhyāṃ maithilīdarśanīnāṃ kuvalayitagavākṣāṃ locanair aṅganānām.

#### <span class="box">12.1</span>

nirviṣṭaviṣayasnehaḥ sa daśāntam upeyivān, āsīd āsannanirvāṇaḥ pradīpārcir ivoṣasi.

#### <span class="box">12.2</span>

taṃ karṇamūlam āgatya rāme śrīr nasyatām iti, kaikeyīśaṅkayevāha palitacchadmanā jarā.

#### <span class="box">12.3</span>

sā paurān paurakāntasya rāmasyābhyudayaśrutiḥ, pratyekaṃ hlādayāṃ cakre kulyevodyānapādapān.

#### <span class="box">12.4</span>

tasyābhiṣekasaṃbhāraṃ kalpitaṃ krūraniścayā, dūṣayām āsa kaikeyī śokoṣṇaiḥ pārthivāśrubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.5</span>

sā kilāśvāsitā caṇḍī bhartrā tatsaṃśrutau varau, udvavāmendrasiktā bhūr bilamagnāv ivoragau.

#### <span class="box">12.6</span>

tayoś caturdaśaikena rāmaṃ prāvrājayat samāḥ, dvitīyena sutasyaicchad vaidhavyaikaphalāṃ śriyam.

#### <span class="box">12.7</span>

pitrā dattāṃ rudan rāmaḥ prāṅ mahīṃ pratyapadyata, paścād vanāya gaccheti tadājñāṃ mudito 'grahīt.

#### <span class="box">12.8</span>

dadhato maṅgalakṣaume vasānasya ca valkale, dadṛśur vismitās tasya mukharāgaṃ samaṃ janāḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.9</span>

sa sītālakṣmaṇasakhaḥ satyād gurum alopayan, viveśa daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ pratyekaṃ ca satāṃ manaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.10</span>

rājāpi tadviyogārtaḥ smṛtvā śāpaṃ svakarmajam, śarīratyāgamātreṇa śuddhilābham amanyata.

#### <span class="box">12.11</span>

viproṣitakumāraṃ tad (?) rājyam astamiteśvaram, randhrānveṣaṇadakṣāṇāṃ dviṣām āmiṣatāṃ yayau.

#### <span class="box">12.12</span>

athānāthāḥ prakṛtayo mātṛbandhunivāsinam, maulair ānāyayām āsur bhartaṃ stambhitāśrubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.13</span>

śrutvā tathāvidhaṃ mṛtyuṃ kaikeyītanayaḥ pituḥ, mātur na kevalaṃ svasyāḥ śriyo 'py āsīt parāṅmukhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.14</span>

sasainyaś cānvagād rāmaṃ darśitān āśramālayaiḥ, tasya paśyan sasaumitrer udaśrur vasatidrumān.

#### <span class="box">12.15</span>

citrakūṭavanasthaṃ ca kathitasvargatir guroḥ, lakṣmyā nimantrayāṃ cakre tam anucchiṣṭasaṃpadā.

#### <span class="box">12.16</span>

sa hi prathamaje tasminn akṛtaśrīparigrahe, parivettāram ātmānaṃ mene svīkaraṇād bhuvaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.17</span>

tam aśakyam apākraṣṭuṃ nirdeśāt svargiṇaḥ pituḥ, yayāce pāduke paścāt kartuṃ rājyādhidevate.

#### <span class="box">12.18</span>

sa visṛṣṭas tathety uktvā bhrātrā naivāviśat purīm, nandigrāmagatas tasya rājyaṃ nyāsam ivābhunak.

#### <span class="box">12.19</span>

dṛḍhabhaktir iti jyeṣṭhe rājyatṛṣṇāparāṅmukhaḥ, mātuḥ pāpasya śuddhyarthaṃ prāyaścittam ivākarot.

#### <span class="box">12.20</span>

rāmo 'pi saha vaidehyā vane vanyena vartayan, cacāra sānujaḥ śānto vṛddhekṣvākuvrataṃ yuvā.

#### <span class="box">12.21</span>

prabhāvastambhitacchāyam āśritaḥ sa vanaspatim, kadācid aṅke sītāyāḥ śiśye kiṃcid iva śramāt.

#### <span class="box">12.22</span>

aindriḥ kila nakhais tasyā vidadāra stanau dvijaḥ, priyopabhogacihneṣu paurobhāgyam ivācaran.

#### <span class="box">12.22*</span>

mṛgamāṃsaṃ tataḥ sītāṃ rakṣantīm ātape dhṛtam, pakṣatuṇḍanakhāghātair babādhe vāyaso balāt.

#### <span class="box">12.23</span>

tasminn āsthad iṣīkāstraṃ rāmo rāmāvabhodhitaḥ, ātmānaṃ mumuce tasmād ekanetravyayena saḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.24</span>

rāmas tv āsannadeśatvād bharatāgamanaṃ punaḥ, āśaṅkyotsukasāraṅgāṃ citrakūṭasthalīṃ jahau.

#### <span class="box">12.25</span>

prayayāv ātitheyeṣu vasann ṛṣikuleṣu saḥ, dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ṛkṣeṣu vārṣikeṣv iva bhāskaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.26</span>

babhau tam anugacchantī videhādhipateḥ sutā, pratiṣiddhāpi kaikeyyā lakṣmīr iva guṇonmukhī.

#### <span class="box">12.27</span>

anusūyātisṛṣṭena puṇyagandhena kānanam, sā cakārāṅgarāgeṇa puṣpoccalita ṣaṭpadam.

#### <span class="box">12.28</span>

saṃdhyābhrakapiṣas tatra virādho nāma rākṣasaḥ, atiṣṭhan mārgam āvṛtya rāmasyendor iva grahaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.29</span>

sa jaharā tayor madhye maithilīṃ lokaśoṣaṇaḥ, nabhonabhasyayor vṛṣṭim avagraha ivāntare.

#### <span class="box">12.30</span>

taṃ viniṣpiṣya kākutsthau purā dūṣayati shtalīm, gandhenāśucinā ceti vasudhāyāṃ nicakhnatuḥ.
#### <span class="box">12.31</span>

pañcavaṭyāṃ tato rāmaḥ śāsanāt kumbhajanmanaḥ, anapoṣhasthitis tasthau vindhyādriḥ prakṛtāv iva.

#### <span class="box">12.32</span>

rāvaṇāvarajā tatra rāghavaṃ madanāturā, abhipede nidāghārtā vyālīva malayadrumam.

#### <span class="box">12.33</span>

sā sītāsaṃnidhāv eva taṃ vavre kathitānvayā, atyārūḍho hi nārīṇām akālajño maobhavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.34</span>

kalatravān ahaṃ bāle kanīyāṃsaṃ bhajasva me, iti rāmo vṛṣasyantīṃ vṛṣaskandhaḥ śaśāsa tām.

#### <span class="box">12.35</span>

jyeṣṭhābhigamanāt pūrvaṃ tenāpy anabhinanditā, sābhūd rāmāśrayā bhūyo nadīvobhayakūlabhāk.

#### <span class="box">12.36</span>

saṃrambhaṃ maithilīhāsaḥ kṣaṇaṃ saumyāṃ nināya tām, nivātastimitāṃ velāṃ candrodaya ivodadheḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.37</span>

phalam asyopahāsasya sadyaḥ prāpsyasi paśya mām, mṛgyaḥ paribhavo vyāghryām ity avehi tvayā kṛtam.

#### <span class="box">12.38</span>

ity uktvā maithilīṃ bhartur aṅke nirviśatīṃ bhayāt, rūpaṃ śūrpaṇakhā-nāmnaḥ sadṛśaṃ pratyapadyata.

#### <span class="box">12.39</span>

lakṣmaṇaḥ prathamaṃ śrutvā kokilāmañjubhāṣiṇīm, śivāghorasvanāṃ paścād bubudhe vikṛteti tām.

#### <span class="box">12.40</span>

parṇaśālām atha kṣipraṃ vidhṛtāsiḥ praviśya saḥ, vairūpyapaunaruktyena bhīṣaṇāṃ tām ayojayat.

#### <span class="box">12.41</span>

sā vakranakhadhāriṇyā veṇukarkaśaparvayā, aṅkuśākārayāṅgulyā tāv atarjayad ambare.

#### <span class="box">12.42</span>

prāpya cāśu jansthānaṃ kharādibhyas tathāvidham, rāmopakramam ācakhyau rakṣaḥparibhavaṃ navam.

#### <span class="box">12.43</span>

mukhāvayavalūṇāṃ tāṃ nairṛtā yat purodadhuḥ, rāmābhiyāyināṃ teṣāṃ tad evābhūd amaṅgalam.

#### <span class="box">12.44</span>

udāyudhān āpatatas tān dṛptān prekṣya rāghavaḥ, nidadhe vijayāśaṃsāṃ cāpe sītāṃ ca lakṣmaṇe.

#### <span class="box">12.45</span>

eko dāśarathī rāmo yātudhānāḥ sahasraśaḥ, te tu yāvanta evājau tāvāṃś ca dadṛśe sa taiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.46</span>

asajjanena kākutsthaḥ prayuktam atha dūṣaṇam, na cakṣame śubhācāraḥ sa dūṣaṇam ivātmanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.47</span>

taṃ śaraiḥ pratijagrāha kharatiśirasau ca saḥ, khramaśas te punas tasya cāpāt samam ivodyayuḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.48</span>

tais trayāṇāṃ śitair bāṇair yathāpūrvaviśuddhibhiḥ, āyur dehātigaiḥ pītaṃ rudhiraṃ tu patatribhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.49</span>

tasmin rāmaśarotkṛtte bale mahati rakṣasām, utthitaṃ dadṛśe 'nyac ca kabandhebhyo na kiṃcana.

#### <span class="box">12.50</span>

sā bāṇavarṣiṇaṃ rāmaṃ yodhayitvā suradviṣām, aprabodhāya suṣvāpa gṛdhracchāye varūthinī.

#### <span class="box">12.51</span>

rāghavāstravidīrṇānāṃ rāvaṇaṃ prati rakṣasām, teṣāṃ śūrpaṇakhaivaikā duṣpratvṛttiharābhavat.

#### <span class="box">12.52</span>

nigrahāt svasur āptānāṃ vadhāc ca dhanadānujaḥ, rāmeṇa nihataṃ mene padaṃ daśasu mūrdhasu.

#### <span class="box">12.53</span>

rakṣasā mṛgarūpeṇa vañcayitvā sa rāghavau, jaharā sītāṃ pakṣīndraprayāsakṣaṇavighnitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.54</span>

tau sītānveṣiṇau gṛdhraṃ lūnapakṣam apaśyatām, prāṇair daśarathaprīter anṛṇaṃ kaṇṭhavartibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.55</span>

sa rāvaṇahṛtāṃ tābhyāṃ vacasācaṣṭa maithilīm, ātmanaḥ sumahat karma vraṇair āvedya saṃsthitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.56</span>

tayos rāvaṇahṛtāṃ tābhyāṃ pitṛvyāpattiśokayoḥ, pitarīvāgnisaṃskārāt parā vavṛtire kriyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.57</span>

vadhanirdhūtaśāpasya kabandhasyopadeśataḥ, mumūrcha sakhyaṃ rāmasya samānavyasane harau.

#### <span class="box">12.58</span>

sa hatvā vālinaṃ vīras tatpade cirakāṅkṣite, dhātoḥ sthāna ivādeśaṃ sugrīvaṃ saṃnyaveśayat.

#### <span class="box">12.59</span>

itas tataś ca vaidehīm anveṣṭuṃ bhartṛcoditāḥ, kapayaś cerur ārtasya rāmasyeva manorathāḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.60</span>

pravṛttāv upalabdhāyāṃ tasyāḥ saṃpātidarśanāt, mārutiḥ sāgaraṃ tīrṇaḥ saṃsāram iva nirmamaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.61</span>

dṛṣṭā vicinvatā tena laṅkāyāṃ rākṣasīvṛtā, jānakī viṣavallībhiḥ parīteva mahauṣadhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.62</span>

tasyai bhartur abhijñāmam aṅgulīyaṃ dadau kapiḥ, pratyudgatam ivānuṣṇais tadānandāśrubhindubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.63</span>

nirvāpya priyasaṃdeśaiḥ sītām akṣavadhoddhataḥ, sa dadāha purīṃ laṅkāṃ kṣaṇasoḍhārinigrahaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.64</span>

pratyabhijñānaratnaṃ ca rāmāyādarśayat kṛtī, hṛdayaṃ svayam āyātaṃ vaidehyā iva mūrtimat.

#### <span class="box">12.65</span>

sa prāpa hṛdayanyastamaṇiparśanimīlitaḥ, apayodharasaṃsargaṃ priyāliṅgananirvṛtim.

#### <span class="box">12.66</span>

śrutvā rāmaḥ priyodantaṃ mene tatsaṃgamotsukaḥ, mahārṇavaparikṣepaṃ laṅkāyāḥ parikhālaghum.

#### <span class="box">12.67</span>

sa pratasthe 'rināśāya harisainyair anudrutaḥ, na kevalaṃ dharā-pṛṣṭhe vyomni saṃbādhavartibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.68</span>

nirviṣṭam udadheḥ kūle taṃ prapede vibhīṣaṇaḥ, snehād rākṣasalakṣmyeva buddhim ādiśya coditaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.69</span>

tasmai niśācaraiśvaryaṃ pratiśuśrāva rāghavaḥ, kāle khalu samārabdhāḥ phalaṃ badhnanti nītayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.70</span>

sa setuṃ bandhayām āsa plavagair lavaṇāmbhasi, rasātalād ivonmagnaṃ śeṣaṃ svapnāya śārṅgiṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.71</span>

tenottīrya pathā laṅkāṃ rodhayām āsa piṅgalaiḥ, dvitīyaṃ hemaprākāraṃ kurvadbhir iva vānaraiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.72</span>

raṇaḥ pravavṛte tatra bhīmaḥ plavagarakṣasām, digvijṛmbhitakākutsthapaulastyajayaghoṣaṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.73</span>

pādapāviddhaparighaḥ śilāniṣpiṣṭamudgaraḥ, atiśastranakhanyāsaḥ śailarugṇa mataṅgajaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.74</span>

atha rāmaśiraśchedadarśanodbhrāntacetanām, sītāṃ māyeti śaṃsantī trijaṭā samajīvayat.

#### <span class="box">12.75</span>

kāmaṃ jīvati me nātha iti sā vijahau śucam, prāṅ matvā satyam asyāntaṃ jīvitāsmīti lajjitā.

#### <span class="box">12.76</span>

garuḍāpātaviśliṣṭameghanādāstrabandhanaḥ, dāśarathyoḥ kṣaṇakleśaḥ svapnavṛtta ivābhavat.

#### <span class="box">12.77</span>

tato bibheda paulastyaḥ śaktyā vakṣasi lakṣmaṇam, rāmas tv anāhato 'py āsīd vidīrṇahṛdayaḥ śucā.

#### <span class="box">12.78</span>

sa mārutisamānītamahauṣadhihatavyathaḥ, laṅkāstrīṇāṃ punaś cakre vilāpācāryakaṃ śaraiḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.79</span>

sa nādaṃ meghanādasya dhanuś cendrāyudhaprabham, meghasyeva śaratkālo na kiṃcit paryaśeṣayat.

#### <span class="box">12.79A</span>

kleśena mahatā nidrāṃ tyājitaṃ raṇadurjayam, rāvaṇaḥ preṣayām āsa yuddhāyānujam ātmanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.79B</span>

jaghāna sa tadādeśāt kapīn ugrān anekaśaḥ, viveśa ca purīṃ laṅkāṃ samādāya harīśvaram.

#### <span class="box">12.80</span>

kumbhakarṇaḥ kapīndreṇa tulyāvasthaḥ svasuḥ kṛtaḥ, rurodha rāmaṃ śṛṅgīva ṭaṅkacchinnamanaḥśilaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.81</span>

akāle bodhito bhrātrā priyasvapno vṛthā bhavān, rāmeṣubhir itīvāsau dīrghanidrāṃ praveśitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.82</span>

itarāṇy api rakṣāṃsi petur vānarakoṭiṣu, rajāṃsi samarotthāni racchoṇitanandīṣv iva.

#### <span class="box">12.83</span>

niryayāv atha paulasthyaḥ punar yuddhāya mandirāt, arāvaṇam arāmaṃ vā jagad adyeti niścitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.84</span>

rāmaṃ padātim ālokya laṅkeṣaṃ ca varūthinam, hariyugyaṃ rathaṃ tasmai parjighāya puraṃdaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.85</span>

tam ādhūtadvajapaṭaṃ vyomagaṅgormivāyubhiḥ, devasūtabhujālambī jaitram adhyāsta rāghavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.86</span>

mātalis tasya māhendram āmumoca tanucchadam, yatrotpaladadalaklaibyam astrāṇy āpuḥ suradviṣām.

#### <span class="box">12.87</span>

anyonyadarśanaprāptavikramāvasaraṃ cirāt, rāmarāvaṇayor yuddhaṃ caritārtham ivābhavat.

#### <span class="box">12.88</span>

bhujamūrdhorubāhulyād eko 'pi dhandānujaḥ, dadṛśe so 'yathāpūrvo mātṛvaṃśa iva sthitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">12.89</span>

jetāraṃ lokapālānāṃ svamukhair arciteśvaram, rāmas tulitakailāsam arātiṃ bahv amanyata.

#### <span class="box">12.90</span>

tasya sphurati paulastyah sītāsaṃgamaśaṃsini, nicakhānādhikakrodhaḥ śaraṃ savyetare bhuje.

#### <span class="box">12.91</span>

rāvaṇasyāpi rāmāsto bhittvā hṛdayam āśugaḥ, viveśa bhuvam ākhyātum uragebhya iva priyam.

#### <span class="box">12.92</span>

vacasaiva tayor vākyam astram astreṇa nighnatoḥ, anyonyajayasaṃrambho vavṛdhe vādinor iva.

#### <span class="box">12.93</span>

vikramavyatihāreṇa astram astreṇa nighnatoḥ, jayaśrīr antarā vedir mattavāraṇayor iva.

#### <span class="box">12.94</span>

kṛtapratikṛtaprītais tayor muktāṃ surāsuraiḥ, parasparaṃ śaravrātāḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ na sehire.
