#### <span class="box">12.95</span>

ayaḥśaṅkucitāṃ rakṣaḥ śataghnīm atha śatrave, hṛtāṃ vaivasvatasyeva kūṭaśālmalim akṣipat.

#### <span class="box">12.96</span>

rāghavo ratham aprāptāṃ tām āśāṃ ca suradviṣām, ardhacandramukhair bāṇaiś ciccheda kadalīsukham.

#### <span class="box">12.97</span>

amoghaṃ saṃdadhe cāsmai dhanuṣy akeadhnurdharaḥ, brāhmam astraṃ priyāśokaśalyaniṣkarṣaṇauṣadham.

#### <span class="box">12.98</span>

tad vyomni daśadhā bhinnaṃ dadṛśe dīptimanmukham, vapur mahoragasyeva karālaphaṇamaṇḍalam.

#### <span class="box">12.99</span>

tena mantraprayuktena nimeṣārdhād apātayat, sa rāvaṇaśiraḥpaṅktim ajñātavraṇavedanām.

#### <span class="box">12.100</span>

bālārkapratimevāpsu vīcibhinnā patiṣyataḥ, rarāja rakṣaḥkāyasya kaṇṭhacchedapraṃparā.

#### <span class="box">12.101</span>

marutāṃ paśyatāṃ tasya śirāṃsi patitāny api, mano nātiviśaśvāsa punaḥ saṃdhānaśaṅkinām.

#### <span class="box">12.102</span>

atha madagurupakṣair lokapāladvipānām anugatam alivṛndair gaṇḍabhittīr vihāya, upanatamaṇibandhe mūrdhni paulastyaśatroḥ surabhi suravimuktaṃ puṣpavarṣaṃ papāta.

#### <span class="box">12.103</span>

yantā hareḥ sapadi saṃhṛtakārmukajyam āpṛcchya rāghavam anuṣṭhitadevakāryam, nāmāṅkarāvaṇaśarāṅkitaketuyaṣṭim ūrdhvaṃ rathaṃ harisahasrayujaṃ nināya.

#### <span class="box">12.104</span>

raghupatir api jātavedoviśuddhāṃ pragṛhya priyāṃ priyasuhṛdi vibhīṣaṇe saṃgamayya śriyaṃ vairiṇaḥ, ravisutasahitena tenānuyātaḥ sasaumitriṇā bhujavijitavimānaratnādhirūḍhaḥ pratasthe purīm.

#### <span class="box">13.1</span>

athāmanaḥ śabdaguṇaṃ guṇajñaḥ padaṃ vimānena vigāhamānaḥ, ratnākaraṃ vīkṣya mithaḥ sa jāyāṃ rāmābhidhāno harir ity uvāca.

#### <span class="box">13.2</span>

vaidehi paśy' ā malayād vibhaktaṃ matsetunā phenilam amburāśim, chāyāpatheneva śaratprasannam ākāśam āviṣkṛtacārutāram.

#### <span class="box">13.3</span>

guror yiyakṣoḥ kapilena medhye rasātalaṃ saṃkramite turaṃge, tadartham urvīm avadārayadbhiḥ pūrvaiḥ kilāyaṃ parivardhito naḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.4</span>

garbhaṃ dadhaty arkamarīcayo 'smād vivṛddhim atrāśnuvate vasūni, abindhanaṃ vahnim asau bibharti prahlādanaṃ jyotir ajany anena.

#### <span class="box">13.5</span>

tāṃ tām avasthāṃ pratipadyamānaṃ sthitaṃ daśa vyāpya diśo mahimnā, viṣṇor ivāsyānavadhāraṇīyam īdṛktayā rūpam iyattayā vā.

#### <span class="box">13.6</span>

nābhiprarūḍhāmburuhāsanena saṃstūyamānaḥ prathamena dhātrā, amuṃ yugāntocitayogandiraḥ saṃhṛtya lokān puruṣo 'dhiśete.

#### <span class="box">13.7</span>

pakṣacchidā gotrabhidāttagandhāḥ śaraṇyam enaṃ śataśo mahīdhrāḥ, nṛpā ivopaplavinaḥ parebhyo dharmottaraṃ madhyamam āśrayante.

#### <span class="box">13.8</span>

rasātalād ādibhavena puṃsā bhuvaḥ prayuktodvahanakriyāyāḥ, asyāccham ambhaḥ pralayapravṛddhaṃ muhūrtavaktrāvaraṇaṃ babhūva.

#### <span class="box">13.9</span>

mukhārpaṇeṣu prakṛtipragalbhāḥ svayaṃ taraṅgādharadānadakṣaḥ, ananyasāmānyakalatravṛttiḥ pibaty asau pāyayate ca sindhūḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.10</span>

sasattvam ādāya nadīmukhāmbhaḥ saṃmīlayanto vivṛtānanatvāt, amī śirobhis timayaḥ sarandhrair ūrdhvaṃ vitanvanti jalapravāhān.

#### <span class="box">13.11</span>

mātaṅganakraiḥ sahasotpatadbhir bhinnān dvidhā paśya samudraphenān, kapolasaṃsarpitayā ya eṣāṃ vrajanti karṇa kṣaṇacāmaratvam.

#### <span class="box">13.12</span>

velānilāya prasṛtā bhujaṃgā mahormivisphūrjathunirviśeṣāḥ, sūryāṃśusaṃparkasamṛddharāgair vyajyanta ete maṇibhiḥ phaṇasthaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.13</span>

tavādharasparadhiṣu vidrumeṣu paryastam etat sahasormivegāt, ūrdhvāṅkuraprotamukhaṃ kathaṃcit kleśad apakrāmati śaṅkhayūtham.

#### <span class="box">13.14</span>

pravṛttamātreṇa payāṃsi pātum āvartavegād bhramatā ghanena, ābhāti bhūyiṣṭham ayaṃ samudraḥ pramathyamāno giriṇeva bhūyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.15</span>

dūrād ayaścakranibhasya tanvī tamālatālīvanarājinīlā, ābhāti velā lavaṇāmburāśer dhārānibaddheva kalaṅkalekhā.

#### <span class="box">13.16</span>

velānilaḥ ketakareṇubhis te saṃbhāvayaty ānanam āyatākṣi, mām akṣamaṃ maṇḍanakālahāner vettīva bimbādharabaddhatṛṣṇam.

#### <span class="box">13.17</span>

ete vayaṃ saikatabhinnaśuktiparyastamuktāpaṭalaṃ payodheḥ, prāptā muhūrtena vimānavegāt kūlaṃ phalāvarjitapūgamālam.

#### <span class="box">13.18</span>

kuruṣva tāvat karabhoru paścānmārge mṛgaprekṣiṇi dṛṣtipātam, eṣā vidūrībhavataḥ samudrāt sakānanā niṣpatatīva bhūmiḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.19</span>

kvacit pathā saṃcarate surāṇāṃ kvacid ghanānāṃ patatāṃ kvacic ca, yathāvidho me manso 'bhilāṣaḥ pravartate paśya tathā vimānam.

#### <span class="box">13.20</span>

asau mahendradvipadānagandhī trimārgagāvīcivimardaśītaḥ, ākāśavāyur dinayauvanotthān ācāmati svedalavān mukhe te.

#### <span class="box">13.21</span>

kareṇa vātāyanalambitena spṛṣṭas tvayā caṇḍi kutūhalinyā, āmuñcatīvābharaṇaṃ dvitīyam udbhinnavidyudvalayo ghanas te.

#### <span class="box">13.22</span>

amī janasthānam apoḍhavighnaṃ matvā samārabdhanavoṭajāni, adhyāsate cīrabhṛto yathāsvaṃ cirojjhitāny āśramamaṇḍalāni.

#### <span class="box">13.23</span>

saiṣā sthalī yatra vicinvatā tvāṃ bhraṣṭaṃ mayā nūpuram ekam urvyām, adṛśyata tvaccaraṇāravindaviśleṣaduḥkhād iva baddhamaunam.

#### <span class="box">13.24</span>

tvaṃ rakṣasā bhīru yato 'panītā taṃ mārgam etāḥ kṛpayā latā me, adarśayan vaktum aśaknuvatyaḥ śākhābhir āvarjitapallavābhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.25</span>

mṛgyaś ca darbhāṅkuranirvyapekṣās tavāgatijñaṃ samabodhayan mām, vyāpārayantyo diśi dakṣiṇasyām utpakṣmarājīni vilocanāni.

#### <span class="box">13.26</span>

etad girer mālayavataḥ purastād āvirbhavaty ambarlekhi śṛṅgam, navaṃ yatra ghanair mayā ca tvadviprayogāśru samaṃ visṛṣṭam.

#### <span class="box">13.27</span>

gandhaś ca dhārāhatapalvalānāṃ kādambam ardhodgatakesaraṃ ca, snigdhāś ca kekāḥ śikhināṃ babhūvur yasmin asahyāni vinā tvayā me.

#### <span class="box">13.28</span>

pūrvānubhūtaṃ smaratā ca yatra kampottaraṃ bhīru tavopagūḍham, guhāvisārīṇy ativāhitāni mayā kathaṃcid ghanagarjitāni.

#### <span class="box">13.29</span>

āsārasiktakṣitibāṣpayogān mām akṣiṇod yatra vibhinnakośaiḥ, viḍambyamānā navakandalais te vivāhadhūmāruṇalocanaśrīḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.30</span>

upāntavānīravanopagūdhāny ālakṣyapāriplavasārasāni, dūrāvatīrṇā pibatīva khedād amūni pampāsalilāni dṛṣṭiḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.31</span>

atrāviyuktāni rathāṅganāmnām anyonyadattotpalakesarāṇi, dvandvāni dūrāntaravartinā te mayā priye saspṛham īkṣitāni.

#### <span class="box">13.32</span>

imāṃ tatāśokalatāṃ ca tanvīṃ stanābhirāmastabakābhinamrām, tvatprāptibuddhyā pariripsamānaḥ saumitriṇā sāsram ahaṃ niṣiddhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.33</span>

amūr vimānāntaralambinīnāṃ śrutvā svanaṃ kāñcanakiṅkiṇīnām, pratyudvrajantīva kham utpatantyo godāvarīsārasapaṅktayas tvām.

#### <span class="box">13.34</span>

eṣā tvayā peśalamadhyayāpi ghaṭāmbusaṃvardhitabālacūtā, āhlādayaty unmukhakṛṣṇasārā dṛṣṭa cirāt pañcavaṭī mano me.

#### <span class="box">13.35</span>

atrānugodaṃ mṛgayānivṛttas taraṅgavātema vinītakhedaḥ, rahas tvadutsaṅganiṣaṇṇamūrdhā smarāmi vānīragṛheṣu suptaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.36</span>

bhrūbheda mātreṇa padān maghonaḥ prabhraṃśayāṃ yo nahuṣaṃ cakāra, tasyāvilāmbhaḥpariśuddhihetor bhaumo muneḥ sthānaparigraho 'yam.

#### <span class="box">13.37</span>

tretāgnidhūmāgram anindyakīrtes tasyedam ākrāntavimānamārgam, ghrātvā havirgandhi rajovimuktaḥ samaśnute me laghimānam ātmā.

#### <span class="box">13.38</span>

etan muner mānini śātakarṇeḥ pañcāpsaro nāma vihāravāri, ābhāti paryantavanaṃ vidūrān meghāntarālakṣyam ivendubimbam.

#### <span class="box">13.39</span>

purā sa darbhāṅkuramātravṛttiś caran mṛgaiḥ sārdham ṛṣir maghonā, samādhibhītena kilopanītaḥ pañcāpsaroyauvanakūṭabhandham.

#### <span class="box">13.40</span>

tasyāyam antarhitasaudhabhājaḥ prasaktasaṃgītamṛdaṅgaghoṣaḥ, viyadgataḥ puṣpakacandraśālāḥ kṣaṇaṃ pratiṣrunmukharāḥ karoti.

#### <span class="box">13.41</span>

havirbhujām edhavatāṃ caturṇāṃ madhye lalāṭaṃtapasaptasaptiḥ, asau tapasyaty aparas tapasvī nāmnā sutīkṣṇaś caritena dāntaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.42</span>

amuṃ sahāsaprahitekṣaṇāni vyājārdhasaṃdarśitamekhalāni, nālaṃ vikartuṃ janitendraśaṅkaṃ surāṅganāvibhramaceṣṭitāni.

#### <span class="box">13.43</span>

eṣo 'kṣamālāvalayaṃ mṛgāṇāṃ kaṇḍūyitāraṃ kuśasūcilāvam, sabhājane me bhujam ūrdhvabāhuḥ savyetaraṃ prādhvam itaḥ prayuṅkte.

#### <span class="box">13.44</span>

vācaṃyamatvāt praṇatiṃ mamaiṣa kampena kiṃcit pratigṛhya mūrdhnaḥ, dṛṣṭiṃ vimānavyavadhānamuktāṃ punaḥ sahasrāciṣi saṃnidhatte.

#### <span class="box">13.45</span>

adaḥ śaraṇyaṃ śarabhaṅganāmnas tapovanaṃ pāvanam āhitāgneḥ, cirāya saṃtarpya samidhir agniṃ yo mantrapūtāṃ tanum apy ahauṣīt.

#### <span class="box">13.46</span>

chāyāvinītādhvapariśrameṣu bhūyiṣṭhasaṃbhāvyaphaleṣv amīṣu, tasyātithīnām adhunā saparyā sthitā suputreṣv iva pādapeṣu.

#### <span class="box">13.47</span>

dhārāsvanodgāridarīmukho 'sau śṛṅgāgralagnāmbudavaprapaṅkaḥ, badhnāti me bandhuragātri cakṣur dṛptaḥ kakudmān iva citrakūṭaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.48</span>

eṣā prasannastimitapravāhā sarid vidūrāntarabhāvatanvī, mandākinī bhāti nagopakaṇṭhe muktāvalī kaṇṭhagateva bhūmeḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.49</span>

ayaṃ sujāto 'nugiraṃ tamālaḥ pravālam ādāya sugandhi yasya, karṇārpiten' T ākaravaṃ kapolam apārthyakālāgurupattralekham Vt.

#### <span class="box">13.50</span>

anigrahatrāsavinītasattvam apuṣpaliṅgāt phalabandhivṛkṣam, vanaṃ tapaḥsādhanam etad atrer āviṣkṛtodagrataraprabhāvam.

#### <span class="box">13.51</span>

atrābhiṣekāya tapodhanānāṃ saptarśihastoddhṛtahemapadmām, pravartayām āsa kil' ānusūyā trisrotasaṃ tryambakamaulimālām.

#### <span class="box">13.52</span>

vīrāsanair dhyānajuṣām ṛṣīnām amī samādhyāsitavedimadhyāḥ, nivātaniṣkampatayā vibhānti yogādhirūḍhā iva śākhino 'pi.

#### <span class="box">13.53</span>

tvayā purastād upayācito yaḥ so 'yaṃ vaṭaḥ śyāma iti pratītaḥ, rāśir maṇīnām iva gāruḍānāṃ sapadmarāgaḥ phalito vibhāti.

#### <span class="box">13.54</span>

kvacit prabhā cāndramasī tamobhiś muktāmayī yaṣṭir ivānuviddhā, anyatra mālā sitapaṅkajānām indīvarair utkhacitāntareva.

#### <span class="box">13.55</span>

kvacit khagānāṃ priyamānasānāṃ kādambasaṃsargavatīva, anyatra śubhrā śaradabhralekhā bhaktir bhuvaś candanakalpiteva.
#### <span class="box">13.56</span>

kvacit prabhā cāndramasī tamobhiś chāyāvilīnaiḥ śabalīkṛteva, anyatra śubhrā śaradabhralekhā randhreṣv ivālakṣyanabhaḥpradeśā.

#### <span class="box">13.57</span>

kvacic ca kṛṣṇoragabhūṣaṇeva bhasmāṅgarāgā tanur īśvarasya, paśyānavadyāṅgi vibhāti gaṅgā bhinnapravāhā yamunātaraṅgaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.57A</span>

tamisrayā śubhraniśeva bhinnā kundasrag indīvaramālayeva, kṛttir hareḥ kṛṣṇamṛgatvaceva bhūtiḥ smarārer iva kaṇṭhabhāsā.

#### <span class="box">13.57B</span>

dṛśyārdhayā śāradameghalekhā nirdhūtanistriṃśarucā viśeva, gavākṣakālāgurudhūmarājyā harmyasthalīlepasudhā naveva.

#### <span class="box">13.57C</span>

tuṣārasaṃghātaśilā himādrer jātyāñjanaprastaraśobhayeva, patatriṇāṃ manasagocarāṇāṃ T śreṇīva kādambavihaṃgapaṅktyā.

#### <span class="box">13.57D</span>

nitāntaśuddhasphuṭikāśayogād vaiḍūryakāntyā raśanāvalīva, gaṅgā raver ātmajayā sametā puṣpyaty udāraṃ parabhāgalekhā.

#### <span class="box">13.58</span>

samudrapatnyor jalasaṃnipāte pūtātmanām atra kilābhiṣekāt, tattvāvabodhena vināpi bhūyas tanutyajāṃ nāsti śarīrabandhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.59</span>

puraṃ niṣādādhipater idaṃ tad yasmin mayā maulimaṇiṃ vihāya, jaṭāsu baddhāsv arudat sumantraḥ kaikeyi kāmāḥ phalitās taveti.

#### <span class="box">13.60</span>

payodharaiḥ puṇyajanāṅganānāṃ nirviṣṭahemāmbujareṇu yasyāḥ, brāhmaṃ saraḥ kāraṇam āptavāco buddher ivāvyaktam udāharanti.

#### <span class="box">13.61</span>

jalāni yā tīranikhātayūpā vahaty ayodhyām anu rājadhānīm, turaṃgamedhāvabhṛtavatīrṇair ikṣvākubhiḥ puṇyatarīkṛtāni.

#### <span class="box">13.62</span>

yāṃ saikatotsaṅgasukhocitānāṃ prājyaiḥ payobhiḥ parivardhitānām, sāmānyadhātrīm iva mānasaṃ me saṃbhāvayaty uttarakosalānām.

#### <span class="box">13.63</span>

seyaṃ madīyā jananīva tena mānyena rājñā sarayūr viyuktā, dūre vasantaṃ śiśirānilair māṃ taraṅgahastair upagūhatīva.

#### <span class="box">13.64</span>

viraktasaṃdhyākapiśaṃ purastād yato rajaḥ pārthivam ujjihīte, śaṅke hanūmatkathitapravṛttiḥ pratyudgato māṃ bharataḥ sasainyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.65</span>

addhā śriyaṃ pālitasaṃgarāya pratyarpayiṣyaty anaghāṃ sa sādhuḥ, hatvā nivṛttāya mṛdhe kharādīn saṃrakṣitāṃ tvām iva lakṣmaṇo me.

#### <span class="box">13.66</span>

asau puraskṛtya guruṃ padātiḥ paścādavasthāpitavāhinīkaḥ, vṛddhair amātyaiḥ saha cīravāsā mām arghyapāṇir bharato 'bhyupaiti.

#### <span class="box">13.67</span>

pitrā nisṛṣṭāṃ madapekṣayā yaḥ śriyaṃ yuvāpy aṅkagatām abhoktā, iyanti varṣāṇi tayā sahogram abhyasyatīva vratam āsidhāram.

#### <span class="box">13.68</span>

etāvad uktavati dāśarathau tadīyām icchāṃ vimānam adhidevatayā viditvā, dyotiṣpathād avatatāra savismayābhir udvīkṣitaṃ prakṛtibhir bharatānugābhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.69</span>

tasmāt puraḥsaravibhīṣaṇadarśitena sevāvicakṣaṇaharīśvaradattahastaḥ, yānād avātarad adūramahītalena mārgeṇa bhaṅgiracitasphaṭikena rāmaḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.70</span>

ikṣvākuvaṃśagurave prayataḥ praṇamya sa bhrātaraṃ bharatam arghyaparigrahānte, paryaśrur asvajata mūrdhani copajaghrau tadbhaktyapoḍhapitṛrāhyamahābhiṣeke.

#### <span class="box">13.71</span>

śmaśrupravṛddhijanitānanavikriyāṃś ca plakṣān prarohajaṭilān iva mantrivṛddhān, anvagrahīt praṇamataḥ śubhadṛṣṭipātair vārttānuyogamadhurākṣarayā ca vācā.

#### <span class="box">13.72</span>

durjātabandhur ayam ṛkṣaharīśvaro me paulastya eṣa samareṣu puraḥ prahartā, ity ādṛtena kathitau raghunandanena vyutkramya lakṣmaṇam ubhau bharato vavande.

#### <span class="box">13.73</span>

saumitriṇā tadanu saṃsasṛje sa cainam utthāpya namraśirasaṃ bhṛśam āliniṅga, rūḍhendrajitpraharaṇavraṇakarkaśena kliśyann ivāsya bhujamadhyam uraḥsthalena.

#### <span class="box">13.74</span>

rāmājñayā haricamūpatayas tadānīṃ kṛtvā manuṣyavapur āruruhur gajendrān, teṣu kṣaratsu bahudhā madavāridhārāḥ śailādhirohaṇasukhāny upalebhire te.

#### <span class="box">13.75</span>

sānuplavaḥ prabhur api kṣaṇadācarāṇāṃ bheje rathān daśarathaprabhavānuśiṣṭaḥ, māyāvikalparacitair api ye tadīyair na syandanais tulitakṛtrimabhaktiśobhāḥ.

#### <span class="box">13.76</span>

bhūyas tato raghupatir vilasatpatākam adhyāsta kāmagati sāvarajo vimānam, doṣātanaṃ budhabṛhaspatiyogadṛśyas tārāpatis taralavidyud iv'ābhravṛndam.

#### <span class="box">13.77</span>

tatreśvareṇa jagatāṃ pralayād ivorvīṃ varṣātyayena rucam abhraghanād ivendoḥ, rāmeṇa maithilasutāṃ daśakaṇṭhakṛcchrāt pratyuddhṛtāṃ dhṛtimatīṃ bharato vavande.

#### <span class="box">13.78</span>

laṅkeśvarapraṇatibhaṅgadṛḍhavrataṃ tad (?) vandyaṃ yugaṃ caraṇayor janakātmajāyāḥ, jyeṣṭhānuvṛttijaṭilaṃ ca śiro 'sya sādhor anyonyapāvanam abhūd ubhayaṃ sametya.

#### <span class="box">13.79</span>

krośārdhaṃ prakṛtipuraḥsareṇa gatvā kākutsthaḥ stimitajavena puṣpakeṇa, śatrughnaprativihitopakāryam āryaḥ sāketopavanam udāram adhyuvāsa.

#### <span class="box">14.1</span>

uttiṣṭha vatse nanu sānujo 'sau daśāntaraṃ tatra samaṃ prapanne, apaśyatāṃ dāśarathī jananyau chedād ivopaghnataror vratatyau.

#### <span class="box">14.2</span>

ubhāv ubhābhyāṃ praṇatau hatārī yathākramaṃ vikramaśobhinau tau, vispaṣṭam asrāndhatayā na dṛṣṭau jñātau sutasparśasukhopalambhāt.

#### <span class="box">14.3</span>

ānandajaḥ śokajam aśru bāṣpas tayor aśītaṃ śiśiro bibheda, gaṅgāsarayvor jalam uṣṇatpataṃ himādrinisyanda ivāvatīrṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.4</span>

te putrayor nairṛtaśastramārgān ārdrān ivāṅge sadayaṃ spṛśantyau, apīpsitaṃ kṣatrakulāṅganānāṃ na vīrasūśabdam akāmayetām.

#### <span class="box">14.5</span>

kleśāvahā bhartur alakṣaṇāhaṃ sīteti nāma svam udīrayantī, svargapratiṣṭhasya guror mahiṣyāv abhaktibhedena vadhūr vavande.

#### <span class="box">14.6</span>

uttiṣṭha vatse nanu sānujo 'sau vṛttena bhartā śucinā tavaiva, kṛcchraṃ mahat tīrṇa iti priyārhāṃ tām ūcatus te priyam apy amithyā.

#### <span class="box">14.7</span>

athābhiṣekaṃ raghuvaṃśaketoḥ prārabdham ānandajalair jananyoḥ, nirvartayām āsur amātyavṛddhās tīrthāhṛtaiḥ kāñcanakumbhatoyaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.8</span>

saritsamudrān sarasīś ca gatvā rakṣaḥkapīndrair upapāditāni, tasyāpatan mūrdhni jalāni jiṣṇor vindhyasya meghaprabhavā ivāpaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.9</span>

tapasviveṣakriyayāpi tāvad yaḥ prekṣaṇīyaḥ sutarāṃ babhūva, rājendranepathyavidhānaśobhā rasyoditāsīt punaruktadoṣā.

#### <span class="box">14.10</span>

sa maularakṣoharimiśrasainyas tūryasvanānanditapauravargaḥ, viveṣa saudhodgatalājavarṣām uttoraṇām anvayarājadhānīm.

#### <span class="box">14.11</span>

saumitriṇā sāvarajena mandam ādhūtavālavyajano rathasthaḥ, dhṛtātapatro bharatena sākṣād upāyasaṃghāta iva pravṛddhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.12</span>

prāsādakālāgurudhūmarājis tasyāḥ puro vāyuvaśena bhinnā, vanān nivṛttena raghūdvahena muktā svayaṃ veṇir ivābhāse.

#### <span class="box">14.13</span>

śvaśrūjanānuṣṭhitacāruveṣāṃ karṇīrathasthāṃ raghuvīrapatnīm, prāsādavātāyanadṛśyabandhaiḥ sāketanāryo 'ñjalibhiḥ praṇemuḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.14</span>

sphuratprabhāmaṇḍalam ānusūyaṃ sā bibhratī śāśvatam aṅgarāgam, rarāja śuddheti punaḥ svapuryai saṃdarśita vahnigateva bhartrā.

#### <span class="box">14.15</span>

veśmāni rāmaḥ paribarhavanti viśrāṇya sauhārdhanidhiḥ suhṛdbyaḥ, bāṣpāyamāṇo balimanniketam ālekhyaśeṣasya pitur viveśa.

#### <span class="box">14.16</span>

kṛtāñjalis tatra yad amba satyān nābhraśyata svargaphalād gurur naḥ, tac cintyamānaṃ sukṛtaṃ taveti jahāra lajjāṃ bharatasya mātuḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.17</span>

tathā ca sugrīvavibhīśaṇādīn upācarat kṛtrimasaṃvidhābhiḥ, saṃkalpamātroditasiddhayas te krāntā yathā cetasi vismayena.

#### <span class="box">14.18</span>

sabhājanāyopagatān sa divyān munīn puraskṛtya hatasya śatroḥ, śuśrāva tebhyaḥ prabhavādi vṛttaṃ svavikrame gauravam ādadhānam.

#### <span class="box">14.19</span>

pratiprayāteṣu tapodhaneṣu sukhād avijñātagatārdhamāsān, sītāsvahastopahṛtāgryapūjān rakṣaḥkapīndrān visasarja rāmaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.20</span>

tac cātmacintāsulabhaṃ vimānaṃ hṛtaṃ surāreḥ saha jīvitena, kailāsanāthodvahanāya bhūyaḥ puṣpaṃ divaḥ puṣpakam anvamaṃsta.

#### <span class="box">14.21</span>

pitur niyogād vanavāsam evaṃ nistīrya rāmaḥ pratipannarājyaḥ, dharmārthakāmeṣu samāṃ prapede yathā tathaivāvarajeṣu vṛttim.

#### <span class="box">14.22</span>

sarvāsu mātṛṣv api vatsalatvāt sa nirviśeṣapratipattir āsīt, ṣaḍānanāpītapayodharāsu netā camūnām iva kṛttikāsu.

#### <span class="box">14.23</span>

tenārthavāṃl lobhaparāṅmukhena tena ghnatā vighnabhayaṃ kriyāvān, tenāsa lokaḥ pitṛmān vinetrā tenaiva śokāpanudena putrī.

#### <span class="box">14.24</span>

sa paurakāryāṇi samīkṣya kāle reme videhādhipater duhitrā, upasthitaś cāru vapus tadīyaṃ kṛtvopabhogotsukayeva lakṣmyā.

#### <span class="box">14.25</span>

tayor yathāprārthitam indriyārthān āseduṣoḥ sadmasu citravatsu, prāptāni duḥkhāny api daṇḍakeṣu saṃcintyamānāni sukhāny abhūvan.

#### <span class="box">14.26</span>

athādhikasnigdhavilocanena mukhena sītā śarapāṇḍureṇa, ānandayitrī pariṇetur āsīd anakṣaravyañjitadohadena.

#### <span class="box">14.27</span>

tām aṅkam āropya kṛśāṅgayaṣṭiṃ varṇāntarākrāntapayodharāgrām, vilajjamānāṃ rahasi pratītaḥ prapraccha rāmāṃ ramaṇo 'bhilāṣam.

#### <span class="box">14.28</span>

sā daṣṭanīvārabalīnihiṃsraiḥ saṃbaddha vaikhānasakanyakāni, iyeṣa bhūyaḥ kuśavanti gantuṃ bhāgīrathītīratapovanāni.

#### <span class="box">14.29</span>

tasyai pratiśrutya raghupravīras tad (?) īpsitaṃ pārśvacarānuyātaḥ, ālokayiṣyan muditām ayodhyāṃ prāsādam abhraṃliham āruroha.

#### <span class="box">14.30</span>

ṛddhāpaṇaṃ rājapathaṃ sa paśyan vigāhyamānāṃ sarayūṃ ca naubhiḥ, vilāsibhiś cādhyuṣitāni pauraiḥ puropakaṇṭhopavanāni reme.

#### <span class="box">14.31</span>

sa kiṃvadantīṃ vadatāṃ purogaḥ svaṛttam uddiśya viśuddhavṛttaḥ, sarpādhirājorubhujo 'pasarpaṃ papraccha bhadraṃ vijitāribhadraḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.32</span>

nirbandhapṛṣṭaḥ sa jagāda sarvaṃ stuvanti paurāś caritaṃ tvadīyam, anyatra rakṣobhavanoṣitāyāḥ parigrahān mānavadeva devyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.33</span>

kalatranindāguruṇā kilaivam abhyāhataṃ kīrtiviparyayeṇa, ayoghanenāya ivābhitaptaṃ vaidehibandhor hṛdayaṃ vidadre.

#### <span class="box">14.34</span>

kim ātmanirvādakathām upekṣe jāyām adoṣām uta saṃtyajāmi, ity ekapakṣāśrayaviklavatvād āsīt sa dolācalacittavṛttiḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.35</span>

niścitya cānanyanivṛtti vācyaṃ tyāgena patnyāḥ parimārṣṭum aicchat, api svadehāt kim utendriyārthād yaśodhanānāṃ hi yaśo garīyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.36</span>

sa saṃnipātyāvarajān hataujās tadvikriyādarśanaluptaharṣān, kaulīnam ātmāśrayam ācacakṣe tebhyaḥ punaś cedam uvāca vākyam.

#### <span class="box">14.37</span>

rājarṣivaṃśasya raviprasūter upasthitaḥ paśyata kīdṛśo 'yam, mattaḥ sadācāraśuceḥ kalaṅkaḥ payodavātād iva darpaṇasya.

#### <span class="box">14.38</span>

paureṣu so 'haṃ vahulībhavantam apāṃ taraṅgeṣv iva tailabindum, soḍhuṃ na tatpūrvam avarṇam īśe ālānikaṃ sthāṇum iva dviependraḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.39</span>

tasyāpanodāya phalapravṛttāv upasthitāyām api nirvyapekṣaḥ, tyakṣyāmi vaidehasutāṃ purastāt samudranemiṃ pitur ājñayeva.

#### <span class="box">14.40</span>

avaimi cainām anagheti kiṃ tu lokāpavādo balavān mato me, chāyā hi bhūmeḥ śaśino malatvenāropitā śuddhimataḥ prajābhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.41</span>

rakṣovadhānto na ca me prayāso vyarthaḥ sa vairapratimocanāya, amarṣaṇaḥ śoṇitakāṅkṣayā kiṃ padā spṛśantaṃ daśati dvijihvaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.42</span>

tad eṣa sargaḥ karuṇārdracittair na me bhavadbhiḥ pratiṣedhanīyaḥ, yady arthitā nirhṛtavācyaśalyān prāṇān mayā dhārayituṃ ciraṃ vaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.43</span>

ity uktavantaṃ janakātmajāyāṃ nitāntarūkṣābhiniveśam īśam, na kaścana bhrātṛṣu teṣu śakto niṣeddhum āsīd anuvartituṃ vā.

#### <span class="box">14.44</span>

sa lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmaṇapūrvajanmā vilokya lokatrayagītakīrtiḥ, saumyeti cābhāṣya yathārthabhāṣī sthitaṃ nideśe pṛthag ādideśa.

#### <span class="box">14.45</span>

prajāvatī dohadaśaṃsinī te tapovaneṣu spṛhayālur eva, saumyeti cābhāṣya yathārthabhāṣī prāpayya vālmīkipadaṃ tyajainām.

#### <span class="box">14.46</span>

sa śuśruvān mātari bhārgaveṇa pitur niyogāt prahṛtam dviṣadvat, pratyagrahīd agrajaśāsanaṃ tad ājñā gurūṇāṃ hy avicāraṇīyā.

#### <span class="box">14.47</span>

athānukūlaśravaṇapratītām atrasnubhir yuktadhuraṃ turaṃgaiḥ, rathaṃ sumantra pratipannaraśmim āropya vaidehasutāṃ pratasthe.

#### <span class="box">14.48</span>

sā nīyamānā rucirān pradeśān priyaṃkaro me priya ity anandat, nābuddha kalpadrumatāṃ vihāya jātaṃ tam ātmany asipattravṛkṣam.

#### <span class="box">14.49</span>

jugūha tasyāḥ pathi lakṣmaṇo yat savyetareṇa sphuratā tad akṣṇā, ākhyātam asyai guru bhāvi duḥkham atyantaluptapriyadarśanena.

#### <span class="box">14.50</span>

sā durnimittopagatād viṣādāt sadyaḥ parimlānamukhāravindā, rājñaḥ śivaṃ sāvarajasya bhūyād ity āśaśaṃse karaṇair abāhyaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.51</span>

guror niyogād vanitāṃ vanānte sādhvīṃ sumitrātanayo vihāsyan, avāryatevotthitavīcihastair jahnor duhitrā shitayā purastāt.

#### <span class="box">14.52</span>

rathāt sa yantrā nigṛhītavāhāt tāṃ bhrātṛhyāyāṃ puline 'vatārya, gaṅgāṃ niṣādāhṛtanauviśeṣas tatāra saṃdhām iva satyasaṃdhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.53</span>

atha vyavasthāpitavāk kathaṃcit saumitrir antargatabāṣpakaṇṭhaḥ, autpātiko megha ivāśmavarṣaṃ mahīpateḥ śāsanam ujjagāra.

#### <span class="box">14.54</span>

tato 'bhiṣaṅgānilavipraviddhā prabhraśyamānābharaṇasprasūnā, svamūrtilābhaprakṛtiṃ dharitrīṃ lateva sītā sahasā jagāma.

#### <span class="box">14.55</span>

ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhavaḥ kathaṃ tvāṃ tyajed akasmāt patir āryavṛttaḥ, iti kṣitiḥ saṃśayiteva tasyai dadau praveśaṃ jananī na tāvat.

#### <span class="box">14.56</span>

sā luptasaṃjñā na viveda duḥkhaṃ pratyāgatāsuḥ samatapyatāntaḥ, tasyāḥ sumitrātmajayatnalabdho mohād abhūt kaṣṭataraḥ prabodhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.57</span>

na cāvadad bhartur avarṇam āryā nirākariṣṇor vṛjinād ṛte 'pi, ātmānam eva sthiraduḥkhabājaṃ punaḥ punar duṣkṛtinaṃ nininda.

#### <span class="box">14.58</span>

āśvāsya rāmāvarajaḥ satīṃ tām ākhyātavālmīkiniketamārgaḥ, nighnasya me bhartṛnideśaraukṣyaṃ devi kṣamasveti babhūva namraḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.59</span>

sītā samutthāpya jagāda vākyaṃ prītāsmi te saumyacirāya jīva, viḍaujasā viṣṇur ivāgrajena bhrātrā yad itthaṃ paravān asi tvam.
#### <span class="box">14.60</span>

śvaśrūjanaṃ sarvam anukrameṇa vijñāpaya prāpitamatpraṇāmaḥ, prajāniśekaṃ mayi vartamānaṃ sūnor anudhyāyata cetaseti.

#### <span class="box">14.61</span>

vācyas tvayā madvacanāt sa rājā vahnau viśuddhām api yat samakṣam, māṃ lokavādaśravaṇād ahāsīḥ śrutasya kiṃ tat sadṛśaṃ kulasya.

#### <span class="box">14.62</span>

kalyāṇabuddher atha vā tavāyaṃ na kāmacāro mayi śaṅkanīyaḥ, mamaiva janmāntarapātakānāṃ vipākavisphūrjathur aprasahyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.63</span>

upasthitāṃ pūrvam apāsya lakṣmīṃ vanaṃ mayā sārdham asi prapannaḥ, tad āspadaṃ prāpya tayātiroṣāt soḍhāsmi na tvadbhavane vasantī.

#### <span class="box">14.64</span>

niśācaropaplutabhartṛkāṇāṃ tapasvinīnāṃ bhavataḥ prasādāt, bhūtvā śaraṇyā śaraṇārtham anyāṃ kathaṃ prapatsye tvayi dīpyamāne.

#### <span class="box">14.65</span>

kiṃ vā tavātyantaviyogamoghe kuryām upekṣāṃ hatajīvite 'smin, syād rakṣaṇīyaṃ yadi me na tejas tvadīyam antargatam antarāyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.66</span>

sāhaṃ tapaḥ sūryaniviṣṭadṛṣṭir ūrdhvaṃ prasūtes caritum yatiṣye, tathā yathā me jananāntare 'pi tvam eva bhartā na ca viprayogaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.67</span>

nṛpasya varṇāśramarakṣaṇaṃ yat sa eva dharmo manunā praṇītaḥ, nirvāsitāpy evam atas tvayāhaṃ tapasvisāmānyam avekṣaṇīyā.

#### <span class="box">14.68</span>

tatheti tasyāḥ pratigṛhya vācaṃ rāmānuje dṛśṭipathaṃ vyatīte, sā muktakaṇṭhaṃ vyasanātibhārāc cakranda vignā kurarīva bhūyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.69</span>

nṛtyaṃ mayūrāḥ kusumāni vṛkṣā darbhān upāttān vijahur hariṇyaḥ, tasyāḥ prapanne samaduḥkhabhāvam atyantam āsīd ruditaṃ vane 'pi.

#### <span class="box">14.70</span>

tām abhyagacchad ruditānusārī kaviḥ kuśedhmāharaṇāya yātaḥ, niṣādaviddhāṇḍajadarśanotthaḥ ślokatvam āpadyata yasya śokaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.71</span>

tam aśru netrāvaraṇaṃ pramṛjya sītā vilāpād viratā vavande, tasyai munir dohadaliṅgadarśī dāśvān supurtrāśiṣam ity uvāca.

#### <span class="box">14.72</span>

jāne viṣṛśṭāṃ praṇidhānatas tvāṃ mithyāpavādakṣubhitena bhartrā, tan mā vyathiṣṭhā viṣayāntarasthaṃ prāptāsi vaidehi pitur niketam.

#### <span class="box">14.73</span>

uthkātalokatrayakaṇṭake 'pi satyapratijñe 'py avikatthane 'pi, tvāṃ praty akasmāt kaluṣapravṛttāv asty eva manyur bharatāgraje me.

#### <span class="box">14.74</span>

tavendukīrtiḥ śvaśuraḥ sakhā me satāṃ bhavocchedakaraḥ pitā te, dhuri sthitā tvaṃ patidevatānāṃ kiṃ tan na yenāsi mamānukampyā.

#### <span class="box">14.75</span>

tapasvisaṃsargavinitatsattve tapovane vītabhayā vasāsmin, ito bhaviṣyaty anaghaprasūter apatyasaṃskāramayo vidhis te.

#### <span class="box">14.76</span>

aśūnyatīrāṃ munisaṃniveśais tamo'pahantrīṃ tamasāṃ vigāhya, tatsaikatotsaṅgabalikriyābhiḥ saṃpatsyate te manasaḥ prasādaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.77</span>

puṣpaṃ phalaṃ cārtavam āharantyo bījaṃ ca bāleyam akṛṣṭarohi, vinodayiṣyanti navābhiṣaṅgām udāravāco munikanyakās tvām.

#### <span class="box">14.78</span>

payoghaṭair āśramabālavṛkṣān saṃvardhayantī svabalānurūpaiḥ, asaṃśayaṃ prāk tanayopapatteḥ stanaṃdhayaprītim avāpsyasi tvam.

#### <span class="box">14.79</span>

anugrahapratyabhinandinīṃ tāṃ vālmīkir ādāya dayārdracetāḥ, sāyaṃ mṛgādhyāsitavedipārśvaṃ svam āśramaṃ śāntamṛgaṃ nināya.

#### <span class="box">14.80</span>

tām arpayām āsa ca śokadīnāṃ tadāgamaprītiṣu tāpasīṣu, nirviṣṭasārāṃ pitṛbhir himāṃśor antyāṃ kalāṃ darśa ivauṣadhīṣu.

#### <span class="box">14.81</span>

tā iṅgudīsnehakṛtapradīpam āstīrṇamedhyājinatalpam antaḥ, tasyai saparyānupadaṃ dinānte nivāsahetor uṭajaṃ viteruḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.82</span>

tatrābhiṣekaprayatā vasantī prayuktapūjā vidhinātithibhyaḥ, vanyena sā valkalinī śarīraṃ patyuḥ prajāsaṃtataye babhāra.

#### <span class="box">14.83</span>

api prabhuḥ sānuśayo 'dhunā syāt kim utsukaḥ śakrajito 'pi hantā, śaśaṃsa sītāparidevanāntam anuṣṭhitaṃ śāsanam agrajāya.

#### <span class="box">14.84</span>

babhūva rāmaḥ sahasā sabāṣpas tuṣāravarṣīva sahasyacandraḥ, kaulīnabhītena gṛhān nirastā na tena vaidehasutā manastaḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.85</span>

nigṛhya śokaṃ svayam eva dhīmān varṇāśramāvekṣaṇajāgarūkaḥ, sa bhrātṛsādhāraṇabhogam ṛddhaṃ rājyaṃ rajoriktamanāḥ śaśāsa.

#### <span class="box">14.86</span>

tām ekabhāryāṃ parivādabhīroḥ sādhvīm api tyaktavato nṛpasya, vakṣasy asaṃghaṭṭasukhaṃ vasantī reje sapatnīrahiteva lakṣmīḥ.

#### <span class="box">14.87</span>

sītāṃ hitvā daśamukharipur nopayema yad anyāṃ tasyā eva pratikṛtisakho yat kratūn ājahāra, vṛttāntena śravaṇaviṣayaprāpiṇā tena bhartuḥ sā durvāraṃ katham api parityāgaduḥkhaṃ viṣehe.

#### <span class="box">15.1</span>

kṛtasītāparityāgaḥ sa ratnākaramekhalām, bubhūje pṛthivīpālaḥ pṛthivīm eva kevalām.

#### <span class="box">15.2</span>

lavaṇena viluptejyās tāmisreṇa tam abhyayuḥ, munayo yamunābhājaḥ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇārthinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.3</span>

avekṣya rāmaṃ te tasmin na prajahruḥ svatejasā, trāṇābhāve hi śāpāstrāḥ kurvanti tapaso vyayam.

#### <span class="box">15.4</span>

pratiśuśrāva kākutsthas tebhyo vighnapratikriyām, dharmasaṃrakṣaṇāyaiva pravṛttir bhuvi śārṅgiṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.5</span>

te rāmāya vadhopāyam ācakhyur vibudhaviṣaḥ, durjayo lavaṇaḥ śūlī viśūlaḥ prārthyatām iti.

#### <span class="box">15.6</span>

ādideśātha śatrughnaṃ teṣāṃ kṣemāya rāghavaḥ, kariṣyann iva nāmāsya yathārtham arinigrahāt.

#### <span class="box">15.7</span>

yaḥ kaścana raghūṇāṃ hi param ekaḥ paraṃtapaḥ, apavāda ivotsargaṃ vyāvartayitum īśvaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.8</span>

agrajena prayuktāśīs tadā dāśarathī rathī, yayau vanstahliḥ paśyan puṣpitāḥ surabhīr abhīḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.9</span>

rāmādeśād anupadaṃ senāṅgaṃ tasya siddhaye, paścād adhyayanārthasya dhātor adhir ivābhavat.

#### <span class="box">15.10</span>

ādiṣṭavartmā munibhiḥ sa gacchaṃs tapatāṃ varaḥ, virarāja rathapṛṣṭhair vālakhilyair ivāṃśumān.

#### <span class="box">15.11</span>

tasya mārgavaśād ekā babhūva vasatir yataḥ, rathasvanotkaṇṭhamṛge vālmīkīye tapovane.

#### <span class="box">15.12</span>

tam ṛṣiḥ pūjayām āsa kumāraṃ klāntavāhanam, tapaḥprabhāvasiddhābhir viśeṣapratipattibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.13</span>

tasyām evāsya yāminyām antarvatnī prajāvatī, sutāv asūta saṃpannau kośadaṇḍāv iva kṣitiḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.14</span>

saṃtānaśravaṇād bhrātuḥ saumitriḥ saumanasyavān, prāñjalir munim āmantrya prātar yuktaratho yayau.
#### <span class="box">15.15</span>

sa ca prāpa madhūpaghnaṃ kumbhīnasyāś ca kukṣijaḥ, vanāt karam ivādāya sattvarāśim upasthitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.16</span>

dhūmadhūmro vasāghandhī jvālābabhruśiroruhaḥ, kravyādgaṇaparīvāraś citāgnir iva jaṅgamaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.17</span>

apaśulaṃ tam āsādya lavaṇaṃ lakṣmaṇānujaḥ, rurodha saṃmukhīno hi jayo randhraprahāriṇām.

#### <span class="box">15.18</span>

nātiparyāptam ālakṣya matkukṣer adya bhojanam, diṣṭyā tvam asi me dhātrā bhīgtenevopapāditaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.19</span>

iti saṃtarjya śatrughnaṃ rākṣasas tajjighāṃsayā, prāṃśum utpāṭayām āsa mustāstambam iva drumam.

#### <span class="box">15.20</span>

saumitrer niśitair bāṇair antarā śakalīkṛtaḥ, gātraṃ puṣparajaḥ prāpa na śākhī nairṛteritaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.21</span>

vināśāt tasya vṛkṣasya rakṣas tasmai mahopalam, prajighāya kṛtāntasya muṣṭiṃ pṛthag iva sthitam.

#### <span class="box">15.22</span>

aindram astram upādāya śatrughnena sa tāḍitaḥ, sikatābhyo 'pi hi parāṃ prapede paramāṇutām.

#### <span class="box">15.23</span>

dakṣiṇaṃ doṣam udyamya rākṣasas tam upādravat, ekatāla ivopātapavanaprerito giriḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.24</span>

kārṣnena pattrinā śatruḥ sa bhinnarhṛdayaḥ patan, ānināya bhuvaḥ kampaṃ jahārāśramavāsinām.

#### <span class="box">15.25</span>

vayasāṃ paṅktayaḥ petur hatasyopari rakṣasaḥ, tatpratidvandino mūrdhni divyāḥ kusumavṛṣṭayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.26</span>

sa hatvā lavaṇaṃ vīras tadā mene mahaujasaḥ, bhrātuḥ sodaryam ātmānam indrajidvadhaśobhinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.27</span>

tasya saṃstūyamānasya caritārthais tapasvibhiḥ, śuśubhe vikramodagraṃ vrīḍayāvanataṃ śiraḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.28</span>

upakūlaṃ sa kālindyāḥ purīṃ pauruṣabhūṣaṇaḥ, nirmame nirmamo 'rtheṣu mathurāṃ madhurākṛtiḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.29</span>

yā saurājyaprakāśābhir babhau pauravibhūtibhiḥ, svargābhiṣyandavamanaṃ kṛtvevopaniveśitā.

#### <span class="box">15.30</span>

tatra saudhagataḥ paśyan yamunāṃ cakravākinīm, hema bhaktimatīṃ bhūmeḥ praveṇīm iva pripiye.

#### <span class="box">15.31</span>

sakhā daśarathasyātha janakasya ca mantrakṛt, saṃcaskārobhayaprītyā maithileyau yathāvidhi.

#### <span class="box">15.32</span>

sa tau kuśalavonmṛṣṭagarbhakledau tadākhyayā, kaviḥ kuśalavāv eva cakāra kila nāmataḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.33</span>

sāṅgaṃ ca vedam adhyāpya kiṃcidutkrāntaśaiśavau, svakṛtiṃ gāpayām āsa kaviprathamapaddhatim.

#### <span class="box">15.34</span>

rāmasya madhuraṃ vṛttaṃ gāyantau mātur agrataḥ, tadviyogavyathāṃ kiṃcic chithilīcakratuḥ sutau.

#### <span class="box">15.35</span>

itare 'pi raghor vaṃśyās trayas tretāgnitejasaḥ, tadyogāt pativatnīṣu patnīṣv āsan dvisūnavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.36</span>

śatrughātini śatrughnaḥ subāhau ca bahuśrute, mathurāvidiśe sūnvor nidadhe pūrvajotsukaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.37</span>

bhūyas tapovyayo mā bhūd vālmīker iti so 'tyagāt, maithilītanayodgītaniṣpandamṛgam āśramam.

#### <span class="box">15.38</span>

vaśī viveśa cāyodhyāṃ rathyāsaṃskāraśobhinīm, lavaṇasya vadhāt paurair atigauravam īkṣitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.39</span>

sa dadarśa sabhāmadhye sabhāsadbhir upasthitam, rāmaṃ sītāparityāgād asāmaṇyapatiṃ bhuvaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.40</span>

tam abhyanandat praṇataṃ lavaṇāntakam agrajaḥ, kālanemivadhāt prītas turāṣāḍ iva śārṅgiṇam.

#### <span class="box">15.41</span>

sa pṛṣṭaḥ sarvato vārttām ākhyād rājñe na saṃtatim, pratyarpayiṣyataḥ kāle kaver ādyasya śāsanāt.

#### <span class="box">15.42</span>

atha jānapado vipraḥ śiśum aprāptayauvanam, avatāry' āṅkaśayyāsthaṃ dvāri cakranda bhūpateḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.43</span>

śocanīyāsi vasudhe yā tvaṃ daśarathāc cyutā, rāmahastam anuprāpya kaṣṭāt kaṣṭataraṃ gatā.

#### <span class="box">15.44</span>

śrutvā tasya śuco hetuṃ goptā jihrāya rāghavaḥ, na hy akālabhavo mṛtyur ikṣvākupadam aspṛśat.

#### <span class="box">15.45</span>

sa muhūrtaṃ sahasveti dvijam āśvāsya duḥkhitam, yānaṃ sasmāra kauberaṃ vaivasvatajigīṣayā.

#### <span class="box">15.46</span>

āttaśastras tad adhyāsya pratisthaḥ sa raghūdvahaḥ, uccacāra puras tasya gūḍharūpā sarasvatī.

#### <span class="box">15.47</span>

rājan prajāsu te kaścid apacāraḥ pravartate, tam anviṣya praśamayer bhavitāsi tataḥ kṛtī.

#### <span class="box">15.48</span>

ity āptavacanād rāmo vineṣyan varṇavikriyām, diśaḥ papāta pattreṇa veganiṣkampaketunā.

#### <span class="box">15.49</span>

atha dhūmābhitāmrākṣaṃ vṛkṣākhāvalambinam, dadarśa kaṃcid aikśvākas tapasyantam adhomukham.

#### <span class="box">15.50</span>

pṛṣṭanāmānvayo rājñā sa kilācaṣṭa dhūmapaḥ, ātmānaṃ śambukaṃ nāma śūdraṃ surapadārthinam.

#### <span class="box">15.51</span>

tapasy anadhikāritvāt prajānāṃ tam aghāvaham, śīrṣacchedyaṃ paricchidya niyantā śastram ādade.

#### <span class="box">15.52</span>

sa tadvaktraṃ himakliṣṭakiñjalkam iva paṅkajam, jyotiṣkaṇāhataśmaśru kaṇṭhanālād apāharat.

#### <span class="box">15.53</span>

kṛtaṇḍaḥ svayam rājñā lebhe śūdraḥ satāṃ gatim, tapasā duścareṇāpi na svamārgavilaṅghinā.

#### <span class="box">15.54</span>

raghunātho 'py agastyena mārgasaṃdarśitātmanā, mahaujasā saṃyuyuje śaratkāla ivendunā.

#### <span class="box">15.55</span>

kumbhayonir alaṃkāraṃ tasmai divyaparigraham, dadau dattaṃ samudreṇa pītenevātmaniṣkrayam.

#### <span class="box">15.56</span>

taṃ dadhan maithilīkaṇṭhanirvyāpāreṇa bāhunā, paścān nivavṛte rāmaḥ prāk parāsur dvijātmajaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.57</span>

tasya pūrvoditāṃ nindāṃ dvijaḥ putrasamāgataḥ, stutyā nivartayām āsa trātur vaivasvatād api.

#### <span class="box">15.58</span>

tam adhvarāya muktāśvaṃ rakṣaḥkapinareśvarāḥ, meghāḥ sasyam ivāmbhobhir abhyavarṣann upāyanaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.59</span>

digbhyo nimantritāś cainam abhijagmur maharṣayaḥ, na bhaumāny eva dhiṣṇyāni hitvā jyotirmayāny api.

#### <span class="box">15.60</span>

upaśalyaniviṣṭais taiś caturdvāramukhī babhau, ayodhyā sṛṣṭalokeva sadyaḥ paitāmahī tanuḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.61</span>

ślāghyas tyāgo 'pi vaidehyāḥ patyuḥ prāgvaṃśavāsinaḥ, ananyahāneḥ tasyāsīt saiva jāyā hiraṇmayī.

#### <span class="box">15.62</span>

vidher adhikasaṃbhāras tataḥ pravavṛte makhaḥ, āsan yatra kriyāvighnā rākṣasā eva rakṣiṇaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.63</span>

atha prācetasopajñaṃ rāmāyaṇam itas tataḥ, maithileyau kuśalavau jagatur gurucoditau.

#### <span class="box">15.64</span>

vṛttaṃ rāmasya vālmīkeḥ kṛtis tau kiṃnarasvanau, kiṃ tad yena mano hartum alaṃ syātāṃ na śṛṇvatām.

#### <span class="box">15.65</span>

rūpe gīte ca mādhuryam tayos tajjñair niveditam, dadarśa sānujo rāmaḥ śuśrāva ca kutūhalī.

#### <span class="box">15.66</span>

tadgītaśravaṇaikāgrā saṃsad aśrumukhī babhau, himanisyandinī prātar nivāgteva vanasthalī.

#### <span class="box">15.67</span>

vayoveṣavisaṃvādi rāmasya ca tayoś ca sā, janatā prekṣya sādṛśyaṃ nākśikampaṃ vyatiṣṭhata.

#### <span class="box">15.68</span>

ubhayor na tathā lokaḥ prāvīṇyena visiṣmiye, nṛpateḥ prītidāneṣu vītaspṛhatayā yathā.

#### <span class="box">15.69</span>

geye kena vinītau vāṃ kasya ceyaṃ kaveḥ kṛtiḥ, iti rājñā svayaṃ pṛṣṭau tau vālmīkim aśaṃsatām.

#### <span class="box">15.70</span>

atha sāvarajo rāmaḥ prācetasam upeyivān, urikrtyātmano dehaṃ rājyam asmai nyavedayat.

#### <span class="box">15.71</span>

sa tāv ākhyāya rāmāya maithileyau tad ātmajau, kaviḥ kāruṇiko vavre sītāyāḥ saṃparigraham.

#### <span class="box">15.72</span>

tāta śuddhā samakṣaṃ naḥ snuṣā te jātavedasi, daurātmyād rakṣasas tāṃ tu nātratyāḥ śraddadhuḥ prajāḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.73</span>

tāḥ svacāritram uddiśya pratyāyayatu maithilī, tataḥ putravatīm enāṃ pratipatsye tadājñayā.

#### <span class="box">15.74</span>

iti pratiśrute rājñā jānakīm āsramān muniḥ, śiṣyair ānāyayām āsa svasiddhiṃ niyamair iva.

#### <span class="box">15.75</span>

anyedyur atha kākutsthaḥ saṃnipātya puraukasaḥ, kavim āhvāyayām āsa prastutapratipattaye.

#### <span class="box">15.76</span>

svarasaṃskāravatyeva putrābhyāṃ saha sītayā, ṛcevodarciṣaṃ sūryaṃ rāmaṃ munir upasthitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.77</span>

kāṣāyaparivītena svapadārpitacakṣuṣā, kavim āhvāyayām āsa śāntena vapuṣaiva sā.

#### <span class="box">15.78</span>

janās tadālokapathāt pratisaṃhṛtacakṣuṣaḥ, tasthus te 'vāṅmukhāḥ sarve phalitā iva sālayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.79</span>

tāṃ dṛṣṭiviṣaye bhartur munir āsthitaviṣṭaraḥ, kuru niḥsaṃśayaṃ vatse svavṛtte lokam ity aśāt.

#### <span class="box">15.80</span>

atha vālmīkśiṣyeṇa puṇyam āvarjitaṃ payaḥ, ācamyodīrayām āsa sītā satyāṃ sarasvatīm.

#### <span class="box">15.81</span>

vāṅmanaḥkarmabhiḥ patyau vyabhicāro yathā na me, tathā viśvaṃbhare devi mām antardhātum arhasi.

#### <span class="box">15.82</span>

evam ukte tayā sādhvyā randhrāt sadyobhavād bhuvaḥ, śātahradam iva jyotiḥ prabhāmaṇḍalam udyayau.

#### <span class="box">15.83</span>

tatra nāgaphaṇotkṣiptasiṃhāsananiṣeduṣī, samudraraśanā sākṣāt prādurāsīd vasuṃdharā.

#### <span class="box">15.84</span>

sā sītām aṅkam āropya bhartari prahitekṣaṇām, mā meti vyāharaty eva tasmin pātālam abhyagāt.

#### <span class="box">15.85</span>

dharāyāṃ tasya saṃrambhaṃ sītāpratyarpaṇaiṣiṇaiḥ, gurur vidhibalāpekṣī śamayāṃ āsa dhanvinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.86</span>

ṛṣīn visṛjya yajñānte suhṛdaś ca puraskṛtān, rāmaḥ sītāgataṃ snehaṃ nidadhe tadapatyayoḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.87</span>

yudhājitas tu saṃdeśāt sa deśa sindhunāmakam, dadau dattaprabhāvāya bharatāya dhṛtaprajaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.88</span>

bharatas tatra gandharvān yudhi nijitya kevalam, ātodyaṃ grāhayām āsa samatyājayad āyudham.

#### <span class="box">15.89</span>

sa takṣapuṣkalau putrau rājadhānyos tadākhyayoḥ, abhiṣicyābhiṣekārhau rāmāntikam agāt punaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.90</span>

aṅgadaṃ candraketuṃ ca lakṣmaṇo 'py ātmasaṃbhavau, śāsanād raghunāthasya cakre kārāpatheśāvarau.

#### <span class="box">15.91</span>

ity āropitaputrās te jananīnāṃ janeśvarāḥ, bhartṛlokaprapannānāṃ nivāpān vidadhuḥ kramāt.

#### <span class="box">15.92</span>

upetya muniveṣo 'tha kālaḥ provāca rāghavam, rahaḥsaṃvādinau pāsyed āvāṃ yas taṃ tyajer iti.

#### <span class="box">15.93</span>

tatheti pratipannāya vivṛtātmā nṛpāya saḥ,  ācakhyau divam adhyāsva śāsanāt parameṣṭhinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.94</span>

vidvān api tayor dvāḥstahaḥ samayaṃ lakṣmaṇo 'bhinat, bhīto durvāsasaḥ śāpād rāmasaṃdarśanārthinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.95</span>

sa gatvā sarayūtīraṃ dehatyāgena yogavit, cakāra vitathāṃ bhrātuḥ pratijñāṃ pūrvajanmanaḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.96</span>

tasminn ātmacaturbhāge prāṅ nākam adhitasthuṣi, rāghavaḥ śithilaṃ tasthau bhuvi dharmas tripād iva.

#### <span class="box">15.97</span>

sa niveśya kuśāvatyāṃ ripunāgāṅkuṣaṃ kuśam, śarāvatyāṃ satāṃ sūktair janitāśrulavaṃ lavam.

#### <span class="box">15.98</span>

udak pratasthe sthiradhīḥ sānujo 'gnipuraḥsaraḥ, anvitaḥ pativātsalyād gṛhavarjam ayodhyayā.

#### <span class="box">15.99</span>

jagṛhus tasya cittajñāḥ padavīṃ harirākṣasāḥ, kadambamukulasthūlair abhivṛṣṭaṃ prajāśrubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">15.100</span>

upasthitavimānena tena bhaktānukampinā, cakre tridivaniḥṣreṇiḥ sarayūr anuyāyinām.

#### <span class="box">15.101</span>

yad gopratarakalpo 'bhut saṃmardas tatra majjatām, atas tadākhyayā tīrthaṃ pāvanaṃ bhuvi paprathe.

#### <span class="box">15.102</span>

sa vibhur vibudhāṃśeṣu pratipannātmamūrtiṣu, tridaśībhūtapaurāṇāṃ svargāntaram akalpayat.

#### <span class="box">15.103</span>

nirvartyaivaṃ daśamukhaśiraśchedakāryaṃ surāṇāṃ viṣvaksenaḥ svatanum aviśat sarvalokapratiṣṭhām, laṅkānāthaṃ pavanatanayaṃ cobhayaṃ sthāpayitvā kīrtistambhadvayam iva girau dakṣiṇe cottare ca.

#### <span class="box">16.1</span>

athetare sapta raghupravīrā jyeṣṭhaṃ purojanmatayā juṇaiś ca, cakruḥ kuśaṃ ratnaviśeṣabhājaṃ saubhrātram eṣāṃ hi kulānusāri.

#### <span class="box">16.2</span>

te setuvārttāgajabandhamukhyair abhyucchritāḥ karmabhir apy avandhyaiḥ, anyonyadeśapravibhāgasīmāṃ velāṃ samudrā iva na vyatīyuḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.3</span>

caturbhujāṃśaprabhavaḥ sa teṣāṃ dānapravṛtter anupāratānām, suradvipānām iva sāmayonir bhinno 'ṣṭhadā viprasasāra vaṃśaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.4</span>

athārdharātre stimitapradīpe śayyāgṛhe suptajane prabuddhaḥ, kuśaḥ pravāsasthakalatraveṣām adṛṣṭapūrvāṃ vanitām apaśyat.

#### <span class="box">16.5</span>

sā sādhusādhāraṇapārthivarddheḥ sthitvā purastāt puruhūtabhāsaḥ, jetuḥ pareṣāṃ jayaśabdapūrvaṃ tasyāñjaliṃ bandhumato babandha.

#### <span class="box">16.6</span>

athānupoḍhārgalam apy agāraṃ chāyām ivādarśatalaṃ praviṣṭām, savismayo dāśarathes tanūjaḥ provāca pūrvārdhaviṣṛṭatalpaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.7</span>

labhdāntarā sāvaraṇe 'pi gehe yogaprabhāvo na ca lakṣyate te, bibharṣi cākāram anirvṛtānāṃ mṛṇālinī haimam ivoparāgam.

#### <span class="box">16.8</span>

kā tvaṃ śubhe kasya parigraho vā kiṃ vā madabhyāgamakāraṇaṃ te, ācakṣva matvā vaśināṃ raghūṇāṃ manaḥ parastrīvimukhapravṛtti.

#### <span class="box">16.9</span>

tam abravīt sā guruṇā navadyā yā nītapaurā svapadonmukhena, tasyāḥ puraḥ saṃprati vītanāthāṃ jānīhi rājann adhidevatāṃ mām.

#### <span class="box">16.10</span>

vasaukasārām abhibhūya sāhaṃ saurājyabaddhotsavayā vibhūtyā, samagraśaktau tvayi sūryavaṃṣye sati prapannā karuṇām avasthām.

#### <span class="box">16.11</span>

viśīrṇatalpāṭṭaśato niveśaḥ paryastaśālaḥ prabhuṇā vinā me, viḍambayaty astanimagnasūryaṃ dināntam ugrānilabhinnamegham.

#### <span class="box">16.12</span>

niśāsu bhāsvatkalanūpurāṇāṃ yaḥ saṃcaro 'bhūd abhisārikāṇām, nadanmukholkāvicitāmiṣābhiḥ sa vāhyate rājapathaḥ śivābhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.13</span>

āsphālitaṃ yat pramadākarāgrair mṛdaṅgadhīradhvanim anvagacchat, vanyair idānīṃ mahiṣais tad ambhaḥ śṛṅgāhataṃ krośati dīrghikāṇām.

#### <span class="box">16.16</span>

citradvipāḥ padmavanāvatīrṇāḥ kareṇubhir dattamṛṇālabhaṅgāḥ, nakhāṅkuśāghātavibhinnakumbhāḥ saṃrabdhasiṃhaprahṛtaṃ vahanti.

#### <span class="box">16.17</span>

stambheṣu yoṣitpratiyātanānām utkrāntavarṇakramadhūsarāṇām, stanottarīyāṇi bhavanti saṅgān nirmokapaṭṭāḥ phaṇibhir vimuktāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.18</span>

kālāntaraśyāmasudheṣu naktam itas tato rūḍhatṛṇāṅkureṣu, ta eva muktāguṇaśuddhayo 'pi harmyeṣu mūrchanti na candrapādāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.19</span>

āvarjya śākhāḥ sadayaṃ ca yāsāṃ puṣpāṇy upāttāni vilāsinībhiḥ, vanyaiḥ pulindair iva vānarais tāḥ kliśyanta udyānalatā madīyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.20</span>

rātrāv anāviṣkṛtadīpabhāsaḥ kāntāmukhaśrīviyutā divāpi, tiraskriyante kṛmitantujālair vicchinnadhūmaprasarā gavākṣāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.21</span>

balikriyāvarjitasaikatāni snānīyasaṃsargam anāpanuvanti, upāntavānīragṛhāṇi dṛṣṭvā śūnyāni dūye sarayūjalāni.

#### <span class="box">16.22</span>

tad arhasīmāṃ vasatiṃ visṛjya mām abhyupaituṃ kularājadhānīm, hitvā tanuṃ kāraṇamānuṣīṃ tāṃ yathā gurus te paramātmamūrtim.

#### <span class="box">16.23</span>

tatheti tasyāḥ praṇayaṃ pratītaḥ pratyagrahīt prāgraharo raghūṇām, pūr apy abhivyaktamukhaprasādā śarīrabandhena tirobabhūva.

#### <span class="box">16.24</span>

tad adbhutaṃ saṃsadi rārtrivṛttaṃ prātar dvijebhyo nṛpatiḥ śaśaṃsa, śrutvā ta enaṃ kularājadhānyā sākṣāt patitve vṛtam abhayanandan.

#### <span class="box">16.25</span>

kuśāvatīṃ śrotriyasāt sa kṛtvā yātrānukūle 'hani sāvarodhaḥ, anudruto vāyur ivābhravṛndaiḥ sainyair ayodhyābhimukhaḥ pratasthe.

#### <span class="box">16.26</span>

sā ketumālopavanā bṛhadbhir vihāraśailānugateva nāgaiḥ, senā rathodāragṛhā prayāṇe tasyābhavaj jaṅgamarājadhānī.

#### <span class="box">16.27</span>

tenātapatrāmalamaṇḍalena prasthāpitaḥ pūrvanivāsabhūmim, babhau balaughaḥ śaśinoditena velām udanvān iva nīyamānaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.28</span>

tasya prayātasya varūthinīnāṃ pīḍām aparyāptavatīva soḍhum, vasuṃdharā viṣṇupadaṃ dvitīyam adhyāruroheva rajaśchalena.

#### <span class="box">16.29</span>

udyacchamānā gamanāya paścāt puro niveśe pathi ca vrajantī, sā yatra senā dadṛṣe nṛpasya tatraiva sāmagryamatiṃ cakāra.

#### <span class="box">16.30</span>

tasya dvipānāṃ madavārisekāt khurābhighātāc ca turaṃgamāṇām, reṇuḥ prapede pathi paṅkabhāvaṃ paṅko 'pi reṇutvam iyāya netuḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.31</span>

mārgaiṣiṇī sā kaṭakāntareṣu vaindhyeṣu senā bahudhā vibhinnā, cakāra reveva mahāvirāvā baddhapratiśrunti guhāmukhāni.

#### <span class="box">16.32</span>

sa dhātubhedāruṇayānanemiḥ prabhuḥ prayāṇadhvanimiśratūryaḥ, vyalaṅghayad vindhyam upāyanāni paśyan pulindair upapāditāni.

#### <span class="box">16.33</span>

tīrthe tadīye gajasetubandhāt pratīpagām uttarato 'sya gaṅgām, ayatnavālagvyajanībabhūvur haṃsā nabholaṅghanalolakpakṣāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.34</span>

sa pūrvajānāṃ kapilena roṣād bhasmāvaśeṣīkṛtavigrahāṇām, surālayaprāptinimittam ambhas traisrotasaṃ naululitaṃ vavande.

#### <span class="box">16.35</span>

ity adhvanaḥ kaiścid ahobhir ante kūlaṃ samāsādya kuśaḥ sarayvāḥ, vedipratiṣṭhān vitatādhvarāṇāṃ yūpān apaśyac chataśo raghūṇām.

#### <span class="box">16.36</span>

ādhūya śākhāḥ kusumadrumāṇāṃ spṛṣṭvā ca śītān sarayūtaraṅgān, taṃ klāntasainyaṃ kularājadhānyāḥ pratyujjagāmopavanāntavāyuḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.37</span>

athopaśalye ripumagnaśalyas tasyāḥ puraḥ paursakhaḥ sa rājā, kuladhvajas tāni caladhvajāni niveśayām āsa balī balāni.

#### <span class="box">16.38</span>

tāṃ śilpisaṃghāḥ prabhuṇā niyuktās tathāgatāṃ saṃbhṛtasādhanatvāt, puraṃ navīcakrur apāṃ visargān meghā nidāghaglapitām ivorvīm.

#### <span class="box">16.39</span>

tataḥ saparyāṃ sapaśūpahārāṃ puraḥ parārdhyapratimāgṛhāyāḥ, upoṣitair vāstuvidhānavidbhir nirvartayām āsa raghupavīraḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.40</span>

tasyāḥ sa rājopapadaṃ niśāntaṃ kāmīva kāntāhṛdayaṃ praviśya, yathārham anyair anujīvilokaṃ saṃbhāvayām āsa gṛhais tadīyaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.41</span>

sā mandurāsaṃśrayibhis turaṃgaiḥ śālāvidhistambhagataiś ca nāgaiḥ, pūr ābabhāse vipaṇisthapaṇyā sarvāṅganaddhābharaṇeva nārī.

#### <span class="box">16.42</span>

vasan sa tasyāṃ vasatau raghūṇāṃ purāṇaśobhām adhiropitāyām, na maithileyaḥ spṛhayāṃ babhūva bhartre divo nāpy alakeśvarāya.

#### <span class="box">16.43</span>

athāsya ratnagrathitottarīyam ekāntapāṇḍustanalambihāram, niḥśvāsahāryāṃśukam ājagāma gharmaḥ priyā veṣam ivopadeṣṭum.

#### <span class="box">16.44</span>

agastyacihnād ayanāt samīpaṃ dig uttarā bhāsvati saṃnivṛtte, ānandaśītam iva bhāṣpavṛṣṭiṃ himasrutiṃ haimavatīṃ sasarja.

#### <span class="box">16.45</span>

pravṛddhatāpo divaso 'timātram atyartham eva kṣaṇadā ca tanvī, ubhau virodhakriyayā vibhinnau jāyāpatī sānuśayāv ivāstām.

#### <span class="box">16.46</span>

dine dine śaivalavanty adhastāt sopānaparvāṇi vimuñcad ambhaḥ, uddaṇḍapadmaṃ gṛhadīrghikāṇāṃ nārīnitambadvayasaṃ babhūva.

#### <span class="box">16.47</span>

vaneṣu sāyanatanamallikānāṃ vijṛmbhaṇodgandhiṣu kuḍ maleṣu, pratyekanikṣiptapadaḥ saśabdaṃ saṃkhyām ivaiṣāṃ bhramaraś cakāra.

#### <span class="box">16.48</span>

svedānuviddhārdranakhakṣatāṅke saṃdaṣṭabhūyiṣṭhaśikhaṃ kapole, cyutaṃ na karṇād api kāminīnāṃ śirīṣapuṣpaṃ sahasā papāta.

#### <span class="box">16.49</span>

yantrapravāhaiḥ śiśiraiḥ parītān rasena dhautān malayodbhavasya, śilāviśeṣān adhiśayya ninyur dhārāgṛheṣv ātapam ṛddhimantaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.50</span>

snānārdramukteṣv anudhūpavāsaṃ vinyastasāyantanamallikeṣu, kāmo vasantātyayamandavīryaḥ keśeṣu lebhe balam aṅganānām.

#### <span class="box">16.51</span>

āpiñjarā baddharajaḥkaṇatvān mañjary udārāśuśubhe 'rjunasya, dagdhvāpi dehaṃ giriśena roṣāt khaṇḍīkṛtā jyeva manobhvasya.

#### <span class="box">16.52</span>

manojñagandhaṃ sahakārabhaṅgaṃ purāṇasīdhuṃ navapāṭalaṃ ca, saṃbadhnatā kāijaneṣu doṣāḥ sarve nidāghāvadhinā pramṛṣṭāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.53</span>

janasya tasmin samaye vigāḍhe babhūvatur dvau saviśeṣakāntau, tāpāpanodakṣamapāda sa codayastho nṛpatiḥ śaśī ca.

#### <span class="box">16.54</span>

athormilolonmadarājahaṃse rodholatāpuṣpavahe sarayvāḥ, vihartum icchā vanitāsakhasya tasyāmbhasi grīṣmasukhe babhūva.

#### <span class="box">16.55</span>

sa tīrabhūmau vihitopakāryām ānāyibhis tām apakṛṣṭanakrām, vigāhituṃ śrīmahimānurūpaṃ pracakrame cakradharaprabhāvaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.56</span>

sā tīrasopānapathāvatārād anyonyakeyūravighaṭṭinībhiḥ, sanūpurakṣobhapadābhir āsīd udvignahaṃsā sarid aṅganābhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.57</span>

parasparābhyukṣaṇatatparāṇāṃ tāsāṃ nṛpo majjanarāgadarśī, nausaṃśrayaḥ pārśvagatāṃ kirātīm upāttavālavyajanāṃ babhāṣe.

#### <span class="box">16.58</span>

paśyāvarodhaiḥ śataśo madīyair vigāhyamāno galitāṅgarāgaiḥ, saṃdhyodayaḥ sābhra ivaiṣa varṇaṃ puṣyaty anekaṃ sarayūpravāhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.59</span>

viluptam antaḥpurasundarīṇāṃ yad añjanaṃ naululitābhir adbhiḥ, tad badhnatībhir madarāgaśobhāṃ vilocaneṣu pratimuktam āsām.

#### <span class="box">16.60</span>

etā guruśroṇipayodharatvād ātmānam udvohuḍhum aśaknuvantyaḥ, gāḍhāṅgadair bāhubhir aspu bālāḥ kleśottaraṃ rāgavaśāt plavante.

#### <span class="box">16.61</span>

amī śirīṣaprasavāvataṃsāḥ prabhraṃśino vārivihāriṇīnām, pāriplavāḥ srotasi nimnagāyāḥ śaivālalolāṃś chalayanti mīnān.

#### <span class="box">16.62</span>

āsāṃ jalāsphālanatatparāṇāṃ muktāphalaspardhiṣu śīkareṣu, payodharotsarpiṣu śīryamāṇāḥ saṃlakṣyate na cchiduro 'pi hāraḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.63</span>

āvartaśobhā natanābhikānter bhaṅgyo bhruvāṃ dvandvacarāḥstanānām, jātāni rūpāvayavopamānāny adūravartīni vilāsinīnām.

#### <span class="box">16.64</span>

tīrasthalībarhibhir utkalāpaiḥ prasnigdhakekair abhinandyamānam, śrotreṣu saṃmūrchati raktam āsāṃ gītānugaṃ vārimṛdaṅgavādyam.

#### <span class="box">16.65</span>

saṃdaṣṭavastreṣv abalānitambeṣv induprakāśāntaritoḍukalpāḥ, amī jalāpūritasūtramārgā maunaṃ bhajante raśanākalāpāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.66</span>

etāḥ karotpīḍitavāridhārā darpāt sakhībhir vadaneṣu siktāḥ, vakretarāgrair alakais taruṇyaś cūrṇāruṇān vārilavān vamanti.

#### <span class="box">16.67</span>

udbaddhakeśaś cyutapattrarekho viśleṣimuktāphalapattraveṣṭaḥ, manojña eva pramadāmukhānām ambhovihārākulito 'pi veṣaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.68</span>

sa nauvimānād avatīrya reme vilolahāraḥ saha tābhir apsu, skandhāvalagnoddhṛtapadminīkaḥ kareṇubhir vanya iva dvipendraḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.69</span>

tato nṛpenānugatāḥ striyas tā bhrājiṣṇunā sātiśayaṃ virejuḥ, prāg eva muktā nayanābhirāmāḥ prāpyendranīlaṃ kim utonmayūkham.

#### <span class="box">16.70</span>

varṇodakaiḥ kāñcanaśṛṅgamuktais tam āyatākṣyaḥ praṇayād asiñcan, tathāgataḥ so 'tirarāṃ babhāse sadhātunisyanda ivādrirājaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.71</span>

tenāvarodhapramadāsakhena vigāhanānena saridvarāṃ tām, ākāśagaṅgāratir apsarobhir vṛto marutvān anuyātalīlaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.72</span>

yat kumbhayoner adigamya rāmaḥ kuśāya rājyena samaṃ dideśa, tad asya jaitrābharaṇaṃ vihartur ajñātapātaṃ salile mamajja.

#### <span class="box">16.73</span>

snātvā yathākāmam asau sadāras tīropakāryāṃ gatamātra eva, divyena śūnyaṃ valayena bāhum upoḍhanepathyavidhir dadarśa.

#### <span class="box">16.74</span>

jayaśriyaḥ saṃvananaṃ yatas tad āmuktapūrvaṃ guruṇā ca yasmāt, sehe 'sya na bhraṃśam ato na lobhāt sa tulyapuṣpābharaṇo hi dhīraḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.75</span>

tataḥ samājñāpayad āśu sarvān ānāyinas tadvicaye nadīṣṇān, vandhyaśramās te sarayūṃ vigāhya tam ūcur āmlānamukhaprasādāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.76</span>

kṛtaḥ prayatno na ca deva labdhaṃ magnaṃ payasy ābharaṇottamaṃ te, nāgena laulyāt kumudena nūnam upāttam antarhradavāsinā tat.

#### <span class="box">16.77</span>

tataḥ sa kṛtvā dhanur ātatajyaṃ dhanurdharaḥ kopavilohitākṣaḥ, gārutmataṃ tīragatas tarasvī bhujaṃganāśāya samādade 'stram.

#### <span class="box">16.78</span>

tasmin hradaḥ saṃhitamātra eva kṣobhāt samāviddhataraṅgahastaḥ, rodhāṃsy abhighnann avapātamagnaḥ karīva vanyaḥ paruṣaṃ rarāsa.

#### <span class="box">16.79</span>

tasmāt samudrād iva mathyamānād udvṛttanakrāt sahasonmamajja, lakṣmyeva sārdhaṃ surarājavṛkṣaḥ kanyāṃ puraskṛtya bhujaṃgarājaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.80</span>

vibhūṣaṇapratyupahārahastam upasthitaṃ vīkṣya viśāṃpatis tam, sauparṇam astraṃ pratisaṃjahāra praheṣv anirbandharuṣo hi santaḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.81</span>

trailokyanāthaprabhavaṃ prabhāvāt kuśaṃ dviṣām aṅkuśam astravidvān, mānonantenāpy abhivandya mūrdhnā mūrdhābhiṣiktaṃ kumudo babhāṣe.

#### <span class="box">16.82</span>

avaimi kāryāntaramānuṣasya viṣṇoḥ sutākhyām aparāṃ tanuṃ tvām, so 'haṃ kathaṃ nāma tavācareyam ārādhanīyasya dhṛter vibhātam.

#### <span class="box">16.83</span>

karābhighātotthitakandukeyam ālokya bālātikutūhalena, javāt pataj jyotir ivāntarikṣād ādatta jatrābharaṇaṃ tvadīyam.

#### <span class="box">16.84</span>

tad etad ājānuvilambinā te jyāghātarekhākiṇa lāñchanena, bhujena rakṣāparigheṇa bhūmer upaitu yogaṃ punar aṃsalena.

#### <span class="box">16.85</span>

imāṃ svasāraṃ ca yavīyasīṃ me kumudvatīṃ nārhasi nānumantum, ātmāparādhaṃ nudatīṃ cirāya śuśrūṣayā pārthiva pādayos te.

#### <span class="box">16.86</span>

ity ūcivān upahṛtābharaṇaḥ kṣitīśaṃ ślāghyo bhavān svajana ity anubhāṣitāram, saṃyojayāṃ vidhivad āsa sametabandhuḥ kanyāmayena kumudaḥ kulabhūṣaṇena.

#### <span class="box">16.87</span>

tasyāḥ spṛṣṭe manujapatinā sāhacaryāya haste māṅgalyorṇāvalayini puraḥ pāvakasyocchikhasya, divyas tūryadhvanir udacarad vyaśnuvāno digantān gandhodagraṃ tadanau vavṛṣuḥ puṣpam āścaryameghāḥ.

#### <span class="box">16.88</span>

itthaṃ nāgas tribhuvanaguror aurasaṃ maithileyaṃ labdhvā bandhuṃ tam api ca kuśaḥ pañcamaṃ takṣakasya, ekaḥ śaṅkāṃ pitṛvadharipor atyajad vainateyāc chāntavyālām avanim aparaḥ paurakāntaḥ śaśāsa.

  |

#### <span class="box">17.1</span>

aithiṃ nāma kākutsthāt putraṃ āpakumudvatī, paścimād yāminīyāmāt prasādam iva cetanā.

#### <span class="box">17.2</span>

sa pituḥ pitṛmān vaṃśaṃ putraṃ āpakumudvatī, apunāt savitevobhau mārgāv uttaradakṣiṇau.

#### <span class="box">17.3</span>

tam ādau kulavidyānām artham arthavidāṃ varaḥ, paścāt pārthivakanyānāṃ pāṇim agrāhayat pitā.

#### <span class="box">17.4</span>

jātyas tenābhijātena śūraḥ śauryavatā kuśaḥ, amanyataikam ātmānam anekaṃ vaśinā vaśī.

#### <span class="box">17.5</span>

sa kulocitam indrasya sāhāyakam upeyivān, jaghāna samare daityaṃ durjayaṃ tena so 'vadhi.

#### <span class="box">17.6</span>

taṃ svasā nāgarājasya kumudasya kumudvatī, anvagāt kumudānandaṃ śaśāṅkam iva kaumudī.

#### <span class="box">17.7</span>

tayor divaspater āsīd ekaḥ siṃhāsanārdhabāk, dvitīyāpi sakhī śacyāḥ pārijātāṃśabhāginī.

#### <span class="box">17.8</span>

tadātmasaṃbhavaṃ rājye mantrivṛddāḥ samādadhuḥ, smarantaḥ paścimām ājñāṃ bhartuḥ saṃgrāmayāyinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.9</span>

te tasya kalpayām āsur abhiṣekāya śilpibhiḥ, vimānaṃ navam udvedi catuḥstambhapratiṣṭam.

#### <span class="box">17.10</span>

tatrainaṃ hemakumbheṣu saṃbhṛtais tīrthavāribhiḥ, upatasthuḥ prakṛtayo bhadrapīṭhopaveśitam.

#### <span class="box">17.11</span>

nadadhbiḥ snigdhagambhīraṃ tūryair āhatapuṣkaraiḥ, anvamīyata kalyāṇaṃ tasyāvicchinnasaṃtati.

#### <span class="box">17.12</span>

dūrvāyavāṅkuraplakṣatvagabhinnapuṭottarān, jñātivṛddhaiḥ prayuktān sa bheje nīrājanāvidhīn.

#### <span class="box">17.13</span>

purohitapurogās taṃ jiṣṇuṃ jaitrair atharvabhiḥ, upacakramire pūrvam abhiṣektuṃ dvijātayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.14</span>

tasyaughamahatī mūrdhni nipatantī vyarocata, saśabdam abhiṣekaśrīr gaṅgeva tripuradviṣaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.15</span>

stūyamānaḥ kṣaṇe tasminn alakṣyata sa bandibhiḥ, pravṛddha iva prajanyaḥ cātakair abhinanditaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.16</span>

tasya san mantrapūtābhiḥ snānam adbhiḥ pratīcchataḥ, vavṛdhe vaidyutasyāgner vṛṣṭisekād iva dyutiḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.17</span>

sa tāvad abhiṣekānte snātakebhyo dadau vasu, yāvat teṣāṃ samāpyeran yajñāḥ paryāptadakṣiṇāḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.18</span>

te prītamanasas tasmai yām āśiṣam udīrayan, sā tasya karmanirvṛttair dūraṃ paścātkṛtā phalaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.19</span>

bandhacchedaṃ sa baddhānāṃ vadhārhāṇām avadhyatām, dhuryāṇāṃ ca dhuro mokṣam adohaṃ cādiṣad gavām.

#### <span class="box">17.20</span>

krīḍāpatatriṇo 'py asya pañjarasthāḥ śukādayaḥ, labdhamokṣās tadādeśād yatheṣṭagatayo 'bhavan.

#### <span class="box">17.21</span>

tataḥ kakṣāntaranyastaṃ gajadantāsanaṃ śuci, sottaracchadam adhyāsta nepathyagrahaṇāya saḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.22</span>

taṃ dhūpāśyānakeśāntaṃ toyanirṇiktapāṇayaḥ, ākalpasādhanais tais tair upaseduḥ prasādhakāḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.23</span>

te' sya muktāguṇonnaddhaṃ maulim antargatasrajam, pratyūpuḥ padmarāgeṇa prabhāmaṇḍalaśobhinā.

#### <span class="box">17.24</span>

candanenāṅgarāgaṃ ca mṛganābhisugandhinā, samāpayya tataś cakruḥ pattraṃ vinyastarocanam.

#### <span class="box">17.25</span>

āmuktābharaṇaḥ sragvī haṃsacihnadukūlavān, āsīd atiśayaprekṣyaḥ sa rājyaśrīvadhūvaraḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.26</span>

nepathyadarśinaś chāyā tasyādarśe hiraṇmaye, virarājodite sūrye merau kalpataror iva.

#### <span class="box">17.27</span>

sa rājakakudavyagrapāṇibhiḥ pārśvavaribhiḥ, yayāv udīritālokaḥ sudharmānavamāṃ sabhām.

#### <span class="box">17.28</span>

vitānasahitaṃ tatra bheje paitṛkam āsanam, cūḍāmaṇibhir udghṛṣṭapādapīṭhaṃ mahīkṣitām.

#### <span class="box">17.29</span>

śuśubhe tena cākrāntaṃ maṅgalāyatanaṃ mahat, śrīvatsalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣaḥ kaustubheneva kaiśavam.

#### <span class="box">17.30</span>

babhau bhūyaḥ kumāratvād ādhirājyam avāpya saḥ, rekhā bhāvād upārūḍhaḥ sāmagryam iva candramāḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.31</span>

prasannamukharāgaṃ taṃ smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇam, mūrtimantam amanyanta viśvāsam anujīvinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.32</span>

sa puraṃ puruhūtaśrīḥ kalpadrumanibhadhvajām, kramamāṇaś cakāra dyāṃ nāgenairāvataujasā.

#### <span class="box">17.33</span>

tasyaikasyocchritaṃ chattraṃ mūrdhni tenāmalatviṣā, pūrvarājaviyogauṣmyaṃ kṛtsnasya jagato hṛtam.

#### <span class="box">17.34</span>

dhūmād agneḥ śikhāḥ paścād udayād aṃśavo raveḥ, so 'tītya tejasāṃ vṛttiṃ samam evotthito guṇaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.35</span>

taṃ prītiviśadair netrair anvayuḥ paurayoṣitaḥ, śaratprasannair jyotirbhir vibhāvarya iva dhruvam.

#### <span class="box">17.36</span>

ayodhyādevatāś cainaṃ praśastāyatanārcitāḥ, anudadhyur anudhyeyaṃ sāṃnidhyaiḥ pratimāgataiḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.37</span>

yāvan nāśyāyate vedir abhiṣekajalāplutā, tāvad evāsya velāntaṃ pratāpaḥ prāpa duḥsahaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.38</span>

vasiṣṭhasya guror mantrāḥ sāyakās tasya dhanvinaḥ, kiṃ tat sādhyaṃ yad ubhaye sādhayeyur na saṃgatāḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.39</span>

sa dharmasthasakhaḥ śaśvad arthipratyarthināṃ svayam, dadarśa saṃśayacchedyān vyavahārān atandritaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.40</span>

tataḥ param abhivyaktāsaumanasyaniveditaiḥ, yuyoja pākābhimukhair bhṛtyān vijñāpanāphalaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.41</span>

prajās tadguruṇā nadyo nabhaseva vivardhitāḥ, tasmiṃs tu bhūyasīṃ vṛddhiṃ nabhasye tā ivāyayuḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.42</span>

yad uvāca na tan mithyā yad dadau na jahāra tat, so 'bhūd bhagnavrataḥ śatrūn uddhṛtya pratiropayan.

#### <span class="box">17.43</span>

vayorūpavibhūtīnām ekaikaṃ madakāraṇam, tāni tasmin samastāni na tasyotsiṣice manaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.44</span>

itthaṃ janitarāgāsu prakṛtiṣv anuvāsaram, akṣobhyaḥ sa navo 'py āsīd dṛḍhamūla iva drumaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.45</span>

anityāḥ śatravo bāhyā viprakṛṣṭāś ca te yataḥ, ataḥ so 'bhyantarān nityān ṣaṭ pūrvam ajayad ripūn.

#### <span class="box">17.46</span>

prasādābhimukhe tasmiṃś capalāpi svabhāvataḥ, nikaṣe hemarekheva śrīr āsīd anapāyinī.

#### <span class="box">17.47</span>

kātaryaṃ kevalā nītiḥ śauryaṃ śvāpadaceṣṭitam, ataḥ siddhiṃ sametābhyām ubhābhyām anviyeṣa saḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.48</span>

na tasya maṇḍale rājño nyastapraṇidhidīdhiteḥ, adṛṣṭam abhavat kiṃcid vyabhrasyeva vivasvataḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.49</span>

rātriṃdivavibhāgeṣu yad ādiṣṭaṃ mahīkṣitām, tat siṣeve niyogena sa vikalpaparāṅmukhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.50</span>

mantraḥ pratidinaṃ tasya babhūva saha mantribhiḥ, sa jātu sevyamāno 'pi guptadvāro na sūcyate.

#### <span class="box">17.51</span>

pareṣu sveṣu ca kṣiptair avijñātaparasparaiḥ, so 'pasarpair jajāgāra yathākālaṃ svapann api.

#### <span class="box">17.52</span>

durgāṇi durgrhāṇy āsaṃs tasya roddhur api dviṣām, na hi siṃho gajāskandī bhayād giriguhāśayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.53</span>

bahvyamukhyāḥ samārambhāḥ pratyavekṣyā niratyayāḥ, garbhaśālisadharmāṇas tasya gūḍhaṃ vipecire.

#### <span class="box">17.54</span>

apathena pravavṛte na jātūpacito 'pi saḥ, vṛddhau nadīmukhenaiva prasthānaṃ lavaṇāmbhasaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.55</span>

kāmaṃ pratkṛtivairāgyaṃ sadyaḥ śamayituṃ kṣamaḥ, yasya kāryaḥ pratīkāraḥ sa tan naivodapādayat.

#### <span class="box">17.56</span>

śakeṣv evābhavad yātrā tasya śaktimataḥ sataḥ, samīraṇasahāyo 'pi nāmbhaḥprārthī davānalaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.57</span>

na dharmam arthakāmābhyāṃ babādhe na ca tena tau, nārthaṃ kāmena kāmaṃ vā so 'rthena sadṛśas triṣu.

#### <span class="box">17.58</span>

hīnāny anupakartḥṇi pravṛddhāni vikurvate, tena madhyamaśaktīni mitrāṇi shtāpitāny ataḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.59</span>

parātmanoḥ paricchidya śaktyādīnāṃ balābalam, yayāv ebhir baliṣṭhaś cet parasmād āsta so 'nyathā.

#### <span class="box">17.60</span>

kośenāśrayaṇīyatvam iti tasyārthasaṃgrahaḥ, ambugarbho hi jīmūtaś cātakair abhinandyate.

#### <span class="box">17.61</span>

parakarmāpahaḥ so 'bhūd udyataḥ sveṣu karmasu, āvṛṇod ātmano randhraṃ randhreṣu praharan ripūn.

#### <span class="box">17.62</span>

pitrā saṃvardhito nityaṃ kṛtāstraḥ sāṃparāyikaḥ, tasya daṇḍavato daṇḍaḥ svadehān na vyaśiṣyata.

#### <span class="box">17.63</span>

sarpasyeva śiroratnaṃ nāsya śaktitrayaṃ paraḥ, sa cakarṣa parasmāt tad ayaskānta ivāyasam.

#### <span class="box">17.64</span>

vāpīṣv iva sravantīṣu vaneṣūpavaneṣv iva, sārthāḥ svairaṃ svakīyeṣu cerur veśmasv ivādriṣu.

#### <span class="box">17.65</span>

tapo rakṣan sa vighnebhyas taskarebhyaś ca saṃpadaḥ, yathāsvam āśramaiś cakre varṇair api ṣaḍsaṃśabhāk.

#### <span class="box">17.66</span>

khanibhiḥ suṣuve ratnaṃ kṣetraiḥ sasyaṃ vanair gajān, dideśa vetanaṃ tasmai rakṣāsadṛśam eva bhūḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.67</span>

sa guṇānāṃ balānāṃ ca ṣaṇṇāṃ ṣaṇmukhavikramaḥ, babhūva viniyogajñaḥ sādhanīyeṣu vastuṣu.

#### <span class="box">17.68</span>

iti kramāt prayuñjāno rāja nītiṃ caturvidhām, ā tīrthād apratīghātaṃ sa tasyāḥ phalam ānaśe.

#### <span class="box">17.69</span>

kūṭayuddhavidhijñe 'pi tasmin sanmārgayodhini, bheje 'bhisārikāvṛttiṃ jayaśrīr vīragāminī.

#### <span class="box">17.70</span>

prāyaḥ pratāpabhagnatvād arīṇāṃ tasya durlabhaḥ, raṇo gandhavipasyeva gandhabhinnānyadantinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.71</span>

pravṛddhau hīyate candraḥ samudro 'pi tathāvidhaḥ, sa tu tasamavṛddhiś ca na cābhūt tāv iva kṣayī.

#### <span class="box">17.72</span>

santas tasyābhigamanād atyarthaṃ mahataḥ kṛṣāḥ, udadher iva jīmūtāḥ prāpur dātṛtvam arthinaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.73</span>

stūyamānaḥ sa jihrāya stutyam eva samācaran, tathāpi vavṛdhe tasya tatkāridveṣino yaśaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.74</span>

duritaṃ darśanena ghnaṃs tattvārthena nudaṃs tamaḥ, prajāḥ svatantrayāṃ cakre śaśvat sūrya ivoditaḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.75</span>

indor agatayaḥ padme sūryasya kumude 'ṃśavaḥ, guṇās tasya vipakṣe 'pi guṇino lebhire 'ntaram.

#### <span class="box">17.76</span>

parābhisaṃdhānaparaṃ yady apy asya viceṣṭitam, jigīṣor aśvamedhāya dharmyam eva babhūva tat.

#### <span class="box">17.77</span>

evam udyan prabhāveṇa śāstgranirdiṣṭavartmanā, vṛṣeva devo devānāṃ rājñāṃ rājā babhūva saḥ.

#### <span class="box">17.78</span>

pañcamaṃ lokapālānāṃ tam ūcuḥ sāmyayogataḥ, bhūtānāṃ mahatām ṣaṣṭham aṣṭamaṃ kulabhūbhṛtām.

#### <span class="box">17.79</span>

dūrāpavarjitacchattrais tasyājñāṃ śāsanārpitām, dadhuḥ śirobhir bhūpālā devaḥ pauraṃdarīm iva.

#### <span class="box">17.80</span>

ṛtvijaḥ sa tathānarca dakṣiṇābhir mahākratau, yathā sādhāraṇībhūtaṃ nāmāsya dhanadasya ca.

#### <span class="box">17.81</span>

indrād vṛṣṭir niyamitagadodrekavṛttir yamo 'bhūd yādonāthaḥ śivajalapathaḥ karmaṇe naucarāṇām, pūrvāpekṣī tadanu vidadhe kośavṛddhiṃ kuberas tasmin daṇḍopanatacaritaṃ bhejire lokapālāḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.1</span>

sa naiṣadhasyārthapateḥ sutāyām utpādayām āsa niṣiddhaśatruḥ, anūnasāraṃ niṣadhān nagendrāt putraṃ yam āhur niṣadhākhyam eva.

#### <span class="box">18.2</span>

tenoruvīryeṇa pitā prajāyai kalpiṣyamāṇena nananda yūnā, suvṛṣtiyogād iva jīvalokaḥ sasyena saṃpattiphalātmakena.

#### <span class="box">18.3</span>

śabdādi nirviśya sukhaṃ cirāya tasmin pratiṣṭhāpitarājaśabdaḥ, kaumudvateyaḥ kumudāvadātair dyām arjitāṃ karmabhir āruroha.

#### <span class="box">18.4</span>

pautraḥ kuśasyāpi kuśeśayākṣaḥ sasāgarāṃ sāgaradhīracetāḥ, ekātapoatrāṃ bhuvam ekavīraḥ purārgalādīrghabhujo bubhoja.
#### <span class="box">18.5</span>

tasyānalaujās tanayas tadante vaṃśaśriyaṃ prāpa nalābhidhānaḥ, yo naḍvalānīva gajaḥ pareṣāṃ balāny amṛdnān nalinābhavaktraḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.6</span>

nabhaścarair gītayaśyāmatanuṃ tanūjam nabhastalaśyāmatanuṃ tanūjam, khyātaṃ nabhaḥśabdamayena nāmnā kāntaṃ nabhomāsam iva prajānām.

#### <span class="box">18.7</span>

tasmai viṣrjyottarakosalānāṃ dharmottaras tat prabhave prabhutvam, mṛgair ajaryaṃ jaraspodaiṣṭam adehabandhāya punar babandha.

#### <span class="box">18.8</span>

tena dvipānām iva puṇḍarīko rājñām ajayyo 'jani puṇḍarīkaḥ, śānte pitary āhṛtapuṇḍarīkā yaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam ivāśritā śrīḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.9</span>

sa kṣemadhanvānam amoghadhanvā putraṃ prajākṣemavidhānadakṣam, kṣmāṃ lambhayitvā kṣamayopapannaṃ vane tapaḥ kṣāntataraś cacāra.

#### <span class="box">18.10</span>

anīkinīnāṃ samare 'grayāyī tasyāpi devapratimaḥ suto 'bhūt, vyaśrūyatānīkapadāvasānaṃ devādi nāma tridive 'pi yasya.

#### <span class="box">18.11</span>

pitā samārādhanatatpareṇa putreṇa putrī sa yathaiva tena, putras tathaivādhikavatsalena sa tena pitrā pitṛmān babhūva.

#### <span class="box">18.12</span>

pūrvas tayor ātmasame ciroḍhām ātmodbhave varṇacatuṣṭayasya, dhuraṃ nidhāyaikanidhir guṇānām jagāma yajvā yajamānalokam.

#### <span class="box">18.13</span>

vaśī sutas tasya vaśaṃvadatvāt sveṣām ivāsīd dviṣatām apīṣṭaḥ, sakṛd (?) vivignān api hi prayuktaṃ mādhuryam īṣṭe hariṇān grahītum.

#### <span class="box">18.14</span>

ahīnagur nāma sa gāṃ samagrām ahīnabāhudraviṇaḥ śaśāsa, yo hīna saṃsargaparāṅmukhatvād mādhuryam īṣṭe hariṇān grahītum.

#### <span class="box">18.15</span>

guroḥ sa cānantaram antarjñaḥ puṃsāṃ pumān ādya ivāvatīrṇaḥ, upakramair askhalitaiś caturbhiś caturdigīśaś caturo babhūva.

#### <span class="box">18.16</span>

tasmin prayāte paralokayātrāṃ jetary arīṇāṃ tanayaṃ tadīyam, uccaiḥśirastvāj jitapāriyātraṃ lakṣmīḥ siṣeve kila pāriyātram.

#### <span class="box">18.17</span>

tasyābhavat sūnur udāraśīlaḥ śilaḥ śilāpaṭṭaviśālavakṣāḥ, jitāripakṣo 'pi śilīmukhair yaḥ śālīnatām avrajad īḍyamānaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.18</span>

tam ātmasaṃpannam aninditātmā kṛtvā yuvānaṃ yuvarājam eva, sukhāni so 'bhuṅkta sukhoparodhi vṛttaṃ hi rājñām uparuddhavṛttam.

#### <span class="box">18.19</span>

taṃ rāgabandhiṣv avitṛptam eva bhogeṣu saubhāgyaviśeṣabhogyam, vilāsinīnām aratikṣamāpi jarā vṛthā matsariṇī jahāra.

#### <span class="box">18.20</span>

unnābha ity udagtasnāmadheyas tasyāyathārthonnatanābhirandhraḥ, suto 'bhavat paṅkajanābhakalpaḥ kṛtsnasya nābhir nṛpamaṇḍalasya.

#### <span class="box">18.21</span>

tataḥ paraṃ vajradharaprabhāvas tadātmajaḥ saṃyati vajraghoṣaḥ, babhūva vajrākarabhuṣaṇāyāḥ patiḥ pṛthivyāḥ kila vajranābhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.22</span>

tasmin gate dyāṃ sukṛtopalabdhāṃ tatsaṃbhavaṃ śaṅkhaṇam arṇavāntā, utkhātaśatruṃ vasudhopatasthe ratnopahārair uditaiḥ khanibhyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.23</span>

tasyāvasāne haridaśvadhāmā pitryaṃ prapede padam aśvirūpaḥ, velātaṭeṣūṣitasainikāśvaṃ purāvido yaṃ dhyuṣitāśvam āhuḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.24</span>

ārādhya viśveśvaram īśvareṇa tena kṣiter viśvasaho 'dhijajñe, pātuṃ saho viśvasakhaḥ samagrāṃ viśvaṃbharām ātmajamūrtir ātmā.

#### <span class="box">18.25</span>

aṃśe hiraṇyākśaripoḥ sa jāte hiraṇyanābhe tanaye nayajñaḥ, dviṣām asahyaḥ sutarāṃ tarūṇāṃ hiraṇyaretā sānilo 'bhūt.

#### <span class="box">18.26</span>

pitā pitḥṇām anṛṇas tam ante vayasy anantāni sukhāni lipsuḥ, rājānam ājānuvilambibāhuṃ kṛtvā kṛtī valkalavān babhūva.

#### <span class="box">18.27</span>

kausalya ity uttarakosalānāṃ patyuḥ pataṃgānvayabhūṣaṇasya, tasyaurasaḥ somasutaḥ suto 'bhūn netrotsavaḥ soma iva dvitīyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.28</span>

kausalya ity uttarakosalānāṃ sa brahmabhūyaṃ gatim ājagāma, brahmiṣṭham ādhāya nije 'dhikāre brahmiṣṭham eva svatanuprasūtam.

#### <span class="box">18.29</span>

yaśobhir ābrahmasabhaṃ prakāśaḥ samyag mahīṃ śāsati śāsanāṅkām, prajāś ciraṃ suprajasi prajeśe nanandur ānandajalāvilākṣyaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.30</span>

pātrīkṛtātmā gurusevanena spṛṣṭākṛtiḥ pattrarathendraketoḥ, taṃ putriṇāṃ puṣkarapattranetraḥ putraḥ samāropayad agrasaṃkhyām.

#### <span class="box">18.31</span>

vaṃśasthitiṃ vaṃśakareṇa tena saṃbhāvya bhāvī sa sakhā maghonaḥ, upaspṛṣan sparśanivṛttalaulyas tripuṣkareṣu tridaśatvam āpa.

#### <span class="box">18.32</span>

tasya prabhānirjitapuṣpa-rāgaṃ pauṣyaṃ tithau puṣyam asūta patnī, yasminn apuṣyann udite samagrāṃ puṣṭiṃ janāḥ puṣya iva dvitīye.

#### <span class="box">18.33</span>

mahīṃ mahecchaḥ parikīrya sūnau manīṣiṇe jaiminaye 'rpitātmā, tasmāt sayogād adhigamya yogam ajanmane 'kalpata janmabhīruḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.34</span>

tataḥ paraṃ tatprabhavaḥ prapede dhruvopameyo dhruvasaṃdhir urvīm, yasminn abhūj jyāyasi satyasaṃdhe saṃdhir dhruvaḥ saṃnamatām arīṇām.

#### <span class="box">18.35</span>

sute śiśāv eva sudarśanākhye darśātyayendupriyadarśane saḥ, mṛgāyatākṣo mṛgayāvihārī siṃhād avāpad vipadaṃ nṛsiṃhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.36</span>

svargāminas tasya tam aikamatyād amātyavargaḥ kulatantum ekam, anāthadīnāḥ prakṛtīr avekṣya sāketanāthaṃ vidhivac cakāra.

#### <span class="box">18.37</span>

vavendunā tan nabhasopameyaṃ śāvaikasiṃhena ca kānanena, raghoḥ kulaṃ kuḍmalapaṅkajena toyena cāprauṣhanarendram āsīt.

#### <span class="box">18.38</span>

lokena bhāvī pitur eva tulyaḥ saṃbhāvito mauliparigrahāt saḥ, dṛṣṭo hi vṛṇvan kalabhapramāṇo 'py āśāḥ purovātam avāpya meghaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.39</span>

taṃ rājavīthyām adhihasti yāntam ādhoraṇālambitam agryaveṣam, ṣaḍvarṣadeśiyam api prabhutvāt praikṣanta paurāḥ pitṛgauraveṇa.

#### <span class="box">18.40</span>

kāmaṃ na so 'kalpata paitṛkasya siṃhāsanasya pratipūraṇāya, tejomahimnā punar āvṛtātmā tad vyāpa cāmīkarapiñjareṇa.

#### <span class="box">18.41</span>

tasmād adhaḥ kiṃcid ivāvatīrṇāv asaṃspṛśantau tapanīyapīṭham, sālaktakau bhūpatayaḥ prasiddhair vavandire maulibhir asya pādau.

#### <span class="box">18.42</span>

maṇau mahānīla iti prabhāvād alpapramāṇe 'pi yathā na mithyā, śabdo mahārāja iti pratītas tathaiva tasmin yuyuje 'rbhake 'pi.

#### <span class="box">18.43</span>

paryantasaṃcāritacāmarasya kapolalolobhayakākapakṣat, tasyānanād uccarito vivādaś cakshāla velāsv api nārṇavānām.

#### <span class="box">18.44</span>

nirvṛttajāmbūnadapaṭṭaśobhe nyastaṃ lalāṭe tilakaṃ dadhānaḥ, tenaiva śūnyāny arisundarīṇāṃ mukhāni sa smeramukhaś cakāra.

#### <span class="box">18.45</span>

śirīṣapuṣpādhikasaukumāryaḥ khedaṃ sa yāyād api śrutavṛddhayogāt, nitāntagurvīm api cānubhāvād dhuraṃ dharitryā bibharāṃ babhūva.

#### <span class="box">18.46</span>

nyastākṣarām akṣarabhūmikāyāṃ kārtsnyena gṛhṇāti lipiṃ na yāvat, sarvāṇi tāvac chrutavṛddhayogāt phalāny upāyuṅkta sa daṇḍanīteḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.47</span>

urasy aparyāptabhāgā prauḍhībhaviṣyantam udīkṣamāṇā, saṃjātalajjeva tam ātapatracchāyāchalenopajugūha lakṣmīḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.48</span>

anaśnuvānena yugopamānam abaddhamaurvīkiṇalāñchanena, aspṛṣṭakhaḍgatsaruṇāpi cāsīd rakṣāvatī tasya bhujena bhūmiḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.49</span>

na kevalaṃ gacchati tasya kāle yayuḥ śarīrāvayavā vivṛddhim, vaṃśyā guṇāḥ khalv api lokakāntāḥ prārambhasūkṣmāḥ prathimānam āpuḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.50</span>

sa pūrvajanmāntaradṛṣṭapārāḥ smarann ivākleśakaro gurūṇām, tisras trivargādhigamasya mūlaṃ jagrāha vidyāḥ prakṛtīś ca pitryāḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.51</span>

vyūhya sthitaḥ kiṃcid ivottarārdham unnaddhacūḍo 'ñcitasvyajānuḥ, ākarṇam ākṛṣṭasabānadhanvā vyarocat' āste sa vinīyamānaḥ.

#### <span class="box">18.52</span>

atha madhu vanitāṃ netranirveśanīyaṃ manasijatarupuṣpam rāgabandhapravālam, akṛtakavidhi sarvāṅgīṇam ākalpajātaṃ vilasitapadam ādyaṃ yauvanaṃ sa prapede.

#### <span class="box">18.53</span>

pratikṛtiracanābhayo dūtisaṃdarśitābhyaḥ samadhikatararūpāḥ śuddhasaṃtānakāmaiḥ, adhivividur amātyair āhṛtās tasya yūnaḥ prathamaparigṛhīte śrībhuvau rājakanyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.1</span>

agnivarṇam abhiṣicya rāghavaḥ sve pade tanayam agnitejasam, śiśriye śrutavatām apaścimaḥ paścime vayasi naimiṣaṃ vaśī.

#### <span class="box">19.2</span>

tatra tīrthasalilena dīrghikās talpam antaritabhūmibhiḥ kuśaiḥ, saudhavāsam uṭajena vismṛtaḥ saṃcikāya phalaniḥspṛhas tapaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.3</span>

labdhapālanavidhau na tatsutaḥ khedam āpa guruṇā hi medinī, bhoktum eva bhujanirjitadviṣā na prasādhayitum asya kalpitā.

#### <span class="box">19.4</span>

so 'dhikāram abhikaḥ kulocitaṃ kāścana svayam avartayat samāḥ, taṃ niveśya saciveṣv ataḥ paraṃ strīvidheyanavayauvano 'bhavat.

#### <span class="box">19.5</span>

kāminīsahacarasya kāminas tasya veśmasu mṛdaṅganādiṣu, ṛddhimantam adhikarddhir uttaraḥ pūrvam utsavam apohad utsavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.6</span>

indriyārthapariśūnyam akṣarmaḥ soḍhum ekam api sa kṣaṇātaram, antare ca viharan divāniśaṃ na vyapaikṣata samutsukāḥ prajāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.7</span>

gauravād yad api jātu mantriṇāṃ darśanaṃ prakṛtikāṅkṣitaṃ dadau, tad gavākṣavivarāvalambinā kevalena caraṇena kalpitam.

#### <span class="box">19.8</span>

taṃ kṛtapraṇatayo 'nujīvinaḥ komalātmanakharāgarūṣitam, bhejire navadivākarātapaspṛṣṭapaṅkajatulādhirohaṇam.

#### <span class="box">19.9</span>

yuvanonnatavilāsinīstanakṣobhalolakamalāś ca dīrghikāḥ, gūḍhamohanagṛhās tadambubhiḥ sa vyagāhata vigāḍhamanmathaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.10</span>

tatra sekahṛtalocanāñjanair dhautarāgaparipāṭalādharaiḥ, aṅganās tam adhikaṃ vyalobhayann arpitaprakṛtikāntibhir mukhaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.11</span>

ghrāṇakāntamadhugandhakarṣiṇīḥ pānabhūmiracanāḥ priyāsakhaḥ, abhyapadyata sa vāsitāsakhaḥ puṣpitāḥ kamalinīr iva dvipaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.12</span>

sātirekamadakāraṇaṃ rahas tena dattam abhileṣur aṅganāḥ, tābhir apy upahṛtaṃ mukhāsavaṃ so 'pibad bakulatulyadohadaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.13</span>

aṅkam aṅkaparivartanocite tasya ninyatur aśūnyatām ubhe, vallakī ca hṛdayaṃgamasvanā valguvāg api ca vāmalocanā.

#### <span class="box">19.14</span>

sa svayaṃ prahatapuṣkaraḥ kṛtī lolamālyavalayo haran manaḥ, nartakīr abhinayātilaṅghinīḥ pārśvavartiṣu guruṣv alajjavat.

#### <span class="box">19.15</span>

cāru nṛtyavigame ca tanmukhaṃ svedabhinnatilakaṃ pariśramāt, premadattavadanāniaḥ manaḥ so 'nvajīvad amarālakeśvarau.

#### <span class="box">19.16</span>

tasya sāvaraṇadṛṣṭasaṃdhayaḥ kāmyavastuṣu naveṣu saṅginaḥ, vallabhābhir upasṛtya cakrire sāmibhuktaviṣayāḥ samāgamāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.17</span>

aṅgulīkisalayāgratarjanaṃ bhrūvibhaṅgakuṭilaṃ ca vīkṣitam, mekhalābhir asakṛc ca bandhanaṃ vañcayan praṇayinīr avāpa saḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.18</span>

tena dūtividitaṃ niṣeduṣā pṛṣṭhataḥ suratavārarātriṣu, śuśruve priyajanasya kātaraṃ vipralambhapariśaṅkino vacaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.19</span>

laulyam etya gṛhiṇīparigrahān nartakīṣv asulabhāsu tadvapuḥ, vartate sma sa kathaṃcid ālikhann aṅgulīkṣaraṇasannavartikaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.20</span>

premagarvitavipakṣamatsarād āyatāc ca madanān mahīkṣitam, ninyur utsavavidhicchalena taṃ devya ujjitaruṣaḥ kṛtārthatām.

#### <span class="box">19.21</span>

prātar etya paribhogaśobhinā darśanena kṛtakhaṇḍanavyathāḥ, prāñjaliḥ praṇayinīḥ prasādayan so 'dunot praṇayamantharaḥ punaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.22</span>

svapnakīrtitavipakṣam aṅganāḥ darśanena kṛtakhaṇḍanavyathāḥ, pracchadāntagalitāśrubindubhiḥ krodhabhinnavalayair vivartanaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.23</span>

kḷptapuṣpaśayanāṃl latāgṛhān etya dūtikṛtamārgadarśanaḥ, anvabhūt parijanāṅganārataṃ so 'varodhabhayavepathūttaram.

#### <span class="box">19.24</span>

nāma vallabhajanasya te mayā prāpya bhāgyam api tasya kāṅkṣyate, lolupaṃ bata mano mameti taṃ gotraviskhalitam ūcur aṅganāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.25</span>

cūrṇababhru lulitasragākulaṃ chinnamekhalam alaktakāṅkitam, utthitasya śayanaṃ vilāsinas tasya vibhramartatāny apāvṛṇot.
