#### <span class="box">19.26</span>

sa svayaṃ caraṇarāgam ādadhe yoṣitaṃ na ca tathā samāhitaḥ, lobhyamānanayanaḥ ślathāṃśukair mekhalāguṇapadair nitambibhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.27</span>

cumbane viparivartitādharaṃ hastarodhi raśanāvighaṭṭane, vighniteccham api tasya sarvato manmathendhanam abhūd vadhūratam.

#### <span class="box">19.28</span>

darpaṇeṣu paribhogadarśinīr narmapūrvam anupṛṣṭhasaṃsthitaḥ, chāyayā smitamanojñayā vadhūr hrīnimīlitamukhīś cakāra saḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.29</span>

kaṇṭhasaktamṛdubāhubandhanaṃ nyastapādatalam agrapādayoḥ, prārthayanta śayanotthitaṃ priyās taṃ niśātyayavisargacumbanam.

#### <span class="box">19.30</span>

prekṣya darpaṇatalstham ātmano rājaveṣam atiśakraśobhinam, pipriye sa na tathā yathā yuvā vyaktalakṣma paribhogamaṇḍanam.

#### <span class="box">19.31</span>

mitrakṛtyam apadiśya pārśvataḥ prasthitaṃ tam anavasthitaṃ priyāḥ, vidma he śaṭha palāyanacchalāny añjaseti rurudhuḥ kacagrahaiḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.32</span>

tasya nirdayaratiśramālasāḥ kaṇṭhasūtram apadiśyayoṣitaḥ, adhyaśerata bṛhad (?) bhujāntaraṃ pīvarastanaviluptacandanam.

#### <span class="box">19.33</span>

saṃgamāya niśi gūḍhacāriṇaṃ cāradūtikathitaṃ puro gatāḥ, vañcayiṣyasi kutas tamovṛtaḥ kāmuketi cakṛṣus tam aṅganāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.34</span>

yoṣitām uḍupater ivāciṣāṃ sparśanirvṛtim asāv anāpnuvan, āruroha kumudākaropamāṃ rātrijāgaraparo divāśayaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.35</span>

veṇunā daśanapīḍitādharā vīṇayā nakhapadāṅkitoravaḥ, śilapakārya ubhayena vejitās taṃ vijihmanayanā vyalobhayan.

#### <span class="box">19.36</span>

aṅgasattvavacanāśrayaṃ mithaḥ strīṣu nṛtyam upadhāya darśayan, sa prayoganipuṇaiḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ saṃjagharṣa saha mitrasaṃnidhau.

#### <span class="box">19.37</span>

aṃsalambikuṭajārjunasrajas tasya nīparajasāṅgarāgiṇaḥ, prāvṛṣi pramadabarhiṇeṣv abhūt kṛtimādriṣu vihāravibhramaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.38</span>

vigrahāc ca śayane parāṅmukhīr nānunetum abalāḥ sa tatvare, ācakāṅkṣa ghanaśabdaviklavās tā vivṛtya viśatīr bhujāntaram.
#### <span class="box">19.39</span>

kārttikīṣu savitānaharmyabhāg yāminīṣu lalitāṅganāsakhaḥ, anvabhuṅkta surataśramāpahāṃ meghamuktaviśadāṃ sa candrikām.

#### <span class="box">19.40</span>

saikataṃ ca sarayūṃ vivṛṇvatīṃ śroṇibimbam iva haṃsamekhalam, svapriyāvilasitānukāriṇīṃ saudhajālvivarair vyalokayat.

#### <span class="box">19.41</span>

marmarair agurudhūpagandhibhir vyaktahemarśanais tam ekataḥ, jahrur āgrathanamokṣalolupaṃ haimanair nivsanaiḥ sumadhyamāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.42</span>

arpitastimitadīpadṛṣṭayo garbhaveśmasu nivātakukṣiṣu, tasya sarvasuratāntarakṣamāḥ sākṣitāṃ śiśirarātrayo yayuḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.43</span>

dakṣiṇena pavanena saṃbhṛtaṃ prekṣya cūtakusumaṃ sapallavam, anvanaiṣur avadhūtavigrahās taṃ durutsahaviyogam aṅganāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.44</span>

tāḥ svam aṅkam adhiropya dolayā preṅkhayan parijanāpaviddhayā, muktarajju nibiḍaṃ bhayacchalāt kaṇṭhabandhanam avāpa bāhubhiḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.45</span>

taṃ payodharaniṣaktacandanair mauktikagrathitacārubhūṣaṇaiḥ, grīṣmaveṣavidhibhiḥ siṣevire śroṇilambimaṇimekhalāḥ priyāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.46</span>

yat sa bhagnasahakāram āsavaṃ raktapāṭalasamāgamaṃ papau, tena tasya madhunirgamāt kṛśaś cittayonir abhavat punarnavaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.47</span>

evam indriyasukhāni nirviśann anyakāryavimukhaḥ sa pārthivaḥ, ātmalakṣaṇaniveditān ṛtūn atyavāhayad anaṅgavāhitaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.48</span>

taṃ pramattam api na prabhāvataḥ śekur ākramitum anyapārthivāḥ, āmayas tu ratirāgasaṃbhavo dakṣaśāpa iva candram akṣiṇot.

#### <span class="box">19.49</span>

dṛṣṭadoṣam api tan na so 'tyajat saṅgavastu bhiṣajām anāśravaḥ, svādubhis tu viṣayair hṛtas tato duḥkham indriyagaṇo nivāryate.

#### <span class="box">19.50</span>

tasya pāṇḍuvadanālpabhūṣaṇā sāvalambagamanā mṛdusvanā, yakṣmaṇāpi parihānir āyayau kāmayānasamavasthayā tulām.

#### <span class="box">19.51</span>

vyoma paścimakalāsthitendu vā paṅkaśeṣam iva gharmapalvalam, rājñi tatkulam abhūt kṣayāture vāmanārcir iva dīpabhājanam.

#### <span class="box">19.52</span>

bāḍham eṣu divaseṣu karma sādhayati putrajanmane, ity adarśitarujo 'sya mantriṇaḥ śaśvad ūcur aghaśaṅkinīḥ prajāḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.53</span>

sa tv anekavanitāsakho 'pi san pāvanīm anavalokya saṃtatim, vaidyayatnaparibhāvinaṃ gadaṃ na pradīpa iva vāyum atyagāt.

#### <span class="box">19.54</span>

taṃ gṛhopavana eva saṃgatāḥ paścimakratuvidā purodhasā, rogaśāntim apadiśya mantriṇaḥ saṃbhṛte śikhini gūḍham ādadhuḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.55</span>

taiḥ kṛtaprakṛtimukhyasaṃgrahair āśu tasya sahadharmacāriṇī, sādhu dṛṣṭaśubhagarbhalakṣaṇā pratyapadyata narādhipaśriyam.

#### <span class="box">19.56</span>

tasyās tathāvidhanarendravipattiśokād uṣṇair vilocanajalaiḥ prathamābhitaptaḥ, nirvāpitaḥ kanakakumbhamukhojjhitena vaṃśābhiṣekavidhinā śiśireṇa garbhaḥ.

#### <span class="box">19.57</span>

taṃ bhāvāya prasavasamayākāṅkṣiṇīnāṃ prajānām antargūḍhaṃ kṣitir iva babhau bījamuṣṭiṃ dadhānā, maulaiḥ sārdhaṃ sthavirasacivair hemasiṃhāsanasthā rājñī rājyaṃ vidhivad aśiṣad bhartur avyāhatājñā.
